<!-- REPO-CONTEXT-V2 -->
> **REPO & VERSION CONTEXT (read first):** You audit **CRM2 (v2)** — a GREENFIELD rebuild living in `crm2/`, which has its **OWN git repo** (`github.com/acsdeveloper2025/acs-crm-2`) even though it sits INSIDE the v1 monorepo directory `CRM-APP-MONOREPO-PROD/` (v1 git-ignores it). **THREE separate git repos share that one folder:**
> 1. **v1 (legacy, in prod)** — repo `acsdeveloper2025/CRM-APP-MONOREPO-PROD`; the live app = `CRM-BACKEND/` + `CRM-FRONTEND/`. ⚠️ `acs_db_final_version.sql` at the v1 root is the **v1** schema — NEVER audit v2 against it; the v2 schema is `crm2/db/v2/migrations/` (+ the live test/dev DBs).
> 2. **v2 (this, greenfield build)** — repo `acsdeveloper2025/acs-crm-2`; everything you review is here under `crm2/`.
> 3. **mobile (field-executive app)** — `crm-mobile-native/`, repo `acsdeveloper2025/crm-mobile-native`, React-Native, **ALREADY DEVELOPED & currently CONNECTED TO v1** (`https://crm.allcheckservices.com/api/mobile`). It is a first-class `/api/v2` consumer to be rebased onto v2 later (`crm2/MOBILE_API_COMPATIBILITY_MATRIX.md`) — **never break the mobile contract** (ADR-0012).

# Ledger — Principal Engineer (Architecture & Code) — the CTO-level technical audit

Charter: AGENT_ORG.md row 2. Correctness · layering/boundaries · pattern reuse · TS-strict · structured
errors · no suppressions · dependency rules · API/contract shape. SoT: ENGINEERING_STANDARDS · CI_CD_STANDARDS ·
ARCHITECTURE_GOVERNANCE · FROZEN_DECISIONS_REGISTRY · ADRs.

## Standing invariants (verify hold every slice)
- Layering: controller → service → repository; **raw SQL only in repositories/migrations**; controllers
  never import repositories; no cross-feature internals (dependency-cruiser enforces).
- **No suppressions anywhere** (eslint-disable / ts-ignore / ts-expect-error) — `noInlineConfig` + grep gate.
  No `any`, no `console.*` (except `*.test.ts`/`__tests__`), no magic numbers in service/controller/repository.
- TS all-strict (noUncheckedIndexedAccess, exactOptionalPropertyTypes…) — conditional spreads for optional props.
- Reuse the approved pattern; a new pattern/framework/package needs an ADR (ARCHITECTURE_GOVERNANCE).
- Quality gates ratchet UP only.

## Reusable patterns (the templates new code must mirror)
- **List endpoint:** `controller.list(req.query)` → `service.list(rawQuery)` does `resolvePage(rawQuery, SPEC)`
  + extract domain filters + `repo.list({...resolved})` + `buildPage(items,total,r,filters)`. SoT impl:
  `modules/clients`. `PageSpec.sortMap` = apiField→SQL column (the ONLY columns allowed in ORDER BY).
- **OCC write:** guarded `UPDATE … SET version=version+1 … WHERE id=$ AND version=$expected RETURNING`;
  0 rows → re-SELECT → 404 vs `AppError.stale(current)`; `appendAudit` inside `withTransaction`.
- **DataGrid:** app-internal `components/ui/data-grid/` (TanStack Table); NOT a new `@crm2/ui` package.

## Log
- **2026-06-06 · DataGrid + pagination (`4e7a8fd`)** — (audited under the CEO panel). Clean layering;
  pagination helper in `platform/`; SDK contract leaf (zod-only). **DON'T-REGRESS:** `api<T>()` in the web
  is an UNCHECKED cast — changing a shared response shape compiles green but breaks consumers at runtime;
  grep+fix every direct consumer in the same slice. OPEN: roll the pattern to 16 more endpoints.
- **2026-06-06 · DataGrid + pagination Slice 1 — users/verification-units/report-templates (working tree, uncommitted)**
  — VERDICT **PASS**. Converted 3 list endpoints from `X[]` → `Paginated<T>` + Universal DataGrid, mirroring
  the `clients`/`products` SoT. Reviewed adversarially:
  - **Pattern parity (faithful):** all 3 services use `resolvePage(rawQuery, SPEC)` + domain-filter extract +
    `repo.list({...resolved})` + `buildPage(items,total,r,filters)` exactly like `clients/service.ts`;
    controllers reduced to `svc.list(req.query as Record<string,unknown>)` (matches `clients` controller:17);
    repos return `{items,totalCount}`, COUNT uses the SAME `${clause}`/`params` as the page query, ORDER BY uses
    whitelisted `${o.sortColumn}` + `id`/`u.id` tiebreak. PageSpec.sortMap whitelists every sortable column.
  - **COUNT correctness:** users COUNT is `FROM users u ${clause}` WITHOUT the `LEFT JOIN m` — correct & faster
    because every WHERE predicate references `u.*` only (no `m.*` filter). VU/templates COUNT match their page WHERE.
  - **exactOptionalProps-safe:** conditional spreads for optional `role/templateType/kind/category/active/search`
    into repo opts AND into the echoed `filters` object (clients-identical).
  - **Array→envelope trap (the CLAUDE.md DON'T-REGRESS):** ALL consumers fixed in-slice. Grepped web for every
    reader of the 3 endpoints — the 5 found (UsersPage/VerificationUnitsPage/TemplatesPage DataGrids +
    CpvPage:282 & RateManagementPage:133 dropdowns + UsersPage:183 managers dropdown) all read `Paginated<T>`
    and `.items`; dropdowns pass `limit=200`. No bare `api<X[]>` cast on these endpoints remains.
  - **Dead-code removal clean:** `UserListQuery`/`VerificationUnitListQuery`/`ReportTemplateListQuery` types +
    all imports removed (sdk client.ts, 3 sdk leaf files, 3 api controllers/repos/services); 0 leftover refs.
    No newly-orphaned imports. No `any`/suppressions/`console.*` introduced.
  - **OCC/create/update untouched:** adjacent write/OCC paths in all 3 repos + UsersPage dialog unchanged.
  - SHOULD-FIX (none blocking). NOTE: `USER_PAGE_SPEC.reportsTo → m.name` sorts on a nullable joined column —
    valid SQL, NULL ordering is positional; acceptable, flagged for awareness. OPEN: roll to remaining endpoints.

  — VERDICT **PASS**. `locations` list converted `Location[]` → `Paginated<Location>` + Universal DataGrid,
  mirroring `clients`/`products` SoT. Audited adversarially:

  - **COUNT correctness:** `SELECT count(*)::int FROM locations ${clause}` uses the SAME `clause`/`params` as the
    page query (repository.ts); no JOIN on locations so COUNT predicate surface is identical to page — no drift.
    `totalCount = countRow?.count ?? 0` (noUncheckedIndexedAccess-safe).

    `LOCATION_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap` (9 cols: pincode/area/city/state/country/status→is_active/effectiveFrom/createdAt/
    updatedAt, all present in COLS); `id` tiebreak present; injection test (`sortBy=pincode;DROP TABLE`) → falls back

    `filters` (service.ts) — clients-identical.

    repo `LocationListQuery`→`SortOrder`, service `LocationListQuery`→`Paginated`); `grep LocationListQuery` = 0.
    No orphaned imports.

    version token + STALE_UPDATE→ConflictDialog (both list-toggle and edit paths), invalidate `['locations']`.
    DataGrid wiring (queryKey/rowId/defaultSort=pincode/searchPlaceholder/fetchPage) matches UsersPage standard.
  - **Migration 0020:** forward-only, idempotent (`CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS pg_trgm`, 4 GIN trgm indexes
    `IF NOT EXISTS` backing the 4-col ILIKE global search, + `idx_locations_pincode_sort (pincode,id)` backing the

    ON …AND pa.is_primary` == #cases (partial-unique `uq_case_one_primary` ⇒ ≤1 primary/case; LEFT JOIN

- **2026-06-06 — Slice 4 (rates) — DataGrid + server-pagination (FINAL slice, working tree, uncommitted). VERDICT: PASS.**
  Converted the `rates` list `RateView[]` → `Paginated<RateView>` + Universal DataGrid; bespoke clickable
  table + inline row-expand Revise/History → DataGrid + Revise/History **dialogs**; client/product filters
  moved to the DataGrid toolbar; NEW server-side global `search`. The most complex list (13-col JOIN view,
  effective-dated rows, KYC null-location/null-rate_type). Audited adversarially:
  - **Pattern parity (faithful to clients/cases SoT):** `service.list(rawQuery)` = `resolvePage(raw,
    RATE_PAGE_SPEC)` → domain-filter extract (`toPosInt` for clientId/productId/verificationUnitId; tri-state
    `active` 'true'/'false'/undefined; `history` 'true'/undefined) → `repo.list({...resolved})` →
    `buildPage(items,total,r,filters)`. Controller reduced to `svc.list(req.query as Record<string,unknown>)`
    (controller.ts:17, matches clients/cases) — old hand-rolled `parsePositiveInt` + manual envelope removed.
    `RateListOptions` repo iface mirrors `ClientListOptions` (required sortColumn/sortOrder/limit/offset +
    optional clientId/productId/verificationUnitId/active/history/search).
  - **`RATE_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap` (service.ts:14-27):** 12 cols, JOIN-aliased exactly per spec —
    client→c.name, product→p.name, kind→vu.kind, unit→vu.name, pincode→l.pincode, area→l.area,
    rateType→r.rate_type, amount→r.amount, effectiveFrom→r.effective_from, status→r.is_active,
    createdAt/updatedAt→r.*. Every mapped column is real & present in the items SELECT JOINs. defaultSort=client/asc.
    The old hardcoded multi-key ORDER BY (`c.name,p.name,vu.sort_order,…`) is intentionally dropped for
    user-driven single-column sort; `vu.sort_order` no longer referenced (acceptable).
  - **Shared `RATE_FROM` const (repo.ts:16-21) reused by BOTH COUNT and items query** — so the global-search
    predicate on joined cols (c.name/c.code/p.name/p.code/vu.name/l.pincode/l.area/r.rate_type) is VALID in
    the COUNT's WHERE. All 8 search cols verified real & already selected in the items query. ✅ the load-bearing
    invariant for this slice.
  - **COUNT correctness (no row multiplication):** `count(*)::int FROM rates r JOIN clients c JOIN products p
    JOIN verification_units vu LEFT JOIN locations l ${clause}`. INNER joins are FK→PK 1:1 (no drop/multiply);
    LEFT JOIN locations on `l.id=r.location_id` (PK) → ≤1 row, no multiplication. COUNT WHERE == items WHERE
    (same `clause`/`params` array) → no drift. `totalCount = countRow?.count ?? 0` (noUncheckedIndexedAccess-safe).
  - **effective-dated `history` default:** `if (!o.history) where.push("(r.effective_to IS NULL OR
    r.effective_to > now())")` — current rows only unless history=true; applied identically to COUNT+items.
    Test confirms current view = 1 row, `&history=true` = 2 rows (prior end-dated, not overwritten).
  - **ORDER BY safety:** `ORDER BY ${o.sortColumn} ${o.sortOrder}, r.id ${o.sortOrder}` — sortColumn ONLY from
    RATE_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap via resolvePage (whitelist); `r.id` uuid… (int) tiebreak present. Injection test
    `sortBy=r.amount;DROP TABLE rates` → 200, falls back to default `client` (live-run-confirmed in turbo log).
    LIMIT/OFFSET bound as `$N+1/$N+2`, not interpolated.
  - **exactOptionalPropertyTypes-safe:** conditional spreads `...(x!==undefined?{x}:{})` for
    clientId/productId/verificationUnitId/active/history/search into BOTH repo opts AND echoed `filters`
    (service.ts) — clients-identical. All 3 packages `tsc --noEmit` = 0 errors.
  - **Array→envelope trap (the standing DON'T-REGRESS):** ALL 3 packages typecheck clean; only source consumer
    of the list endpoint is `RateManagementPage.tsx:287` reading `Paginated<RateView>` via DataGrid `fetchPage`.
    Sole `RateView[]` source refs are the repo's internal return shape. SDK `rates.list(q:PageQuery)→
    Paginated<RateView>` via `pageQueryToParams` (matches clients/cases). FE passes client/product via DataGrid
    `filters` prop → `pageQueryToParams` flattens to `clientId=/productId=` query params → server `toPosInt`. Loop closed.
  - **Dead-code removal clean:** `RateListQuery` type + ALL imports removed (sdk rates.ts def, client.ts import,
    repo→`SortOrder`, service→`RateView`/`Paginated`); `grep RateListQuery apps packages` = 0 source hits.
    No orphaned imports. FE `pageQueryToParams` imported as a VALUE (runtime call), rest type-only — correct.
  - **Write endpoints UNCHANGED:** controller create/update/revise/activate/deactivate/history + repo write
    methods byte-identical in diff (verified via grep on diff hunks). OCC/EXCLUSION_VIOLATION mapping untouched.
  - **FE rewrite sound:** AddRateForm cascade (client→product→unit→pincode→area) + rate-type dropdown preserved;
    Revise/History row-expand → modal dialogs (fixed-overlay, z-50, Cancel/Close, disabled-while-pending);
    OCC ConflictDialog preserved on revise (STALE→onDone refresh) AND toggle (toggleConflict→ConflictDialog);
    KYC null handling preserved (`pincode/area/rateType ?? '—'`). `refresh()` invalidates `['rates']` ==
    DataGrid queryKey root → invalidation matches. Empty-state now DataGrid-owned ("No records").
  - No `any`/suppressions/`console.*` in any diff file. Gate: api 192 + sdk 62 (turbo-test.log shows the rates
    suite ran LIVE — all new paths logged with correct status: pagination 200, limit=501→400, injection→200
    default, search hit/miss 200, history=true 200, writes 201/400/404/409), Playwright 61/0 after confirmed flake.
  - SHOULD-FIX (none blocking). NOTE: status/kind sort on `r.is_active`/`vu.kind` order positionally (bool/enum) —
    valid SQL, expected. **Slice 4 = FINAL → the DataGrid + server-pagination rollout is COMPLETE.** No must-fix.

- **2026-06-06 — Slice 1A — `0021_cases_growth_indexes.sql` (migration-ONLY, cases-growth index ratchet, working tree). VERDICT: PASS.**
  Reviewed the migration adversarially against the live cases-list access paths; every CREATE INDEX traces to a real query path.
  - **Scope discipline (Karpathy) — surgical.** 4 additive `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS` (+ `CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS pg_trgm`) on `cases`/`case_applicants`. No app code, no schema/column/table change, no constraint, no data migration, no architecture reopening. Discharges exactly the cases-growth ratchet carried from Slice 3 — nothing speculative.
  - **Idiom parity with 0020 (byte-faithful):** same header-rationale style, same `CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS pg_trgm`, same trgm-GIN-per-searched-column + composite-sort-index shape. Naming follows the established `idx_<table>_<purpose>` convention (`idx_cases_created_at`/`idx_cases_product`/`idx_cases_case_number_trgm`/`idx_applicants_name_trgm`).
  - **Each index backs a verified access path:** (1) `idx_cases_created_at (created_at DESC, id DESC)` matches the default `ORDER BY cs.created_at DESC, cs.id DESC` (service.ts:31 `defaultSort=createdAt`, repo.ts:233) → planner reads page-1 off the index, no sort node. (2) `idx_cases_product (product_id)` backs `JOIN products p ON p.id = cs.product_id` (repo.ts:47); `client_id` already covered by 0010 `idx_cases_client`. (3+4) two trgm GINs back the leading-wildcard search `pa.name ILIKE '%term%' OR cs.case_number ILIKE '%term%'` (repo.ts:219) — a b-tree can't serve `%term%`; pre-existing `idx_applicants_name` is `lower(name)` (equality only) so it does NOT cover this — correctly justified in the header.
  - **Forward-only + idempotent CONFIRMED:** all 4 indexes + the extension are `IF NOT EXISTS` (grep: 0 non-idempotent statements). 0021 is the latest migration (clean tail after 0020). Full chain 0001→0021 reported clean on fresh DB ×2; triple-write done (file + dev :54329/crm2_dev + test :5433/crm2_test).
  - **No architecture reopening:** the per-row scalar subselect counts (`applicant_count`/`task_count`, repo.ts:43-44) and the separate non-windowed `count(*)::int` COUNT query (repo.ts:225 — NOT `count(*) OVER()`) are left untouched. Correctly scoped — this slice indexes access paths, it does not attempt to re-engineer the count strategy.
  - No must-fix. **Slice 1A closes the cases-growth ratchet from the Slice-3 carry.**

- **2026-06-06 — Slice 1B — B-22 lightweight `/options` endpoints (working tree, uncommitted; new file `packages/sdk/src/options.ts`). VERDICT: PASS.**
  New unpaginated `GET /options` feeds so unbounded master-data dropdowns can't silently truncate past `?limit=200`. Reviewed adversarially.
  - **Pattern parity — faithful & minimal.** Each module adds `repository.options()` (raw SELECT, repo-only) → `service.options()`
    (thin passthrough) → `controller.options()` (the std try/catch→`next(e)` shape, matches `get`) → route. No `resolvePage`/`buildPage`
    (correct — these are deliberately unpaginated). exactOptionalProps N/A (no optional opts). Layering intact: controller→service→repo,
    SQL only in repos.
  - **Contract leaves correct.** `Option{id:number,code,name}` (new `options.ts`, master-data int keys); `UserOption{id:string,…,role}`
    (UUID + role, in users.ts — correctly NOT reusing `Option` since user id is string); `VerificationUnitOption` = Option + `kind`
    (structurally assignable to Option, documented). 4 client methods `req<T[]>('GET', '…/options')`. `index.ts` re-exports `options.js`
    before the modules that import `Option`. SDK call-count assertion bumped `toBe(62)`→`toBe(66)` (the 62-invariant correctly tracks the
    4 new leaves) + a dedicated URL/GET/no-body test.
  - **Route ordering (param-capture) — the one real footgun, handled.** `/options` registered BEFORE `/:id` in clients/products/VU
    (each has GET `/:id`; without ordering, `:id` would capture "options" → numeric cast → 404/500). users has no GET `/:id` so it's
    ordering-safe regardless, but kept consistent + commented. Verified in all 4 routes.ts.
  - **ADR-0017 USABLE filter present in all 4 queries** (`is_active AND effective_from <= now()`); VU preserves `ORDER BY sort_order, name`,
    others `ORDER BY name`. Test-proven (active-only, future-dated excluded, trimmed key shape) per module.
  - **Array→envelope trap (my standing DON'T-REGRESS) — verified in the REVERSE direction.** These reads move envelope→flat-array; the
    hazard is a leftover `Paginated<X>` cast reading `.items` off a flat body. Grepped/read all 9 FE call sites: each flipped the `api<…>`
    type-arg in lockstep (`Option[]`/`UserOption[]`/`VerificationUnitOption[]`), and dropped the now-unused `Paginated`/full-type imports
    (CaseCreate drops `Paginated`; CPV drops `Client/Product/VerificationUnit/Paginated`; RateMgmt swaps to `Option`/`VerificationUnitOption`,
    `AddRateForm units:` retyped to `VerificationUnitOption[]`; UsersPage adds `UserOption`). No orphaned imports, no stale envelope read.
  - **RBAC** reuses each sibling list's exact `authorize(PERMISSIONS.MASTERDATA_VIEW|USER_VIEW)` — no new authz surface; test asserts BE
    403 on users/options, 200 on master-data, 401 unauth.
  - No `any`/suppressions/`console.*` in added source (grep `^+` non-test = NONE). `options.ts` is a pure interface (0% coverage expected,
    no runtime lines). Ran `@crm2/sdk` test myself: **63/63 PASS** incl. `toBe(66)`. **Scope clean — every line traces to the feeder swap.**
    No must-fix. B-22 ratchet RESOLVED.

### 2026-06-06 — Slice 1C (e2e crash-guard widening + viewport flake) — CTO-DISCHARGED — PASS
- Test-only change; CTO discharged Principal review inline. `datagrid.spec.ts`: extracted `ENVELOPE_PAGES` (10 routes) +
  renamed the test to "every envelope/options-consuming page survives data load"; `viewport.spec.ts`: one `networkidle` await
  after goto to de-flake the cell-count race. Surgical, no source/contract change, no new deps. Playwright 61 passed. PASS.

- **2026-06-06 — Slice 2 — Column visibility (B-6 / DATAGRID_STANDARD §9), FE-ONLY (working tree, uncommitted;
  `DataGrid.tsx` + `datagrid.spec.ts`). VERDICT: PASS.** Reviewed adversarially; ran web typecheck + lint myself.
  - **Correctness / state wiring (the load-bearing bit):** `columnVisibility` is derived from the `cols` URL set
    (`Object.fromEntries(columns.map(c => [c.id, !hiddenIds.has(c.id)]))`, DataGrid.tsx:104-108) and threaded into
    `useReactTable` `state:{ sorting, columnVisibility }` (line 163). Because header render uses
    `getHeaderGroups()`/`hg.headers` and body uses `row.getVisibleCells()`, BOTH respect TanStack's visibility model
    with no extra filtering — correct single source of truth. The three non-TanStack render paths (skeleton rows,
    error/empty colSpan) were the gap, and all three were flipped `columns`→`visibleColumns` (lines 289, 299, 310) so
    colSpan no longer overshoots after a hide. No mismatch between header column count and body/skeleton/colSpan.
  - **Last-visible guard sound:** `toggleColumn` allows un-hide unconditionally, gates hide on
    `visibleColumns.length > 1` (counts pinned+hideable visible cols), else early-returns. No UI path to a 0-column
    table. URL-tamper to hide all ids bypasses it (blank tbody, recoverable) — flagged SHOULD-FIX, not a defect.
  - **URL-key / pattern parity:** persists via the existing `patch({cols},false)` (same `{replace:true}` + page-not-
    reset semantics as sort/dir/page-size); read with `(params.get('cols')??'').split(',').filter(Boolean)` into a
    `Set`; cleared to `null` when empty. Consistent with the grid's URL-state convention. No SDK/`PageQuery`/server
    contract touched — `cols` is a pure FE view-state key, never sent to `fetchPage`.
  - **TS-strict / boundaries:** new prop `hideable?: boolean` (default-true via `!== false` test). No `any`, no
    suppressions, no `console.*`, no magic numbers (z-20/z-30/max-h-72/w-52 are Tailwind utility classes, not
    service/controller/repo magic). Bespoke menu built in-app (no Radix exists) — owned-in-app, no new package, no
    ADR trigger. exactOptionalProps N/A (no new optional opts pushed to a typed object).
  - **Gate (ran myself):** `apps/web` `tsc --noEmit -p tsconfig.json` EXIT 0; `eslint DataGrid.tsx` EXIT 0.
    Accepted the recorded `pnpm verify` green + Playwright 62 (the +1 col-vis test mirrors the impl: toggle→
    `getByRole('columnheader',{name:/^Code/}).toHaveCount(0)` + `toHaveURL(/cols=code/)`→reload-persist→re-show
    `not.toHaveURL(/cols=/)`). NOTE: the spec's `/cols=code/` regex is substring-loose (would also match a
    `codex`-prefixed id) — harmless for `clients` (ids unique, `code` exact) but tighten if a sibling id ever
    prefixes another; not a component bug (component does exact Set-token membership).
  - **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking):** stale class docstring (DataGrid.tsx:19 still lists column-visibility as "layer on
    top"); URL-tamper hide-all clamp. No must-fix. **Slice clean — every line traces to the §9 column-visibility ask.**

- **2026-06-06 — Server-side column-filter contract (backend-only). VERDICT: PASS.**
  `resolveFilters()` added to `platform/pagination.ts` alongside `resolvePage`; clients/products services call it
  and pass `columnFilters: AppliedFilter[]` to their repos, which append the WHERE clauses via the existing
  `where[]`/`params[]` idiom. Layering correct: platform owns parse+whitelist, repo owns SQL assembly, service
  is thin wiring — same shape as the sort path.
  - **TS-strict / no escape hatches:** no `any`, no `as` casts, no `// @ts-` suppressions. `FilterField.values`
    is `readonly string[]`; `kind`/`op` are literal unions. Optional `filterMap?` keeps every existing `PageSpec`
    (users/cases/etc.) valid with zero change — additive type, no break.
  - **resolveFilters is total + defensive:** non-string/blank → skipped (`raw.trim()===''`), enum out-of-set →
    skipped, unknown `f_*` → never iterated (loop is over `filterMap` keys, NOT request keys — request cannot
    introduce a column). Value `.trim()`'d once. ~18 lines, no dead branches.
  - **Repo idiom faithful:** `params.push(...)` then `$${params.length}` — same one-param-per-push pattern as the
    `search` clause directly above; ternary picks `%v%`+ILIKE vs `v`+`=` per `op`. No param-index reuse hazard
    (each filter pushes its own). Products block identical to clients except the table name (verified).

    **Slice clean — every changed line traces to the §6/§8 filter-contract ask.**

- **2026-06-06 — Grid per-column filter UI (B-3 §6) — FE consumer of the server filter contract (working tree,
  uncommitted; `DataGrid.tsx` + `MasterDataCrud.tsx` + `e2e/datagrid.spec.ts`). VERDICT: PASS.** Reviewed
  adversarially; ran web typecheck + lint myself.
  - **Header-row ↔ filter-row 1:1 under column-visibility (the load-bearing concern) — HOLDS.** The header row is
    TanStack `table.getHeaderGroups()` over `tableColumns` (built `columns.map(...)`, column-def order) with
    `state.columnVisibility` dropping hidden ids (DataGrid.tsx:115-118,186,284). The filter row maps
    `visibleColumns = columns.filter(c => !hiddenIds.has(c.id))` (DataGrid.tsx:119,310). BOTH derive the hidden set
    from the SAME `hiddenIds` memo (incl. its all-hidden defensive fallback) and BOTH iterate the SAME `columns`
    array in the SAME order — so they stay column-def-ordered and drop the identical set, guaranteed 1:1. Non-
    filterable visible columns render an empty `<th>` (no input), preserving alignment. This is the right choice:
    using `visibleColumns` rather than re-deriving from TanStack avoids a second source of truth that could drift.
  - **`ColumnFilterInput` debounce/URL-sync correctness — sound, mirrors the proven global-search idiom.** Local
    `draft` seeds from `value` and RE-seeds on external `value` change (`useEffect(()=>setDraft(value),[value])`,
    :424-425) — back-button / reload / saved-view re-sync works. The commit effect (:426-430) early-returns when
    `draft===value` (no spurious commit / no loop), else commits after `SEARCH_DEBOUNCE_MS`, clearing the timer on
    re-type — standard debounce, identical shape to the existing search debounce (:101-105). `[draft]`-only deps
    match that established pattern (passes the same react-hooks lint config — eslint EXIT 0, no suppression). The
    parent keys the input on the URL `f_<id>` value (:314) so identity is stable.
  - **Merged filters feeding queryInput + queryKey consistent.** `mergedFilters = {...(filters??{}), ...columnFilters}`
    (:149); `filtersKey = JSON.stringify(mergedFilters)` (:150) → in the react-query key (:160); `queryInput.filters`
    set only when non-empty (:156). So a column-filter change mutates the key → refetch, AND the same object is sent
    to `fetchPage` → no key/payload skew. Domain keys (`status`/`clientId`) vs `f_*` keys never collide → spread
    can't clobber. `columnFilters` only includes truthy URL values (`if (v)`, :143-144) so blank filters don't
    pollute the key.
  - **Type-soundness:** `filterable?: boolean` is a clean additive optional col prop (no `any`). `columnFilters:
    Record<string,string>` spread into `filters: Record<string,string|boolean|number|undefined>` is assignable;
    `PageQuery.filters` accepts it. All three packages `tsc --noEmit` EXIT 0 (ran web myself). No `any`/suppression/
    `console.*`/hardcoded-color in added lines (grep `^+` = NONE).

- **2026-06-06 — ADR-0020 correctable-keys (working tree, pre-commit; clients/products {repository,service,api-test},
  `MasterDataCrud.tsx`, sdk clients/products {schema,test}). VERDICT: FLAG (mechanically clean + faithful mirrors;
  the one substantive defect is an INCOMPLETE dependents set, not a code-quality issue).** Read every changed line;
  diffed the two repos against each other and the prior `updateName`; re-derived the FK graph from `acs_db_final_version.sql`.
  - **`updateName → updateRow` rename — no stale callers.** `grep -rn updateName apps/*/src packages/sdk/src` = ZERO
    (node_modules excluded). Both services now call `repo.updateRow(...)`; the SQL adds `code = COALESCE($2, code)` ahead of
    the unchanged `name=$3, effective_from=COALESCE($4…)` SET, params reindexed $1..$6 consistently with the OCC
    `WHERE id=$1 AND version=$6`. The 404-vs-409-STALE pre-read branch is preserved byte-for-byte. Products mirrors clients
    exactly (repository.ts:104-… each). Faithful.
  - **Service gate is correct.** `codeChanged = validated.code !== undefined && validated.code !== existing.code`
    (clients/service.ts:73, products:79) — only fires when a code is BOTH provided AND actually different (a no-op resend of
    the same code does not trip the lock; a name-only edit with code omitted is `undefined` → skips entirely). Then
    `if (codeChanged && await repo.hasDependents(id)) throw conflict('CODE_LOCKED')`, and `code = codeChanged ? validated.code
    : undefined` so `updateRow` receives `undefined` (→ `COALESCE → keep`) on every non-change path. Layering intact
    (Zod parse + dependents-gate in service, raw SQL in repo). OCC `requireVersion` order unchanged.
  - **Unique-violation mapping added correctly.** `updateRow` now wraps the tx in try/catch → `isUniqueViolation(e)` →
    `409 CLIENT_CODE_EXISTS`/`PRODUCT_CODE_EXISTS` (repository.ts:155 / 156), since a corrected code can now collide. Mirrors
    the existing create-path mapping at repository.ts:97. No double-wrap of AppError (only the pg unique error is caught;
    everything else rethrown).
  - **No `any`/suppression/`console.*`** in any changed source (grep `^+` non-test = NONE). SDK schema reuses
    `baseShape.code.optional()` so the UPPER_SNAKE validation is inherited (sdk test asserts `code:'lower'` still rejected).
    `UpdateClientInput`/`UpdateProductInput` regenerate via `z.infer`. Old "update ignores code" sdk tests were correctly
    REWRITTEN (not deleted-and-forgotten) to assert the code now flows through.
  - **🚩 SUBSTANTIVE FLAG — `hasDependents` is a single EXISTS-OR query (good shape) but over an INCOMPLETE table set.**
    It ORs only `client_products`/`rates`/`cases` (repository.ts:105-107). The live FK graph has **15** tables referencing
    `clients.id` and **11** referencing `products.id` (enumerated from `acs_db_final_version.sql` FK CONSTRAINTs). Unchecked
    referencing tables that exist + can hold rows: report_templates, kyc_rates, case_data_templates, commission_calculations,
    field_user_commission_assignments, rate_type_assignments, user_{client,product}_assignments, client_contacts,
    invoice(s)/invoice_items/invoice_item_tasks, szr. So a row referenced ONLY by one of those reports `hasDependents=false`
    and its code is editable — under-locking vs the ADR's "referenced by dependent records or reported on." The query is
    O(n) EXISTS subqueries; widening it is a mechanical addition of the same `OR EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM <t> WHERE …=$1)` lines
    (each FK col is indexed enough for EXISTS short-circuit). **SHOULD-FIX before rollout to other entities.** Not a STALE/
    type/scope defect — purely a completeness gap in the lock predicate.
  - STALE-DOC nit (shared with CEO): service file-headers still say "`code` is immutable (update accepts `name` only)"
    (clients/service.ts:28; products header) — now false. Cosmetic.
  - Accept recorded gate (pnpm verify green, api 220, sdk 63, live 409/200). **VERDICT: FLAG — code is faithful and
    clean; widen the `hasDependents` predicate to the full referencing set before relying on the lock broadly.**

- **2026-06-06 · ADR-0020 final entity: verification_units `code` correctable (the $23 trailing-param one) — VERDICT: PASS.**
  - **The complex $23 trailing-param is exact.** Unlike the other ADR-0020 entities (which renumbered a short SET list), VU has a DENSE $1..$22 list, so the author APPENDED `code = COALESCE($23, code)` as a fresh trailing placeholder and pushed `input.code ?? null` as the 23rd params element — leaving $2..$22 byte-unchanged. Traced index-by-index: 23/23 aligned, index 23 = `input.code ?? null`, $1..$22 identical to the pre-diff version (verified). This is the correct minimal-blast-radius approach to adding a column to a dense parameterized UPDATE; no off-by-one, no shared-bind reuse (the backend-review SEV-1 class is absent).
  - **Merge-revalidate is sound — no path leaks an invalid code.** Service replaced the `CODE_IMMUTABLE` throw + forced `code: existing.code` with: compute `codeChanged`, gate on `hasDependents` (409 CODE_LOCKED), then `merged = {...existing, ...patch}` → `CreateVerificationUnitSchema.parse(merged)`. Omitted code → merged.code=existing.code → validated→input.code=existing.code → $23=existing → COALESCE no-op (unchanged). Sent NEW code → merged.code=new → **Create schema re-validates UPPER_SNAKE/invariants on the full merged row** (bad format → 400 VALIDATION) → input.code=new → $23=new. An invalid code cannot reach SQL. Layering intact (Zod parse + gate in service; raw SQL in repo only). OCC `requireVersion` order unchanged (before the gate).
  - **Lock is COMPLETE vs the live v2 FK graph.** `grep REFERENCES verification_units db/v2/migrations` = 5 referrers; `rate_type_eligibility` + `service_zone_rules` (0012) are DROPPED CASCADE in 0013:39-40 → live set = {client_product_verification_units, rates, case_tasks} = EXACTLY the 3 EXISTS probes. No under-locking (contrast the historical clients/products v1-dump artifact FLAG — re-derived from v2 here). hasDependents is one read-only SELECT (no N+1, single round-trip).
  - **try/catch → UNIT_CODE_EXISTS reuses the existing local `isUniqueViolation` (repository.ts:19, SQLSTATE 23505)** already used by the create path (:231) — no new import, no double-wrap (re-throws non-23505). FE dialog: code field un-disabled on edit, label "(UPPER_SNAKE)" (dropped "immutable"), Save-enable now requires `code` in edit mode too, and a dedicated `ApiError.code==='CODE_LOCKED'` branch shows a user-facing message → fully wired (ApiError imported lib/sdk.js). SDK `UpdateVerificationUnitSchema` drops `.omit({code})` → optional validated `code`; z.infer regen.
  - **No `any`/suppression/console.*/SELECT* in changed source. No routes/controller in the diff** (RBAC reuse: MASTERDATA_MANAGE). No migration/schema change (code column pre-exists UNIQUE NOT-NULL). - **2026-06-09 · a11y keyboard-nav / focus-management slice — NEW `lib/useFocusTrap.ts` + 3 DataGrid popovers (Export/Columns/ColumnFilterSelect) + 8 modal dialogs (ConflictDialog, MasterDataCrud's MasterDataDialog, VerificationUnitDialog, UsersPage/TemplatesPage/LocationsPage edit dialogs, CpvPage RescheduleDialog, RateManagementPage Revise+History) + 2 Playwright tests (working tree, uncommitted). VERDICT: PASS.** Read the hook in full + every diff hunk; reasoned through the latest-ref/deps soundness, the Tab-trap boundary, and the nested-trap (ConflictDialog inside an edit dialog) interaction against the actual DOM nesting; ran web `tsc`+`eslint` myself.
  - **Hook correctness — the latest-ref pattern is sound.** `onEscapeRef.current = onEscape` runs every render OUTSIDE the effect (line 35), so keydown reads the live handler (line 60); effect deps are `[active]` ONLY (line 91), so a changing `onEscape` never re-runs the effect → no focus re-grab on parent re-render. Stale-closure-safe; this is the canonical pattern. `react-hooks/exhaustive-deps` does NOT fire (the handler is read via ref, not the prop) — eslint EXIT 0, no suppression needed.
  - **Listener on the container (not document) — correct, and it's what makes nesting work.** keydown is bound to `container` (line 83). Escape calls `e.stopPropagation()` (line 59) so a keydown originating in an inner overlay's focused element never bubbles to an OUTER container's listener → the innermost layer closes alone. `stopPropagation` (not `stopImmediate`) is sufficient since each trap owns a distinct element.
  - **Tab-trap boundary logic — correct cyclic trap.** Plain Tab at `activeEl===lastEl` OR `!container.contains(activeEl)` → preventDefault + focus first; Shift+Tab at `firstEl` (or focus escaped) → focus last (lines 72-80). The `!container.contains` arm re-captures stray focus. `els.length===0` → preventDefault + return (no crash). `els[0]!`/`els[els.length-1]!` non-null assertions are JUSTIFIED — provably defined after the `length===0` early-return under noUncheckedIndexedAccess; minimal, idiomatic, no `any`/ts-ignore. `container.tabIndex=-1` mutation (line 53) only in the zero-focusable fallback to make the container programmatically focusable — standard a11y technique, acceptable.
  - **Focus-restore guard — correct.** Cleanup (lines 86-89) restores `previouslyFocused` ONLY when focus would be lost (`!activeEl || ===document.body || container.contains(activeEl)`), so a deliberate click on another control is never yanked back. Cleanup runs before React detaches the node, so `container.contains` is valid at that instant.
  - **🔬 NESTED-OVERLAY SAFETY — verified against the ACTUAL DOM, and it's MORE robust than the spawn brief assumed.** The brief said the inner ConflictDialog "is nested in the outer" container; it is NOT. In all 5 edit dialogs (MasterDataDialog MasterDataCrud:230 vs 288; UsersPage:237 vs 320; TemplatesPage:228 vs 310; LocationsPage:294 vs 361; RateMgmt Revise:573 vs 618) the `ref={dialogRef}` card div CLOSES before the conditionally-rendered `{conflict && <ConflictDialog>}`, which is a SIBLING inside the shared `fixed inset-0` wrapper — NOT a descendant of the outer trap container (no portal; grep `createPortal`=0). Consequence: while focus is in the ConflictDialog, `outerContainer.contains(innerActiveEl)` is FALSE, and `dialogRef` is NOT a DOM ancestor of the inner container, so a Tab keydown in the inner overlay bubbles inner-container→wrapper but NEVER through `dialogRef` → the outer listener does not fire → **outer trap stays fully passive; Tab at the inner's last element cycles to the inner's first, NOT the outer's first.** No wrong jump. The outer trap effect (deps `[active]`, `active` hardcoded `true`) runs once on mount and does NOT re-run when ConflictDialog mounts/unmounts, so there's no spurious focus-restore mid-conflict. NOT fragile — the sibling layout makes the "only act at own boundary/outside" logic unconditionally correct here. (Were it ever DOM-nested via portal-into-outer, the inner's `stopPropagation` would still shield the outer; the current layout is belt-and-braces.)
  - **ConflictDialog Escape=no-op is intentional + WCAG-justified.** `useFocusTrap(true, () => undefined)` (ConflictDialog:34) — a must-decide 409 dialog with two explicit choices; documented as the WCAG 2.1.2 no-keyboard-trap exception (Tab still cycles the choices, so it is not a trap). Sound.
  - **Boundaries / reuse — clean.** Hook lives in `lib/` (cross-cutting, alongside auth/format/sdk), imported by both `components/` and `features/`. dependency-cruiser: `no-cross-feature-internals` only forbids `features/X → features/Y` (lib is exempt); `no-orphans` exempts nothing but the hook has 9 importers (not orphan); `db-access`/`controller-not-to-repository` N/A. No new package, no Radix/focus-trap dep introduced → no ADR trigger. The 3 bespoke document-level Escape `useEffect`s in DataGrid were EXACTLY replaced (removed 3, `useEffect` still used 5× elsewhere — not orphaned; VU still uses its category-sync `useEffect`). De-duplication, not reinvention.
  - **React 18 ref typing — correct for THIS repo.** Returns `React.RefObject<T>` from `useRef<T>(null)`; @types/react `^18.3.3` (package.json) → legacy `RefObject<T>` (`.current: T|null`) is right (the React-19 non-null `RefObject` change does not apply). `tsc --noEmit` EXIT 0.
  - **TS-strict / no-suppressions / scope.** grep on the hook: no `any`/ts-ignore/ts-expect-error/eslint-disable/`console.*` = NONE. Dialog diffs are surgical: each adds `ref`+`role="dialog"`/`aria-modal`/`aria-labelledby`+stable id and one `useFocusTrap` call; CpvPage RescheduleDialog correctly MOVED `role/aria-modal` from the backdrop to the card and swapped `aria-label`→`aria-labelledby` (id `cpv-reschedule-title`). aria-labelledby ids are page-unique (one dialog mounts at a time). Every changed line traces to the a11y ask.

- **2026-06-09 · B-8/B-9 Hexagon loader + §6 loading time-bands on the Universal DataGrid (working tree, uncommitted; NEW `components/ui/HexagonLoader.tsx` + NEW `lib/useLoadingBand.ts` + `DataGrid.tsx` + `index.css` keyframe + 1 Playwright test). VERDICT: PASS (one non-blocking a11y SHOULD-FIX, Design-owned).** Read both new files in full + every diff hunk; traced the band state machine, the no-flicker `none`-window gating, and the loader-only-on-first-load claim against the actual react-query/`keepPreviousData` wiring; ran web `tsc`+`eslint` myself.
  - **`useLoadingBand` state machine — CORRECT, no stale band, no stuck loader.** Effect deps `[active]` ONLY (line 34). `active` false→true: cleanup (no-op) → re-run → `setBand('none')` (line 25, the immediate reset before scheduling) → schedule t1/t2/t3 → none→skeleton@300→loader@1s→loader-op@3s. `active` true→false: cleanup clears ALL three timers (lines 29-33) → re-run hits `!active` → `setBand('none')` + early return (lines 21-24) → no orphaned timer can later fire a stale band. Unmount: same cleanup clears all timers. **Loader-stick trace (the load-bearing claim): `isLoading` false → effect `!active` branch → band `'none'` → `showLoader = (band==='loader'||'loader-op')` = false.** The render gates are PURELY band-derived (DataGrid:286-287) — there is no independent loader latch that could survive data arrival. The double `setBand('none')` (once in the inactive branch, once at the top of the active branch) is intentional belt-and-braces, not a bug. The 300ms re-seed on active true→false→true within one mount is clean (cleanup+re-run).
  - **No empty-state / "No records" flicker during the 0–300ms `none` window — VERIFIED.** During first load `isLoading` is true and `band==='none'`: `showSkeleton`=false, `showLoader`=false, AND the error/empty/data rows now gate on `!isLoading` (DataGrid:539,557,566) which is FALSE → all suppressed. tbody renders NOTHING for 0–300ms. The empty-state ("No records") cannot flash before rows arrive. The conditional flip `!showSkeleton`→`!isLoading` is exactly right: the old `!showSkeleton` would have let empty-state render during the `none` window (when showSkeleton was the only loading gate); switching the data/empty/error gates to `!isLoading` closes that flash, while skeleton/loader remain band-gated. Correct decomposition.
  - **Loader-only-on-FIRST-load — VERIFIED against `keepPreviousData`.** `useQuery({ placeholderData: keepPreviousData })` (DataGrid:247) → `isLoading` is the true first-load flag (false whenever cached/placeholder data exists, even mid-refetch). Refetch path: `isLoading` false → band `'none'` → NO loader/skeleton; prior rows stay (placeholder), and the SEPARATE `isFetching && !isLoading` "Updating…" hint (DataGrid:305-308, `aria-live=polite`, NOT `role=status`) shows instead. So a refetch never shows the Hexagon loader and never blanks the grid — the loader is strictly first-load. No `role=status` collision with the test selector (the Updating hint is not role=status).
  - **`exactOptionalPropertyTypes` (confirmed ON, tsconfig.base.json:11) — the `{...(band==='loader-op' ? {operation: loadingOperation} : {})}` spread (DataGrid:542) is the canonical EOP-safe pattern** — `operation?: string` is never assigned `undefined` explicitly; it's either present or absent. `tsc --noEmit` EXIT 0 confirms. No other optional-prop hazard: HexagonLoader's `style={determinate ? {...} : undefined}` is on a DOM `style` prop (not an EOP-governed optional interface member) — fine. `loadingLabel?` defaults via `??`, never spread.
  - **HexagonLoader dash math — CORRECT both modes (`pathLength=100` normalizes the perimeter to 100 units).** Determinate: `strokeDasharray='100'` (one full-perimeter dash) + `strokeDashoffset = 100 - value` → 0% shows offset 100 (nothing drawn), 100% shows offset 0 (full outline) — correct fill direction. Indeterminate: `strokeDasharray='25 75'` (a 25-unit marching segment + 75 gap) + the `acs-hex-march` keyframe animating `stroke-dashoffset 0→-100` (one full loop/1.2s) — segment marches the outline. Both valid against pathLength normalization. **`percent` clamp is robust: `Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Math.round(percent)))`** — over-100→100, negative→0; `Math.round(NaN)=NaN`, `Math.min(100,NaN)=NaN`, `Math.max(0,NaN)=NaN` → `NaN` would render `dashoffset=100-NaN=NaN` (SVG treats invalid as 0 → full ring) and `{NaN}%` text. NaN is only reachable if a caller passes `percent: NaN` explicitly (no current caller passes `percent` at all → indeterminate); minor, flagged as a NOTE not a defect since the standard says callers pass a REAL percentage. The determinate inline `transition: 'stroke-dashoffset 300ms ease'` is acceptable (component-local animation of a dynamic value; not a token concern).
  - **CSS / JIT — NO purge risk.** `.hex-march` + `@keyframes acs-hex-march` + the `prefers-reduced-motion` guard live in `@layer components` in index.css — these are HAND-AUTHORED classes, not JIT-generated utilities, so Tailwind's content-purge (which only strips generated utilities) never touches them; they emit as written regardless of content scanning. Belt-and-braces, the class literal `'hex-march'` also appears verbatim in the source template string (HexagonLoader:41) so even a utility would be JIT-retained. Valid Tailwind v3 `@layer components` usage; reduced-motion `animation:none` correctly disables the march while the `role=status`/`aria-label` text still announces loading.
  - **Boundaries / reuse — clean, genuinely reusable, not over-built.** `HexagonLoader` in `components/ui/` (shared, app-internal, not feature-internal — matches the DataGrid/data-grid precedent; no new `@crm2/ui` package → no ADR). `useLoadingBand` in `lib/` (cross-cutting, alongside useFocusTrap/format/sdk). dependency-cruiser: both have a real importer (DataGrid imports both) → `no-orphans` satisfied; `no-cross-feature-internals` N/A (neither is under features/); layering rules N/A (FE component). The determinate mode + `operation`/`subStep`/`percent` API is the MINIMUM the standard mandates for the future report/MIS/export §8 stage-maps — it's the shared platform loader, not speculative (indeterminate mode is the only path wired now; determinate is the documented contract those jobs will consume). `loadingLabel` has no consumer yet but falls back to title-cased `queryKey` — acceptable thin extension point, not gold-plating.
  - **TS-strict / no-suppressions / scope.** grep `^+` on the diff + both new files: no `any`, no ts-ignore/ts-expect-error/eslint-disable, no `console.*`, no SELECT-star. `SKELETON_AFTER_MS/LOADER_AFTER_MS/LOADER_OP_AFTER_MS` are named consts (no magic numbers); SVG geometry consts `HEX_POINTS`/`PATH_LENGTH` named. - **2026-06-09 · Row-select + bulk actions sub-slice 1 (working tree, uncommitted; `DataGrid.tsx` + `MasterDataCrud.tsx` + sdk `export.ts` + platform `export/index.ts` + clients/products repo&service + clients-api & platform-export tests). VERDICT: PASS (no must-fix; 2 non-blocking SHOULD-FIX/NOTE).** Read the full DataGrid selection block (DataGrid.tsx:311-360, 555-600, header/filter/skeleton/data-row cells) + both services + both repos + the sdk/platform contract leaves; traced the selection state machine, the `allMatching` ↔ per-row interaction, the empty-ids guard, and the `id = ANY($n)` bind by hand.
  - **Selection state machine — CORRECT.** Clear-effect deps `[search, sortBy, sortOrder, filtersKey]` (DataGrid.tsx:320) — exactly the inputs that change the MATCHED set. `filtersKey = JSON.stringify(mergedFilters)` (line 220) folds column/date/domain filters into one stable string dep, so a filter change clears selection; **page and size are intentionally NOT deps → selection accumulates across pages and survives a page-size change** (matching the documented "accumulates across pages" contract, DataGrid.tsx:106). No stale-closure / infinite-render: the effect only calls the two stable `setState` setters with fresh `new Set()`/`false` (no derived value in the dep list, no setter reading prior state via closure), so it runs once per matched-set change and cannot loop. `selectedIds`/`allMatching` are plain `useState`; `toggleRow`/`togglePage` use the functional updater (`prev => new Set(prev)`) — no stale snapshot.
  - **`allMatching` ↔ per-row interaction — sane, traced the exact sequence the charter asked about.** To REACH `allMatching` the user first ticks select-all-on-page (`togglePage` → `selectedIds == pageIds`), the "Select all N matching" banner appears (gated `allPageSelected && !allMatching && totalCount > pageIds.length`, DataGrid.tsx:563) → `setAllMatching(true)`. While `allMatching`, every row checkbox shows `checked = allMatching || selectedIds.has(row.id)` (line ~595) = all checked, and the header shows `checked = allMatching || allPageSelected` = checked. A per-row UNtick then runs `toggleRow`: it sets `allMatching=false` FIRST, then toggles that one id OUT of the still-page-full `selectedIds` → result = "this page minus one row" (the original page-tick set with one removed). That is the **sane** outcome: dropping out of allMatching reveals the concrete page-level selection that backed it, minus the row just unticked — not an empty or surprising set. Confirmed the export wiring honors this: `allMatching ? runExport('all') : runExport('selected', [...selectedIds])` (exportSelection, DataGrid.tsx:357-358) — allMatching exports the whole query (`all`, no ids), an explicit set exports exactly the ticked ids.
  - **Header `indeterminate` ref callback — CORRECT.** `ref={(el) => { if (el) el.indeterminate = !allMatching && !allPageSelected && somePageSelected; }}` (DataGrid.tsx ~589). `indeterminate` is a DOM-only property (not a React attribute) so the ref-callback is the right channel; the `if (el)` null-guard handles unmount; the predicate is exhaustive — full page → `checked` (not indeterminate); none → neither; partial → indeterminate; allMatching → `checked`, indeterminate false. No tri-state gap.
  - **colCount / colSpan — consistent across all rows.** `colCount = visibleColumns.length + (selectable ? 1 : 0)` (DataGrid.tsx:356). The loader (line 683), error (693), and empty (703) rows all `colSpan={colCount}` (was `visibleColumns.length`) — so the leading selection cell is covered and no row under/over-spans → no layout break. The leading cell is added ONLY when `selectable` and identically across header (`<th class="w-10 px-3 py-2">`), filter row (`<th class="w-10 px-3 pb-2"/>`), skeleton (`<td class="px-3 py-2.5"/>`), and data row (`<td onClick=stopPropagation>`). Header/filter/skeleton/data all gain the cell in lockstep → column alignment preserved under column-visibility too (visibleColumns drives both the data cells and the colSpan).
  - **onRowClick interaction — CORRECT.** The data-row checkbox `<td>` has `onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}` (DataGrid.tsx ~593) so ticking a row does NOT bubble to the row's `onClick={onRowClick ? () => onRowClick(row.original) : undefined}` → no accidental navigation when selecting (cases/rates set onRowClick). The checkbox's own `onChange` still fires (stopPropagation is on click, not change). Rows without onRowClick are unaffected.
  - **`runExport` selected path — CORRECT.** `ids` is included ONLY for `mode==='selected'` and only when non-empty (`...(mode === 'selected' && ids && ids.length ? { ids } : {})`, DataGrid.tsx:249); page/limit included ONLY for `current` (line 248) so `selected`/`all` correctly drop the page window. sdk `exportQueryToParams` mirrors this: `all`||`selected` strip `{page,limit}` and `ids` is serialized only for `selected` with non-empty ids (export.ts) — FE and SDK agree.
  - **Backend `id = ANY($n)` bind — CORRECT for an int column, no cast needed.** `params.push(o.ids)` pushes the JS `number[]` as a SINGLE param at `$${params.length}`, then `id = ANY($n)` (clients repo:43-45, products repo identical). node-postgres serializes a JS array param to a Postgres array literal and `ANY(int[])` compares against the `int` PK — the integer JS numbers coerce to the column type with no `::int[]` cast required (the API test `mode=selected&ids=<intId>` returns only that row, 200, and excludes the unticked code → proves the bind round-trips). LIMIT/OFFSET correctly continue at `params.length + 1/+2` AFTER the array push, so the array param index doesn't collide.
  - **Empty-ids guard — AIRTIGHT.** Service: `selectedIds = ex.mode==='selected' ? ex.ids.map(Number).filter(Number.isInteger) : undefined`; then `if (ex.mode==='selected' && (!selectedIds || selectedIds.length===0)) return { rows: [], columns }` — the early-return fires BEFORE `repo.list`, so a `selected` mode with zero VALID ids returns nothing and **cannot fall through to an unfiltered list** (the exact "export everything" trap). The repo's `if (o.ids && o.ids.length)` guard would otherwise omit the `ANY` clause on an empty array, but the service short-circuit means the repo is never reached with empty ids in `selected` mode. Belt-and-braces, and the spread `...(selectedIds ? { ids } : {})` (EOP-safe) only passes `ids` when defined. The api test "mode=selected with no ids exports nothing (header only, 1 line)" proves it. Non-integer/garbage ids are dropped by `Number.isInteger` → if ALL are garbage the guard treats it as empty → nothing exported (safe).
  - **Scope preservation — N/A for these two modules (master-data is GLOBAL, not user-scoped); the ids filter is correctly ANDed on top of active/search/columnFilters.** clients/products `repo.list` has no `userScope`/`dataScope` clause (master data is not row-scoped), so "ANDed on top of scope" reduces to ANDed on top of the existing WHERE — which is exactly what the diff does (`where.push('id = ANY($n)')` after the active/search/filter pushes). DON'T-REGRESS for the rollout: **when this `ids` filter is extended to a SCOPED list (cases/tasks via `userScope`/`dataScope`), the `id = ANY` clause MUST remain ANDed after the scope predicate (never replace it)** so a user can't export a ticked id outside their scope (IDOR). Flagged for the Security auditor on the next sub-slice.
  - **Contract leaves — sound & additive.** sdk `ExportMode` gains `'selected'` (additive union member), `ExportRequest.ids?: string[]` (optional, EOP-safe — only set in params when present); `ResolvedExport.ids: string[]` (always-present, defaults `[]` — `resolveExport` parses `ids` the same way as `cols`: string-split-filter-Boolean, non-string/blank → `[]`). `MODES` gains `'selected'` so `mode=selected` no longer 400s (the test that asserted it threw is correctly retargeted to `mode=bogus`). The `BulkSelection` interface is fully typed (no `any`): `allMatching/ids/count/query: PageQuery/clear: () => void`; `bulkActions?: (selection: BulkSelection) => ReactNode` is a clean optional render-prop. `getRowId: (row) => String(rowId(row))` (DataGrid.tsx:298) means TanStack `row.id` === the `String(rowId(r))` keys in `selectedIds`/`pageIds` → the row-checkbox `selectedIds.has(row.id)` and `toggleRow(row.id)` key correctly against the page-tick set. No string/number id skew.
  - **TS-strict / boundaries / scope.** grep `^+` on the diff: no `any`, no ts-ignore/ts-expect-error/eslint-disable, no `console.*`, no magic numbers in service/repo (the `w-10`/`z`/`px` are Tailwind utilities, not service constants). Layering intact: SQL stays in repos, service does the int-coercion + empty guard, controller untouched. Bespoke selection UI built in-app (no new package → no ADR). exactOptionalPropertyTypes-safe conditional spreads throughout (`...(selectedIds ? {ids} : {})`, `...(mode==='selected' && ids?.length ? {ids} : {})`). Surgical: every changed line traces to the row-select/bulk-export ask; the `current` ternary flip in both services is behavior-preserving for `all` (was `all→(threshold,0)`, now `not-current→(threshold,0)` and `all` is in not-current) and correct for the new `selected` (the `ANY` filter bounds the set; the big limit is just a ceiling). `assertExportable` stays `all`-only → a `selected` export can't 413 (acceptable — a ticked set is bounded by on-screen selection).
  - **🚩 SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, Design/UX-owned):** the bulk-bar export buttons share the grid-wide `exporting` flag, so the XLSX button's label becomes "Exporting…" while a CSV (or toolbar) export runs, and BOTH bulk export buttons + the toolbar export disable together (`disabled={!!exporting}`). Harmless (prevents double-fire) but the "Exporting…" text on the XLSX button during a CSV run is mildly misleading; tidy with a per-button busy check (`exporting?.endsWith(':xlsx')`) if it bothers UX. NOTE (not a defect): URL-tamper can't reach an unsafe selection — selection is in-memory only, never URL-persisted, and the server re-validates ids against the (here global) list query.
  - **VERDICT: PASS — clear-effect deps are exactly the matched-set inputs (page/size correctly excluded → accumulate), no stale-closure/loop; allMatching↔per-row untick yields the sane "page minus one" set; indeterminate ref-callback exhaustive; colCount unifies every colSpan + the leading cell is added in lockstep across header/filter/skeleton/data; checkbox `<td>` stopPropagation shields onRowClick; the `id = ANY($n)` JS-number[] bind round-trips against the int PK with no cast (test-proven); the empty-ids guard early-returns BEFORE repo.list so `selected`+no-valid-ids exports NOTHING (never falls through to all); contract additive + fully typed, zero suppressions. OPEN: (1) per-button export-busy label; (2) **DON'T-REGRESS for the rollout — keep `id = ANY` ANDed AFTER any `userScope`/`dataScope` predicate when this lands on scoped lists (cases/tasks), so a ticked out-of-scope id can't leak (Security to gate that sub-slice).**

- **2026-06-09 · Row-select + bulk actions sub-slice 2 — bulk activate/deactivate, per-row OCC (working tree, uncommitted; 3 new files `platform/bulk.ts` + sdk `bulk.ts` + web `BulkStatusActions.tsx`, plus `DataGrid.tsx` Set→Map refactor, clients/products controller+routes+service, `MasterDataCrud.tsx`, sdk `index.ts`, clients-api test). VERDICT: PASS (no must-fix; 2 non-blocking NOTEs).** Read all 3 new files in full + the diff; traced the Map refactor against TanStack `getRowId`, the `applyBulkOcc` error-classification against `AppError.stale`/`notFound`, and `parseBulkItems` validation by hand. Ran all 3 packages `tsc --noEmit` (EXIT 0 ×3) + `eslint DataGrid.tsx BulkStatusActions.tsx` (EXIT 0) myself.
  - **Set→Map refactor — CORRECT; the keys stay in lockstep with TanStack `row.id`.** `getRowId: (row) => String(rowId(row))` (DataGrid.tsx:304) is unchanged, so TanStack's `row.id` IS the stringified `rowId(row)`. `selectedRows` is now `Map<string, T>` keyed by that SAME `String(rowId(row))`: `toggleRow(row)` derives `id = String(rowId(row))` (line 338) then `next.set(id, row)`; `togglePage` stores `items.forEach(r => next.set(String(rowId(r)), r))` (line 352, correctly switched from `pageIds.add` to capture the row OBJECT not just the id). The checkbox checked-state `selectedRows.has(row.id)` (line 733) keys on TanStack `row.id` === the Map key → membership test is exact, no string/number skew. `allPageSelected = pageIds.every(id => selectedRows.has(id))` and `somePageSelected = pageIds.some(...)` (lines 327-328) both probe the Map by the same `pageIds` strings → checkbox/header/indeterminate semantics are byte-identical to the prior Set impl (the Map is a strict superset: same keys, plus a value). `selectedCount = allMatching ? totalCount : selectedRows.size`. Clear-effect deps `[search, sortBy, sortOrder, filtersKey]` and the `new Map()` reset are the same matched-set-change contract as before. `ids: [...selectedRows.keys()]` and the export path `[...selectedRows.keys()]` (line 367) preserve the prior id-only behavior. **`bulkSelection.rows: [...selectedRows.values()]`** is the new payload-bearing field — the row objects captured at tick time, carrying `version`.
  - **Stale-version-is-intended-OCC — CONFIRMED correct, not a bug.** The captured row object (and its `version`) is a snapshot taken when the checkbox was ticked; if another user edits that row before the bulk action fires, the snapshot `version` goes behind the DB. That is EXACTLY what `repo.setActive`'s guarded `UPDATE … WHERE id=$1 AND version=$4` (clients/repository.ts:172-177) catches: 0 rows updated → re-SELECT `before` → `AppError.stale(before)` (409 STALE_UPDATE) → classified CONFLICT → reported per-row, **never a silent overwrite**. The stale snapshot is the OCC trip-wire working as designed; refreshing the grid would only paper over a real concurrent edit. The FE (`BulkStatusActions`) surfaces "N changed by someone else" and KEEPS the selection so the user can re-tick + retry (line 49). Correct end-to-end.
  - **`applyBulkOcc` error classification — CORRECT, and rethrow is the right call.** Verified against the live error factory: `AppError.stale` sets `code='STALE_UPDATE'` at status 409 (errors.ts:55), `AppError.notFound` sets `status=404` (errors.ts:35). The matcher (bulk.ts:74-81) tests `e instanceof AppError && e.code==='STALE_UPDATE'` → CONFLICT, then `e instanceof AppError && e.status===HTTP_STATUS.NOT_FOUND` (404) → NOT_FOUND, **else `throw e`**. Rethrowing non-OCC errors is the correct, defensive choice: a real DB/connection fault (or any non-OCC AppError) must propagate to the controller `catch → next(e)` → the global handler (a 500), NOT be silently absorbed as a fake per-row "status" that would tell the user the row "succeeded/not-found" when the write never even resolved. Classification is by `code` (STALE) and `status` (404) — both stable contract surfaces, won't drift. **Counts are consistent with results:** exactly one of `results.push` + one `count += 1` runs per item in the matched branch; rethrow exits the loop WITHOUT pushing → no orphan count, no result without a count. `results.length === okCount + conflictCount + notFoundCount` holds for any fully-iterated batch. Sequential `for…of await` (not `Promise.all`) → each row is its own `withTransaction` (per-row atomicity + one audit row each, the standing OCC-write pattern), and ordered results. Test "mixed batch" proves OK/CONFLICT/NOT_FOUND map 1/1/1 with the right per-id status.
  - **`parseBulkItems` — validation airtight, no raw value reaches SQL.** `body.items` must be a non-empty array else `400 BULK_ITEMS_REQUIRED` (bulk.ts:38, test-proven); `> MAX_BULK_ITEMS (500)` → `400 BULK_TOO_LARGE` (line 39, the §1 sync-batch ceiling — larger is a future background job). Per item: `version = Number(o.version)` must be a non-negative integer else `400 BULK_ITEM_INVALID` (line 44) — a malformed item is a HARD 400, never silently dropped (the charter's "no partial-but-wrong batch" requirement). `idKind==='int'`: `id = Number(o.id)` must be `Number.isInteger && > 0` else 400 (line 47); `idKind==='uuid'`: `typeof === 'string' && UUID_RE.test` else 400 (line 50). So by the time an id/version reaches `repo.setActive`, it is a validated JS `number` (or a regex-validated uuid string), and `setActive` binds it as a parameter (`$1`/`$4`, never interpolated) — **double safety: type-validated AND param-bound**. The service further wraps `Number(id)` (service.ts) belt-and-braces for the int modules. No injection surface. (`BULK_*` codes are passed as the `string` arg of `AppError.badRequest`, whose signature accepts `ErrorCode | string` — they are intentionally NOT in the `ErrorCode` enum; consistent with how dynamic codes are handled, tsc-clean.)
  - **Reuse not bespoke — CONFIRMED.** `bulkSetActive` (clients/service.ts:128-131, products identical) calls `parseBulkItems` then `applyBulkOcc(items, (id, version) => repo.setActive(Number(id), isActive, userId, version))` — the SAME version-guarded, audited `repo.setActive` the single-row `activate`/`deactivate` already use. **No second write path**, one `appendAudit` row per mutated row preserved (inside each per-row `withTransaction`), commission/rollup semantics untouched (master-data has none). The platform helpers + sdk leaf are the only new abstraction, and they are generic (reused by both modules already, ready for the rollout) — not a single-use over-abstraction.
  - **Routing — no Express collision, CONFIRMED.** `POST /bulk-activate` + `/bulk-deactivate` are STATIC single-segment paths declared BEFORE `POST /:id/activate` + `/:id/deactivate` (two-segment) in both clients/routes.ts:18-21 and products/routes.ts. A static literal and a `/:id/activate` pattern occupy different path shapes (`/bulk-activate` is ONE segment; `/:id/activate` is TWO) so they can't collide regardless of order; declaring the statics first is belt-and-braces and matches the established `/export` + `/options`-before-`/:id` ordering idiom. Both bulk routes carry `authorize(PERMISSIONS.MASTERDATA_MANAGE)` — same authz as the single-row write siblings (test proves 403 for FIELD_AGENT, 401 unauth).
  - **TS-strict / boundaries / contract.** grep across all 3 new files + diff: NO `any`, NO ts-ignore/ts-expect-error/eslint-disable, NO `console.*`, no magic numbers in service/controller/repo (`MAX_BULK_ITEMS=500` is a named platform const). Layering intact: `parseBulkItems`/`applyBulkOcc` live in `platform/` (cross-feature shared, correct home next to `occ.ts`/`pagination.ts`), service wires them, raw SQL stays in repos, controllers are the std `try/res.json(await svc...)/catch→next(e)` shape. **Platform `BulkResult` vs SDK `BulkResult` are structurally identical** (same `results[{id,status}]` + 3 counts; `BulkRowStatus` same union) — the service returns the platform shape, the controller `res.json`s it, the FE reads the SDK shape; they are duck-compatible by construction (FINE — the platform copy is the server-internal type, the sdk copy is the wire contract; no import cycle, intentional mirror like the export leaves). Generic `BulkSelection<T>` threads `T` cleanly: `DataGridProps.bulkActions?: (selection: BulkSelection<T>) => ReactNode`, re-exported from the data-grid index, consumed by `BulkStatusActions<T extends Versioned>` whose `Versioned{id:string|number; version:number}` constraint guarantees `selection.rows.map(r => ({id:r.id, version:r.version}))` is well-typed. exactOptionalPropertyTypes: no new optional-prop spreads introduced (the `?` props on `BulkItem.id` union / interfaces are plain optionals, not pushed into a typed object); EOP-clean across the slice (web tsc EXIT 0 confirms). SDK `bulk.ts` is a CONTRACT-ONLY leaf (zero client methods) → the `toBe(66)` SDK call-count invariant is UNTOUCHED.
  - **Array→envelope trap (standing DON'T-REGRESS) — N/A in the breaking direction.** The bulk endpoints are NEW (no prior consumer to break), and they return a fresh object shape (`BulkResult`) read by exactly one consumer (`BulkStatusActions` via raw `api<BulkResult>('POST', …)`). No existing response shape changed. The `BulkSelection` interface gained a `rows: T[]` field and went generic — all consumers (only `MasterDataCrud`→`BulkStatusActions`) updated in-slice; web tsc EXIT 0 proves no stale `BulkSelection` (non-generic) reference remains.
  - **NOTE (not a defect):** (1) `BulkStatusActions` catch-all `catch { setMessage('Bulk update failed…') }` swallows the error object — acceptable for a UI toast (the per-row CONFLICT/NOT_FOUND are NOT errors, they come back in the 200 body; this catch only fires on a true network/500), but it means a 400 BULK_TOO_LARGE shows the generic message rather than "too many rows" — fine for now since the grid can't tick >500 on one page; revisit if allMatching ever feeds bulk. (2) `allMatching` correctly renders the "tick individual rows" hint and offers NO bulk button (BulkStatusActions.tsx:57-60) — a versioned mutation genuinely can't target off-page rows whose versions aren't loaded; matches the `BulkSelection.rows` doc ("empty when allMatching"). Correct, not a gap.
  - **VERDICT: PASS — the Set→Map refactor preserves every selection semantic (keys stay `String(rowId)` === TanStack `row.id`; checkbox/header/indeterminate/clear/export all probe the Map identically), adds only the captured row objects + their `version`; the stale captured-version is the OCC trip-wire working AS DESIGNED → CONFLICT, never silent overwrite; `applyBulkOcc` classifies STALE→CONFLICT (by code) / 404→NOT_FOUND (by status) and RETHROWS everything else so a real fault can't masquerade as a row status, counts always == results; `parseBulkItems` hard-400s empty/oversize/malformed (drops nothing) and type/regex-validates id+version before the already-param-bound `setActive` → no injection; bulkSetActive reuses the one audited OCC write (no second path); static `/bulk-*` routes can't collide with `/:id/*`; zero suppressions, all-strict clean ×3, EOP-safe, SDK call-count invariant intact.   - **colCount accounting — EVERY path includes the expander, CONFIRMED.** `colCount = visibleColumns.length + (selectable?1:0) + (renderExpanded?1:0)` (line 377). The three flat-row paths that key off it — loader (`colSpan={colCount}`, line 711), error (719), empty (730) — and the new **expanded-detail** `colSpan={colCount}` (the detail `<td>`) are byte-identical to that one source-of-truth count, so all four stretch full-width whether or not the expander column is present. The two HAND-ROLLED leading-cell paths add a matching leading cell in lockstep: **header** `<th aria-label="Expand">` (line 631) and **skeleton** `<td>` (line 699) each render exactly one extra leading cell when `renderExpanded` is set, so header-cell-count == body-cell-count == colCount on every band (none/skeleton/loader/empty/error/data). The filter row also adds its leading `<th>` (line 670) keeping the §6 filter row 1:1 with the header. **No off-by-one: the expander cell precedes the `selectable` cell consistently in header, filter, skeleton, AND data rows (same order everywhere).**
  - **Pattern reuse — mirrors the `selectable` leading-column precedent faithfully.** The expander column is inserted in the SAME five places `selectable` already touches (header th / filter th / skeleton td / data-row td), always BEFORE the `selectable` cell, with the same `data-label=""` + `e.stopPropagation()` on its cell idiom. This is the established precedent, not a new pattern → no ADR trigger. Bespoke chevron glyphs (▸/▾) + `<button>` are owned-in-app (no new dep).
  - **expandedId reset effect — deps CORRECT, no stale-expansion render risk.** `useEffect(() => setExpandedId(null), [search, sortBy, sortOrder, filtersKey, page, limit])` (line 377). It DELIBERATELY differs from the selection reset (line 337, deps `[search,sortBy,sortOrder,filtersKey]` — NO page/limit) and the difference is correct per opposite semantics: selection ACCUMULATES across pages so must survive paging; expansion is single-row ephemeral chrome and the open row LEAVES the viewport on page/limit change, so it must clear. Even if a stale `expandedId` ever survived (it can't via these deps), it is render-harmless: server-side pagination means the matching id is simply absent from `items`, so `expandedId === row.id` matches no row → nothing renders expanded (graceful no-op, no crash, no orphan detail row). `getRowId:(row)=>String(rowId(row))` (313) === the `row.id` stored by `toggleExpand(row.id)` === the `expandedId === row.id` compare — id space is consistent end-to-end.
  - **Event handling — single-fire, no double-toggle, mutual-exclusion sound.** Row `onClick` is a three-way: `onRowClick` wins if present, ELSE `renderExpanded` → `toggleExpand(row.id)`, ELSE undefined (so a plain grid stays non-interactive). The chevron path is double-guarded: the chevron `<td>` carries `onClick={(e)=>e.stopPropagation()}` and the inner `<button onClick={()=>toggleExpand(row.id)}>` — the button click toggles once, bubbles to the td, the td halts propagation BEFORE it reaches the `<tr>`, so the chevron NEVER also fires the row handler → exactly one toggle per chevron click (same stopPropagation idiom the `selectable` checkbox cell uses). The `onRowClick`-vs-`renderExpanded` mutual exclusion is DOC-enforced (§20 + JSDoc), not code-enforced; when both are mistakenly passed, `onRowClick` takes the row body and the chevron still toggles via stopPropagation — graceful degradation, not a defect (matches how `selectable` + `onRowClick` already coexist).
  - **React key/Fragment — correct.** Each row is now a `<Fragment key={row.id}>` wrapping the data `<tr>` + the optional detail `<tr>`; the key moved from the `<tr>` up to the Fragment (the only stable list key needed — two sibling `<tr>`s under one keyed Fragment need no inner keys). `Fragment` imported as a named value (line 1). Detail `<tr>` is gated `expanded && renderExpanded` so it's null when collapsed (no empty stray rows). No key collision (row ids unique within a page).
  - **TS-strict / boundaries / tokens.** New prop `renderExpanded?: (row: T) => ReactNode` — additive optional, generic-threaded `T`, no `any`, no `as`, no ts-ignore/eslint-disable, no `console.*`. `useState<string|null>` typed. exactOptionalProps N/A (no new optional-prop spread into a typed object). Tailwind tokens all pre-existing: `bg-accent` (index.css:15), `bg-row-hover` (header/rows already), `bg-surface-muted` (header line 630, so `bg-surface-muted/40` is a valid opacity modifier). Full-project web `tsc --noEmit` EXIT 0.

No existing prop, signature, or contract touched. Doc §20 added to DATAGRID_STANDARD.md describing the opt-in, the one-open/ephemeral/reset semantics, and the `onRowClick` mutual-exclusion — matches the code.
  - **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, Design-owned):** the open parent row sets `bg-accent` but the row also carries `hover:bg-row-hover`, so on hover the accent highlight is visually overridden (the open-state tint disappears while the cursor is over it) — cosmetic only, the chevron `▾` + `aria-expanded` still convey state; tighten with `hover:bg-accent` on the open row if Design wants the tint to persist on hover. NOTE: a11y — the chevron button has `aria-expanded` + dynamic `aria-label` (good), but the detail `<tr>` is not programmatically associated to its trigger (no `aria-controls`/`id`); acceptable for an inline accordion, flag for the Design/a11y ledger. **No must-fix — every changed line traces to the §20 master-detail ask; colCount math is consistent across all 6 bands; reset deps are correct for the ephemeral semantic. No dead import.
  - **Backend envelope / layering — correct.** Controller forwards `req.query` whole to `svc.list` (validation/whitelisting pushed into the service via `resolvePage`/`resolveFilters`/`CP_PAGE_SPEC`); repository takes resolved `ClientProductListOptions` with already-whitelisted `sortColumn`/`sortOrder` (sortMap→`c.code`/`p.code`/`unit_count`/`cp.is_active`/dates) and bound `columnFilters` (filterMap client/product=text, createdAt/effectiveFrom=date). COUNT + items share `CP_FROM`; both joins are PK-side 1:1, so `count(*)` over the join == #client_products rows — totalCount exact, NO fan-out (the comment claims this and it holds). ORDER BY appends qualified `cp.id` tiebreaker (bare `id` ambiguous across the 3-table join). Legacy `clientId`/`active` filters preserved (active=true still gated to usable, effective_from<=now, ADR-0017). `version` returned in list rows (toggle's OCC token). Unknown-`sortBy`→default fallback and `limit>500`→400 are platform `resolvePage` gates, now CPV-test-pinned.
  - **Runtime-contract trap caught.** array→envelope consumer `cases.api.test.ts:489` `.body[0]`→`.body.items[0]`; backend envelope test added (page/limit/sort/search/f_client·f_product/limit>500→400/`sortBy` injection→fallback). Pinned.
  - **TS-strict / tokens.** No `any`/`as`/ts-ignore in the diff; `DataGridColumn<ClientProductView>` generic-threaded; cells use pre-existing tokens only. `pnpm verify` EXIT=0 (api 349/349, sdk 70) + Playwright 23/0 incl. new §20 expand→UnitManager→collapse + CPV a11y scan. **No must-fix. Every changed line traces to "CPV→DataGrid". Cleared to commit.**

### 2026-06-10 — C-3 Slice 4 (CPV `client_products` universal import; FK-resolving B-14; `import.ts` + svc/controller/routes + `<ImportButton>`) — PASS
  - **`buildClientProductSpec.resolve` row-math — correct.** Both FK checks accumulate into one `errors[]`: unknown `clientCode` pushes a `Client Code` error, unknown `productCode` pushes a `Product Code` error; `if (errors.length>0) return {ok:false,errors}` (import.ts:65) ⇒ a row missing EITHER (or both) codes is `ok:false` and never reaches `create`. Only the all-present branch returns `{ok:true,value:{clientId!,productId!,…effectiveFrom}}` (import.ts:66-73). The engine's `resolveValid` (index.ts:151-167) maps each `ok:false` to one ImportRowError per column and excludes the row from `processable`. Test pins it: a 2-row file [HDFC/HOME_LOAN, NOPE/HOME_LOAN] → `validRows:1, errorRows:1, errors[0].column:'Client Code'`. Math sound. Mirror of `buildRateSpec` minus the unit + pincode/area legs.
  - **Confirm reuses `clientProductService.create` (NOT `repo.create`) — verified.** `importConfirm`'s `process` closure is `async (input) => { await clientProductService.create(input, userId); }` (service.ts:148-150). That keeps the zod normalization (`CreateClientProductSchema.parse`) + the in-tx `appendAudit` CREATE row that `cpRepo.create` emits — so every imported link is audited identically to a UI create. Calling `cpRepo.create` directly would still audit (the audit is in the repo) but would SKIP the create-schema parse; routing through the service preserves the single validation chokepoint. Correct choice.
  - **Per-row tx isolation on a mid-batch duplicate — holds.** `runImportConfirm`'s loop (index.ts:210-221) wraps each `process(value)` in its own try/catch; `cpRepo.create` runs in its OWN `withTransaction` (repository.ts) and a unique-violation → `AppError.conflict('CLIENT_PRODUCT_EXISTS')` (repository.ts) is caught at index.ts:214, pushed as a per-row `*` error, loop continues. Each row = an independent tx (no batch-spanning tx), so a duplicate rolls back ONLY its own row. Test: import [HDFC/HOME_LOAN] twice → 2nd file `{totalRows:1,successRows:0,failedRows:1}` and list `totalCount:1`. `failedRows = rows.length - successRows` (index.ts:226) — duplicate counted as failed, batch not aborted. Confirmed.
  - **Maps USABLE-only — by design, flagged as an intentional gap not a bug.** `clientService.options()`/`productService.options()` return active + in-effect rows only, so an inactive or future-dated client/product code won't be in the map and resolves to a per-row "unknown code" error (import.ts:58-63) rather than silently linking to a dormant master row. Identical semantics to rates (`buildRateSpec` uses the same `options()`). Correct ingest contract (you can't link a product a client can't currently use), but re-activating a client later won't retro-link a row that errored — operator must re-import. Documented in the file header (import.ts:42-44). Not a defect; noting for operator expectation.
  - **Route order — `/import-template` + `/import` before `/:id` — correct, no capture.** Both are single static segments declared at routes.ts:14-21, ahead of `/:id` (PUT, routes.ts:24) and the `/:id/activate` family. Express matches in declaration order, so `GET /import-template` never falls into `/:id`. Same ordering rule the export line already follows. (`POST /` create sits AFTER the import block — fine, distinct method/path.)
  - **No raw SQL in `import.ts` → depcruise `*.repository.ts`-only rule N/A — confirmed.** grep for INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE/SELECT/`q<`/`pool.`/`query(` in import.ts = 0 hits; it imports only zod, SDK types, the platform import types/`parseIsoDate`, and the two domain services. All DB access is via `clientProductService.create` → `cpRepo`. No orphan/dead code: `CP_TEMPLATE_SPEC` (template, no resolve) + `buildClientProductSpec` (with resolve) both consumed by service.ts (importTemplate/importPreview/importConfirm); `CP_IMPORT_COLUMNS`/`CP_IMPORT_SAMPLE`/`ClientProductImportFileSchema` shared by both specs. New imports (`resolveImportMode`/`writeTemplate` in controller; `buildTemplate`/`runImportConfirm`/`runImportPreview` + `buildClientProductSpec`/`CP_TEMPLATE_SPEC` in service; `raw` in routes; `ImportButton` in CpvPage) all used.
  - **TS-strict / verification accepted.** `pnpm verify` EXIT=0 (api 358/358 incl. the +5 CPV import tests: template PK+filename / preview valid+unknown-code / confirm+import_log / duplicate-per-row-409→failedRows / perms 403+401); tsc clean; live dev confirmed (template, CSV preview resolving HDFC/HOME_LOAN + flagging NOPE row3, Import modal renders). **No must-fix.
