- **INFO · old `total` bug fixed** (see (b)) — if any downstream consumer relied on the old under-counted `total`, it now reports higher; no such consumer found (FE reads `stats.data?.[b.stat]` per-chip; `total` only feeds the "All" chip count, which SHOULD be the superset).
- **INFO · `aging`/`overdue`/`OPEN_HELD` untouched** — still include SUBMITTED_FOR_REVIEW (separate aging concern, correctly not folded into the new SLA predicate).
**Bottom line:** the SLA predicate is correct, OPEN-only, param-free and safely inlined as column+filter+aggregate; the stats refactor fixes a real old `total` under-count and the camelize bridge maps `in_progress`/`out_of_tat`/`awaiting_completion` correctly; the dashboard SLA duplication is the RIGHT call under the module-boundary invariant (the file already duplicates `caseScopePredicate`); the 2-query dashboard is a forced grain split, not N+1, with independent param arrays; layering clean, 0 suppressions, 3 packages typecheck EXIT 0, no stale `awaitingReview`/`cancelled` readers. Two FLAG-minors (SLA-const drift, cross-grain scope semantics) are latent/future, not dev-blocking. **Cleared to commit — RUN `tasks.api` + `dashboard.api` against a live test DB first (couldn't execute in sandbox).**

- **2026-06-15 — slice-2c-1 commit review — field-execution ingest spine (ADR-0032). VERDICT: PASS.**
  New `verification-tasks` module (controller/service/routes + tests), 5 device methods in `cases/repository.ts`, `task.execute` perm (`@crm2/access` + migration 0053), `app.ts` mount. Reviewed adversarially against the lens; typecheck EXIT 0, the 4-test suite ran LIVE on :54329/crm2_dev → 4 passed, service 100% cov.
  - **(a) idempotent-by-state pattern — CORRECT, and the state predicate IS the concurrency guard.** Each writer does `UPDATE … WHERE status IN (<from>) RETURNING id`; 0-row → re-SELECT `TASK_VIEW_BY_ID` → target-reached returns current (200) else `AppError.conflict('INVALID_TRANSITION')` (409). The `<from>` set IS the OCC: if the office concurrently moves the row off `<from>` (e.g. unassign ASSIGNED→PENDING), the device UPDATE matches 0 rows → re-read → not-target → 409. No lost update. The device owns its task and sends no version; sending none is SOUND because the row-level status predicate already serializes — no TOCTOU window (read→write is one atomic UPDATE, not select-then-update). `taskForAssignee` re-reads inside no tx but only to resolve caseId for the WHERE; the authoritative gate is the in-tx UPDATE predicate (`id=$1 AND case_id=$2 AND status IN …`), so a stale caseId can't mis-target (caseId is bound, not trusted).
  - **(b) rollup discipline — CORRECT.** complete + revoke call `recomputeCaseStatus` (the single case-status writer, repo:93) inside the tx, after `appendAudit`. start + priority correctly SKIP it. **start ASSIGNED→IN_PROGRESS genuinely needs no rollup:** recompute's `active` bucket = `PENDING|ASSIGNED|IN_PROGRESS` (repo:98) — the task stays in `active`, `agg.active` is unchanged, computed status identical, and the guarded `… AND status <> $2` UPDATE would no-op anyway. priority is metadata-only (no status change) → also correctly skips. revoke→REVOKED and complete→COMPLETED both leave the `active` bucket → can flip the case to AWAITING_COMPLETION/IN_PROGRESS → rollup REQUIRED, present. Test confirms single-task complete → case AWAITING_COMPLETION.
  - **(c) version ratchet — bumped on every writer** (start/complete/revoke/priority all `version = version + 1`), preserving the web-OCC monotonic ratchet so a later office OCC write sees a fresh version. ✅
  - **(d) layering — CORRECT boundary.** Device repo methods live in `cases/repository.ts` (owner of `case_tasks` + the *private* `recomputeCaseStatus`, which is NOT exported) — the rollup can only be invoked from inside the file, so co-locating the writers there is the only way to reach it without leaking the private writer. New module's `service.ts` imports `caseRepository` — established pattern (`tasks/service.ts:13` already imports it for `assignTask`). controller→service→repo intact; raw SQL repo-only; controller never imports repo. Schema verified: `IN_PROGRESS/COMPLETED/REVOKED` all in `chk_case_task_status` (0037), `priority`+chk (0037), `started_at` (0052), `completed_by` (0041) all exist.
  - **(e) single-layer / office-collision — CONFIRMED + 2c-2 GAP NOTED (non-blocking).** `completeTaskByDevice` records NO result: SET touches status/completed_by/completed_at/version only — `verification_outcome` stays null (test asserts `verificationOutcome` null on both start and complete). No collision with the office ADR-0025 `completeTask` (repo:687) which is OCC-version-guarded (`AND version=$6`) and gated in `cases/service.ts:306` to source `ASSIGNED|SUBMITTED_FOR_REVIEW`. ⚠️ **2c-2 GAP:** a device-`COMPLETED` task is NEITHER `ASSIGNED` nor `SUBMITTED_FOR_REVIEW`, so the office can't later record the per-task result on it — `completeTask` would 409 INVALID_TRANSITION. The single-layer slice intentionally ships the field→COMPLETED leg without the office result-recording-on-completed path; that office leg (or routing field submits to SUBMITTED_FOR_REVIEW instead of COMPLETED) is a 2c-2 concern. Flagged, NOT blocking per the brief.
  - **(f) reuse vs reinvent — reuses `TASK_VIEW_BY_ID`/`recomputeCaseStatus`/`appendAudit`/`withTransaction`/`AppError`; raw SQL stays in the repo.** revoke reason rides the audit `after` JSON (no new column) — minimal, no schema churn. controller UUID-regex `parseId` + std try/catch→`next(e)`; route gates `task.execute`; service binds ownership (out-of-ownership ≡ 404, IDOR-safe — test proves non-assignee FA→404, BACKEND_USER→403, assignee→200). `RevokeSchema`/`PrioritySchema` zod-validated (empty reason→400, `PRIORITIES` enum reused from `@crm2/sdk`). Migration 0053 forward-only/idempotent (`ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`), mirrors `@crm2/access` parity. No `any`/suppressions/`console.*`.
  - **NOTE (cosmetic, non-gating):** the service/repo doc-comments cite an "Idempotency-Key" the device sends, but the SERVER parses no such header — server idempotency is purely state-based. The comment describes the device's retry posture (why state-idempotency matters for single-owner retries), not a server claim; accurate but could mislead a reader into grepping for header handling. Optional doc tweak.
  - **Bottom line:** the idempotent-by-state pattern is correct and self-serializing (state predicate = OCC), rollup is invoked exactly where the bucket can change and correctly skipped where it can't, version ratchets on every writer, the cross-module repo import is the established + necessary boundary (private recompute), and single-layer keeps `verification_outcome` null. ONE noted-not-blocking 2c-2 gap: no office path to record a result on a device-COMPLETED task. Cleared to commit.

- **2026-06-15 — slice-2c-2a commit review — OFFICE per-task RESULT recording + device revoke-reason→remark column (ADR-0032 D3). VERDICT: PASS.**
  Closes the 2c-1 noted gap: a device-COMPLETED task carries no result; the office now records the official per-task outcome via new `POST /cases/:id/tasks/:taskId/result` (`recordTaskResult`). Reviewed adversarially against the lens. Files: cases/{repository,service,controller,routes}.ts, sdk/{cases,client}.ts, CaseDetailPage.tsx, cases.api.test.ts.
  - **(a) OCC compare-and-set — CORRECT, byte-faithful to the proven completeTask/assign pattern.** `repo.recordTaskResult` (repository.ts:786-826) does the guarded `UPDATE … SET verification_outcome=$3, remark=$4, completed_by=$5, version=version+1, updated_by=$5, updated_at=now() WHERE id=$1 AND case_id=$2 AND version=$6 AND status='COMPLETED' RETURNING id`; 0-row → re-SELECT `TASK_VIEW_BY_ID` → `!cur || caseId≠` → 404 TASK_NOT_FOUND, else `status≠COMPLETED` → 409 INVALID_TRANSITION, else `AppError.stale(cur)` (version mismatch). All three discriminations present and correctly ordered. `appendAudit` in-tx after the UPDATE. Mirrors the OCC-write template (compare-and-set + 0-row re-SELECT triage) exactly.
  - **(b) status UNCHANGED — confirmed correct, no rollup.** The SET touches NO status column and the writer does NOT call `recomputeCaseStatus` (unlike complete/revoke). Sound: the case is already AWAITING_COMPLETION (all tasks terminal); recording a per-task result on an already-COMPLETED task doesn't move ANY task bucket (recompute's `active=PENDING|ASSIGNED|IN_PROGRESS`, `done=COMPLETED` — the row was COMPLETED before and after), so the computed case status is identical — skipping rollup is the correct optimization, not an omission. Test asserts `status==='COMPLETED'` post-record.
  - **(c) completed_at preserved / completed_by=actor — COHERENT.** SET does not touch `completed_at` (the device field-completion timestamp is preserved — correct, that's when the work was done). `completed_by=$5=actorId` is reassigned to the office resulter. Slight semantic overload (`completed_by` now means "result author" not "field completer", while `completed_at` stays the field time) but DEFENSIBLE: in the single-layer model the office IS the completing authority for the result, and the field-completion actor is recoverable from the device-complete audit row + the `task_assignment_history`. Coherent for the per-task result-author intent; flagged for awareness, not blocking. version ratchets `+1` (preserves the web-OCC monotonic ratchet for any later office OCC write).
  - **(d) layering / reuse — CORRECT.** controller→service→repo intact; raw SQL repo-only; reuses `taskAssignmentState`(scope) + `requireVersion` + `RecordTaskResultSchema.parse` + `TASK_VIEW_BY_ID` + `appendAudit` + `withTransaction` + `AppError`. Service (service.ts:327-334) is structurally identical to `unassignTask`/`completeTask`: parse → requireVersion → state-scope → null→404 → status≠COMPLETED→409 → repo. The repo-layer status re-guard (`AND status='COMPLETED'` in the UPDATE) is defense-in-depth against a TOCTOU between the service's `taskAssignmentState` read and the write (sound — the authoritative gate is the in-tx UPDATE predicate). SDK leaf `RecordTaskResultSchema` = `{result: enum(KYC_RESULTS), remark?: trim.max(2000)}` (cases.ts:374-384); `version` rides OUTSIDE via requireVersion — same envelope as Complete/Finalize. No new pattern, no ADR needed.
  - **(e) device revoke remark — no collision.** `revokeTaskByDevice` now `SET remark=$4` (=`reason`, validated `z.string().trim().min(1).max(MAX_REASON)` in verification-tasks/service.ts:16,37) in addition to the existing audit `after:{status,reason}`. A REVOKED task NEVER holds an office result (it's terminal-before-result; recordTaskResult only touches COMPLETED), so `remark` is free — no path writes both. The `reason` still rides the audit row too (dual-write, not a move). **NOTE (cosmetic, non-gating):** the repository.ts:907 doc-comment "(the reason rides the audit row, not a column)" is now STALE — it IS a column write as of this slice. Same stale-comment class flagged on prior ADR-0020 entries. Optional doc tweak.
  - **(f) FE — clean status-branch on a shared form.** One `CompleteForm` serves both legs (CaseDetailPage.tsx:410-420): `onSubmit` routes `(t.status==='COMPLETED' ? recordResult : complete).mutate(...)`. "Record Result" button shows ONLY for `canComplete && t.status==='COMPLETED' && !t.verificationOutcome` (line 376) — exactly the field-completed-no-result case; pending/error fold both mutations; both invalidate `['case', caseId]`. The form requires `remark.trim().length>0` (line 577) so the FE always sends a remark even though the schema makes it optional — compatible (strict superset; closed schema strips, version read raw). Revoked-remark now rendered inline (line 318, `status==='REVOKED' && t.remark`). No `any`/suppressions/`console.*` in diff.
  - **Bottom line:** recordTaskResult is a faithful clone of the proven completeTask OCC pattern — compare-and-set + 0-row triage (404/409/stale), status-unchanged with correctly-skipped rollup (case already AWAITING_COMPLETION, no bucket moves), completed_at preserved + completed_by=resulter (coherent result-author semantics), closed schema + actor-sourced completed_by (no mass-assignment), in-tx audit. Device revoke→remark is a free, collision-free dual-write. TWO cosmetic notes (stale repo:907 comment; completed_by semantic overload), ZERO blocking. Cleared to commit — RUN `cases.api` (incl the new recordResult test) green on a live test DB before ship.

- **2026-06-15 — slice-2c-2b device form-submit (`submitVerificationForm` + service `submitForm` + 1 route). VERDICT: PASS.** Correct: `jsonb_set(COALESCE(form_data,'{}'::jsonb), ARRAY[$4], $5::jsonb, true)` upserts the blob under `form_data[slug]` (idempotent — resubmit overwrites the slug key, returns 200, matching the device's no-409-swallow DLQ contract); `version=version+1` bumped (web OCC), `updated_by/updated_at` set; **status UNCHANGED, no rollup** (submit ≠ complete — the form upload is separately queued and may arrive post-`complete`, so the allowed set is `ASSIGNED|IN_PROGRESS|COMPLETED`; REVOKED/CANCELLED → 409 INVALID_TRANSITION, 0-row→re-SELECT→404-vs-409 mirrors the established device-writer pattern). - **2026-06-16 — slice-3 (ADR-0033) — task lineage + REVISIT + REASSIGN-AFTER-REVOKE + verdict history (working tree, uncommitted). VERDICT: PASS** (no BLOCK/must-fix; 2 cosmetic NOTEs, 1 INFO). Files: mig `0054_task_lineage.sql`, `ADR-0033`, cases/{repository,service,controller,routes}.ts, sdk/{cases,client}.ts + cases.test.ts, access/permissions.ts, web CaseDetailPage.tsx, +2 generated openapi/api-test.   - **(a) revisit INSERT…SELECT — column/value alignment EXACT (15-col).** `(case_id, verification_unit_id, applicant_id, address, trigger, priority, visit_type, pincode_id, area_id, status, task_number, parent_task_id, task_origin, created_by, updated_by)` ← `p.case_id, p.verification_unit_id, p.applicant_id, p.address, p.trigger, p.priority, p.visit_type, p.pincode_id, p.area_id, 'PENDING', (SELECT case_number FROM cases WHERE id=$1)||'-'||$3::text, p.id, 'REVISIT', $4, $4`. 15=15, positionally correct; clones CPV+applicant+address+trigger+priority+visit_type+location from parent (`p.*`), status hardcoded PENDING, lineage `parent_task_id=p.id`+`task_origin='REVISIT'`, actor=$4. `WHERE p.id=$2 AND p.case_id=$1` (scope-bound, not trusted). 0-row→`AppError.notFound('TASK_NOT_FOUND')`. ✅

Then `task_assignment_history` INSERT with `previous_assigned_to = parent.assigned_to` (re-read in-tx, $1 caseId-scoped). FK_VIOLATION (bad assignee)→`badRequest('INVALID_ASSIGNEE')` belt-and-braces under the service's pool pre-check.
  - **(c) task_number seq under `uq_case_task_number (case_id, task_number)` — byte-identical to addTasks.** `seq = (count(*) WHERE case_id)+1`, suffix `case_number-seq` via correlated subselect — same pattern as `addTasks` (repo:382-402). Concurrent revisit/add-tasks read the same count → UNIQUE catches → both new writers wrap the whole tx in try/catch mapping `UNIQUE_VIOLATION→conflict('TASK_NUMBER_CONFLICT')` (retryable 409) — the proven TOCTOU handling, present on BOTH. No second open revisit double-bills (service `hasActiveRevisitOf` gate + the per-parent guard).
  - **(d) recomputeCaseStatus reuse — SINGLE writer, NO new status path.** Grep `UPDATE cases SET status` = exactly 2: `recomputeCaseStatus` (repo:114, the rollup) + `finalizeCase` (repo:758, the only COMPLETED-setter, pre-existing). Both revisit+reassign call `recomputeCaseStatus(q, caseId, actorId)` in-tx after the task INSERT+audit. Re-open is the rollup's job (new PENDING/ASSIGNED task → `active>0` → IN_PROGRESS) and verdict-invalidation rides the SAME UPDATE (`verification_outcome=NULL, result_remark=NULL, completed_*=NULL` on any non-COMPLETED move). Lock order preserved (caller writes case_tasks first, then recompute takes `cases FOR UPDATE`). Test proves revisit→case IN_PROGRESS + `verificationOutcome` NULL; reassign→IN_PROGRESS; both leave the parent row untouched (COMPLETED/REVOKED — mobile landmine #2 honoured: never re-activated in place).
  - **(e) verdict-history audit query — CORRECT + cast-safe + deterministic.** `entity_type='case' AND entity_id=$1 AND after_data->>'verificationOutcome' IS NOT NULL` precisely isolates `finalizeCase` rows: finalize writes `entityType:'case'` + `{verificationOutcome, resultRemark}` (repo:777-781); per-task complete/recordResult write `entityType:'case_task'` (repo:713, :815) so they're excluded by the entity_type leg even though they also carry `verificationOutcome` — the filter is doubly-correct. `result`/`remark`/`at`/`actor_name` aliases → camelize (db.ts:16) → `result/remark/at/actorName` exactly matching `CaseVerdictEvent`. **No cast error:** `audit_log.actor_id` is `text`, `entity_id` `text` (mig 0017); `u.id::text = a.actor_id` casts the uuid SIDE (text=text), `entity_id = $1` is text-vs-bound-param (text=text) — neither parses `actor_id` as uuid, so a non-uuid/null actor_id can't throw, just LEFT-JOINs to `actorName=null`. `ORDER BY created_at DESC, id DESC` is fully deterministic — `id` is `bigint GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY` (monotonic insertion order), a MEANINGFUL tiebreak (not a random uuid); backed by `idx_audit_log_entity (entity_type, entity_id, created_at DESC)`. Test asserts newest-first + actorName resolves + length 2 across a revisit cycle. `result` typed `KycResult` is safe (finalize validates via CaseFinalizeSchema → only KYC_RESULTS values land in after_data).
  - **(f) layering / scope / reuse — CLEAN.** Raw SQL repo-only; service does scope (`resolveScope`→`taskAssignmentState`/`caseVisible`, out-of-scope→404 IDOR-safe) + status-guard (revisit: COMPLETED else 409 INVALID_TRANSITION; reassign: REVOKED else 409) + the duplicate-revisit guard + assignee eligibility (`taskRepository.eligibleTaskIdsForAssignee([taskId], …)` — reuses the SAME pool∩hierarchy∩territory path as a normal assign, checking the parent task's OWN `area_id/pincode_id` which the replacement clones → coherent; OFFICE bypasses territory; test: BACKEND_USER not in OFFICE pool→400). Controllers thin (parseUuidParam ×2 → svc → 201). No business logic in controller/SDK. `taskRepository` cross-module import is the established pattern (already used for assign). New perm `task.rework` (BACKEND_USER+MANAGER, SA via grants_all) added to `@crm2/access` AND mig 0054 `role_permissions` — parity. No `task.revoke` (owner correction honoured). SDK leaves: `ReworkTaskSchema`/`ReassignTaskSchema` closed `z.object` (strip unknowns → a stray `version` from the reused FE AssignForm is dropped; `ReassignTaskSchema` ⊇ `AssignTaskInput` + optional reason). FE: REVISITABLE/REASSIGNABLE status-gated buttons (mutually-exclusive open-rows), reuses `AssignForm` for reassign + new `ReasonForm` for revisit, invalidates `['case']`+`['case-verdict-history']`, lineage badge on non-ORIGINAL tasks. The old assign button's `disabled` removed in favour of a `status PENDING|ASSIGNED` render-gate (terminal tasks now route to revisit/reassign) — correct.
  - **(g) migration 0054 — forward-only/idempotent.** `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS` (parent_task_id self-FK `ON DELETE NO ACTION`, task_origin NOT NULL DEFAULT 'ORIGINAL' backfills), `DROP CONSTRAINT IF EXISTS`+re-ADD CHECK `IN ('ORIGINAL','REVISIT')`, partial `idx_case_tasks_parent WHERE parent_task_id IS NOT NULL`, `INSERT … ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING` for the perm. Latest mig (clean tail after 0053). DB auditor owns triple-write apply.
  - **NOTE (cosmetic ×1, non-gating):** service.ts revisit doc-comment "(a live task is reassigned, a REVOKED one reassigned-after-revoke)" slightly conflates — a *live* (PENDING/ASSIGNED/IN_PROGRESS) task isn't "reassigned" by this slice's reassign (that's REVOKED-only); a live one is re-assigned via the normal assign flow. Accurate intent, loose wording. Optional.
  - **INFO:** `completed_by` semantic note from slice-2c-2a still stands (recordResult overloads it) — untouched here. The revisit/reassign actor rides `created_by`/audit, not `completed_by`, so no new overload.
  - **Bottom line:** both INSERT…SELECT writers are column-aligned (15-col revisit, 20-col reassign), param-indexed correctly, clone the parent's location while taking visit/bill/assignee from input (reassign) and bill separately via `task_origin='REVISIT'` while reassign keeps the parent origin; task_number seq + UNIQUE_VIOLATION→409 mirrors the proven addTasks TOCTOU handling; re-open + verdict-invalidation flow through the ONE rollup writer (no second status path); the verdict-history query is entity_type-isolated, cast-safe (text=text both joins), and deterministically ordered on a monotonic identity id; layering/scope/RBAC clean, 4 packages typecheck EXIT 0, 0 suppressions. **Cleared to commit — RUN `cases.api` (5 new tests) green on a live test DB first (sandbox DBs down).** OPEN: slice-5 commission gate must read `task_origin='REVISIT'` for the additional-bill class.

- **2026-06-16 — Slice 2c-2 — device FIELD-PHOTO upload `POST /api/v2/verification-tasks/:id/attachments` (ADR-0034, working tree, uncommitted). VERDICT: PASS.**
  New: `platform/photo.ts` (sharp lazy-import), verification-tasks {routes(multer memoryStorage)/controller/service.uploadAttachments}, cases/repository.ts {insertFieldAttachment, fieldAttachmentsByOperation, FIELD_ATTACH_COLS}, @crm2/sdk sync.ts {DeviceAttachment, DeviceAttachmentUploadResult}, mig 0055, ALLOWED_DEPENDENCIES (multer/sharp/@types/multer), openapi.json. Reviewed adversarially:
  - **Control flow / partial-write — CORRECT, no visible inconsistency.** Per-file try/catch collects `failed[]`; STORAGE `STORAGE_NOT_CONFIGURED` (503) re-thrown (whole request fails — infra, not a per-file fault); 23505 race → re-fetch `fieldAttachmentsByOperation(base)` → return cached set (200, idempotent); idempotency pre-check by base op-id before the loop. storage.put precedes the DB insert per file → a DB failure AFTER a successful put orphans bytes in storage, but NO DB row references them so they're invisible to every reader (all reads `kind='FIELD_PHOTO' AND deleted_at IS NULL`) — acceptable per ADR (no partial-write an API consumer can observe). operation_id `${base}:${i}` + partial-UNIQUE `uq_case_attachments_operation` = at-most-once per (upload,file index).
  - **sharp usage — CORRECT.** `sharp(bytes).rotate()` (no-arg auto-orient from EXIF, then encode WITHOUT `.withMetadata()` → strips EXIF/GPS + drops orientation tag) → `.clone().toBuffer()` keeps source format (stripped evidence) + `.clone().resize(200,200,{fit:'inside',withoutEnlargement:true}).jpeg({quality:80}).toBuffer()` (thumbnail). `.clone()` is the documented multi-output-from-one-input pattern (each clone re-runs the pipeline) — both branches independent; thumbnail in its own try/catch → null on failure, NEVER fails the upload (v1 parity, matches `ProcessedFieldPhoto.thumbnail: Buffer|null`). PERF NOTE (readiness, non-gating): two clones = source decoded twice; fine at 25 MiB/≤20 files, revisit only if hot.
  - **Repo SQL — column/value alignment EXACT (17-col INSERT).** cols `(case_id,task_id,kind,original_name,mime_type,file_size,storage_key,thumbnail_key,sha256,client_sha256,hash_verified,geo_location,photo_type,submission_id,verification_type,operation_id,uploaded_by)` ← `($1,$2,'FIELD_PHOTO',$3,$4,$5,$6,$7,$8,$9,$10,$11::jsonb,$12,$13,$14,$15,$16)`; 16 bound params positionally correct, kind literal, geo `$11::jsonb` with `JSON.stringify(geo)` null-guarded. RETURNING via `FIELD_ATTACH_COLS` aliased (`file_size AS size, storage_key AS url, thumbnail_key AS thumbnail_url, created_at AS uploaded_at`) → `camelize` (db.ts:16) → `{id,originalName,mimeType,size,photoType,geoLocation,url,thumbnailUrl,uploadedAt}` = SDK `DeviceAttachment` EXACTLY. `fieldAttachmentsByOperation` uses `split_part(operation_id,':',1)=$1` + `kind='FIELD_PHOTO' AND deleted_at IS NULL`, deterministic `ORDER BY created_at ASC, operation_id ASC`. `if(!row) throw AppError.internal` guards noUncheckedIndexedAccess.
  - **Layering — CLEAN.** Raw SQL repo-only (2 new methods); multer routes-only (memoryStorage, `limits:{fileSize:MAX_ATTACHMENT_BYTES,files:20}`, error→`badRequest('UPLOAD_REJECTED')` 400); sharp platform/photo-only (lazy `await import('sharp')`); service transport-agnostic via `UploadedPhoto{buffer,originalName,size}` (decoupled from multer types). `detectAttachment` REUSED (image-only gate: `!detected || !type.startsWith('image/')` → 400 per-file). storage key built from `caseId/taskId/randomUUID().ext` — `originalName` NEVER enters the key (no path-traversal; only sliced to 255 for the stored display name). Controller thin: casts `req.files` to a structural `{buffer,originalname,size}[]` (NOT `any`), maps to `UploadedPhoto`, reads `Idempotency-Key` header / `operationId` field. Response = locked `{success,message,data}` envelope (device shape, isolated to this endpoint per ADR), NOT the v2 raw-JSON convention.
  - **multer typing — no `any`/suppressions.** `parseFieldPhotos` wraps `photoUpload.array('files',20)` with `(err:unknown)` → 400; `@types/multer` added. Diff grep: 0 `eslint-disable`/`ts-ignore`/`ts-expect-error`/`: any`/`as any`/`console.*` (logger.warn on hash-mismatch only, allowed). hash: `client_sha256` `^[0-9a-f]{64}$` validated (else null), `hash_verified=clientSha===sha256(received)`, mismatch logged never rejected (rollout safety, ADR).
  - **Gate:** api + sdk `tsc --noEmit` EXIT 0. `verification-tasks.api.test.ts` 7/7 PASS on live test DB (:5433, after applying 0055) incl 2 new ADR-0034 tests (happy-path: 200 {success,data}, FIELD_PHOTO row, server evidence sha256, hash_verified=true, op-id `op-PH-1:0`, replay → 200 cached + NO second row; guards: non-assignee→404, missing idem-key→400, non-image PDF→200 success=false+failed[1]). service.ts coverage 96%. openapi.json regenerated with the new path (drift gate satisfied).
  - **SHOULD-FIX (non-gating ×2):** (1) ADR-0034 §Decision + ALLOWED_DEPENDENCIES sharp row both say "lazy-imported in `platform/image`", but the code lives in `platform/photo.ts` (`platform/image.ts` already exists for user avatars — distinct). Doc/code path drift; fix the two doc refs to `platform/photo`. (2) On an idempotency REPLAY, the echoed `data.verificationType`/`submissionId` come from the CURRENT request's fields, not the originally-stored rows — so a replay that omits those fields echoes `null` while the first delivery echoed the real values. The `attachments[]` array (authoritative) is correct either way; cosmetic for the device. Optional: source the two echo fields from the cached rows on replay.

- **2026-06-16 — Backend/office task REVOKE + repo rename `revokeTaskByDevice→revokeTaskInPlace` (ADR-0033 correction, working tree, uncommitted). VERDICT: PASS.**
  NOTE ON SCOPE: the audit prompt described TWO features (A device field-photo upload + B backend revoke), but the working tree (`git status`) contains ONLY feature B — the field-photo slice (A) is the PRIOR committed slice already cleared in the entry above. Audited the actual uncommitted diff: cases revoke endpoint + the shared-method rename + mig 0056 + `task.revoke` perm + SDK + tests.
  - **Rename — BOTH callers updated, ZERO dangling refs.** `grep revokeTaskByDevice` (all `*.ts`) = 0; `revokeTaskInPlace` = exactly 3 (repo def + device caller `verification-tasks/service.ts:112` + new office caller `cases/service.ts:361`). Both pass `(caseId, taskId, actorId, reason)` — identical 4-arg shape; device resolves `caseId` via `ownedCaseId(taskId, actor)` (ownership), office via the scope-guard. No compile breakage (api `tsc --noEmit` EXIT 0).
  - **Transition UNCHANGED by the rename (the load-bearing invariant).** repo.ts:1115 — `UPDATE … SET status='REVOKED', remark=$4, version=version+1 … WHERE id=$1 AND case_id=$2 AND status IN ('ASSIGNED','IN_PROGRESS') RETURNING id`; 0 rows → re-SELECT → `notFound('TASK_NOT_FOUND')` if gone, `return cur` if already REVOKED (idempotent), else `conflict('INVALID_TRANSITION')` (COMPLETED/PENDING → 409). `appendAudit` + `recomputeCaseStatus` inside `withTransaction`. Byte-identical to the pre-rename device behavior; only the doc-comment + the internal error string (`'device revoke'→'revoke'`) changed. CORRECT.
  - **Sharing ONE repo method across device(ownership) + office(scope) — CLEAN.** The repo method is auth-agnostic: it takes a pre-resolved `(caseId, actorId)` and performs the SQL transition only. Each SERVICE owns its own gate BEFORE calling: device `verificationTaskService.revoke` → `ownedCaseId(taskId, actor)` (ownership-bound); office `caseService.revokeTask` → `taskAssignmentState(caseId, taskId, await resolveScope(actor))` → null ⇒ `notFound` (scope-bound, IDOR-safe 404). This is the EXACT pattern the sibling revisit/reassign services already use (service.ts:296/309) — faithful reuse, correct separation (auth in service, transition in repo). The DB transition being identical while auth differs is the right factoring; no leak of one caller's auth model into the other.
  - **Idempotency note (re: prompt's operation_id/23505-race question):** that question pertains to feature A (field-attachment insert), NOT in this diff. This revoke path has its own idempotency = re-revoke returns the cached REVOKED row (no OCC version sent by caller; the WHERE-status guard + re-SELECT handles concurrency). Sound.
  - **Layering — CLEAN.** Raw SQL stays in repo; controller `revokeTask` is thin (parse 2 uuid params → `svc.revokeTask(…, actor(req))` → `res.json`, std try/catch→next), byte-matching the adjacent revisit/reassign controllers; multipart N/A. `svc`/`parseUuidParam`/`actor` all in scope.
  - **Permission parity DB↔code — MATCHED.** mig 0056 grants `task.revoke` to BACKEND_USER+MANAGER `ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING`; `@crm2/access` ROLE_PERMISSIONS gives it to MANAGER (L85)+BACKEND_USER (L108)+SUPER_ADMIN (`Object.values`, grants_all); KYC_VERIFIER/FIELD_AGENT lack it. `PERMISSION_META['task.revoke']` added. Route gated `authorize(PERMISSIONS.TASK_REVOKE)`. Fully-specified route `/:id/tasks/:taskId/revoke` (no param-capture ambiguity; `GET /:id` registered after). ADR-0033 amended with a dated "Correction" superseding the earlier "backend never revokes" cut.
  - **Contract/SDK:** `RevokeTaskSchema = {reason: trim().min(1).max(MAX_REMARK=2000)}` (== device `RevokeSchema` MAX_REASON=2000 → no divergence); `cases.revokeTask(caseId,taskId,input)→CaseTaskView`; openapi.json regenerated with the new path. No `any`/suppressions/`console.*` in diff. api+access+sdk `tsc --noEmit` all EXIT 0.
