- **2026-06-16 — Sync down-sync delta arrays + per-task execution fields (slice 2c-2 tail, ADR-0035, mig 0057, working tree, uncommitted). VERDICT: PASS.**
  Audited the actual `git diff` (sync repo `revokedAssignmentIdsForUser` + `SyncTaskRow.startedAt/completedAt`; service `toMobileTask` inProgressAt/completedAt + offset-0-only delta; mig 0057 index; ADR-0035; +5 tests). Reviewed adversarially against the lifecycle writers and the locked ADR-0012 wire.
  - **Delta query correctness — SOUND on every branch.** `SELECT DISTINCT h.task_id FROM task_assignment_history h JOIN case_tasks ct WHERE h.previous_assigned_to=$1 AND h.created_at>$2 AND ct.assigned_to IS DISTINCT FROM $1`. (a) `IS DISTINCT FROM` is the correct NULL-safe operator: UNASSIGNED → `ct.assigned_to=NULL` → `NULL IS DISTINCT FROM uuid` = TRUE → purged (a plain `<>` would have been NULL→excluded, the classic bug — avoided). (b) REASSIGNED-away → `ct.assigned_to=fa2` → TRUE → purged. (c) reassigned-THEN-back → `ct.assigned_to=$1` → FALSE → correctly EXCLUDED (flows via `cases` as still-mine; ADR §1). (d) `DISTINCT` dedupes multiple history rows per task (assign→reassign→reassign churn) to one UUID. (e) REVOKED-but-still-mine keeps `assigned_to=me` → FALSE → excluded → reaches device via `cases`+`isRevoked` (the keep-the-row path, NOT a purge) — verified the revoke UPDATE (cases/repo.ts:1115) keeps the assignee, and the dedicated test asserts `revokedAssignmentIds=[]` + `cases[0].isRevoked=true`.
  - **History writers feed it correctly (cross-checked).** Both REASSIGN (cases/repo.ts:631, `previous_assigned_to = updated.previousAssignedTo`) and UNASSIGN (repo.ts:682, `'UNASSIGNED', NULL, $3=prev`) write `previous_assigned_to` IN THE SAME tx as the `case_tasks` UPDATE — so the history `created_at` and the `case_tasks.updated_at` move together; no skew between the cases-watermark and the delta-watermark.
  - **Watermark cutoff consistency — EXACT.** ONE `cutoff: Date` from `download()` feeds both `downloadForUser` (`COALESCE(ct.updated_at, cs.updated_at) > $2`) and `revokedAssignmentIdsForUser` (`h.created_at > $2`); both serialize via the same `.toISOString()`, both STRICT `>`. No watermark drift between the two queries.
  - **offset-0-only — justified + tested.** `offset === 0 ? await repo.revokedAssignmentIdsForUser(...) : []`. Device cycles from offset 0 each sync (persists watermark only after a full cycle) and the device-side purge is idempotent + `recentlyCleaned`-deduped, so per-page repetition of the unbounded-history scan is pure waste. ADR §5 + the inline doc state this; the CARRY (revisit if the device ever resumes from offset>0) is correctly flagged. The `0` literal is the idiomatic boundary (lint exempt) — not a magic number.
  - **Execution fields — exactOptionalProps-safe, contract-safe.** `...(r.startedAt ? { inProgressAt: iso(r.startedAt) } : {})` / completedAt — conditional spreads never assign `undefined` (TS-strict honored); SDK `MobileSyncTask` already declares `inProgressAt?/completedAt?/formData?` optional (sync.ts:41/53/61) → wire byte-compat, no SDK/OpenAPI change. `started_at = COALESCE(started_at, now())` (idempotent start) + `completed_at = now()` on complete ⇒ `completedAt >= inProgressAt` holds; test asserts `>=` (tolerant of equal). `formData` correctly NOT emitted (ADR §4: device has no conflict-resolution on inbound formData → would blind-overwrite the local draft; test asserts `formData` undefined). `isSaved` left device-owned.
  - **Layering / SoC — CLEAN.** Raw SQL stays in the repo (new method is a sync READ concern → belongs in the sync repo, not a cross-feature reach: it reads `task_assignment_history`+`case_tasks`, both within the sync read-model's natural surface); service orchestrates + maps; controller untouched. No `any`/suppressions/`console.*` in the diff; `eslint` + api `tsc --noEmit` both EXIT 0.
  - **Index — correct + justified.** mig 0057 `idx_task_assignment_history_prev (previous_assigned_to, created_at)` exactly serves the new predicate; the pre-existing `(task_id, created_at DESC)` (mig 0036) does not. Forward-only, idempotent, BEGIN/COMMIT, header rationale present — idiom-faithful to prior migs. (DB auditor owns triple-write apply.)
  - **FLAG (non-gating, by-design TOCTOU window):** the cases page and the delta set are TWO separate queries (not one snapshot tx). A reassign-away landing BETWEEN them yields the task in the cases page (stale, read pre-reassign) but NOT yet in `revokedAssignmentIds` (read post-reassign) → device upserts the orphan this cycle, purges it next cycle. Self-healing, one-cycle lag, never the dangerous reverse (in-revoked + in-cases-as-mine is impossible — both filter on CURRENT `assigned_to`, and the delta runs AFTER the page, so any task in the delta has already left the page). ADR §1's "disjoint by construction" is true at each query's snapshot but the two snapshots aren't atomic; acceptable for an eventually-consistent down-sync, worth noting. No fix required.
  - **Tests — cover the matrix.** reassign-away (old assignee: cases=[] + revoked=[taskId]; new assignee: cases=1 + revoked=[]); revoked-still-mine (revoked=[] + isRevoked=true); start→complete (inProgressAt/completedAt strings, ordering, formData absent); locked-envelope-shape (exact `{success,message,data}` keys, NOT Paginated `items/total/page`); offset-0-only (offset=0→[taskId], offset=1→[]). DB-gated (`describe.skipIf(!RUN)`) like the suite — not run here (no DATABASE_URL); typecheck+lint clean.
  - **Bottom line:** delta query is correct on all four assignment-transition branches (the `IS DISTINCT FROM` NULL-safety is the load-bearing detail and it is right), watermark is one cutoff shared by both queries with no drift, offset-0 short-circuit is justified+tested, execution fields are exactOptionalProps/contract-safe with `formData` correctly withheld, the new method belongs in the sync repo, mig 0057 backs the exact predicate, 0 suppressions, typecheck+lint EXIT 0. **Cleared to commit.** One non-gating FLAG = the two-query (non-atomic) page-vs-delta TOCTOU window (self-healing, one-cycle lag, safe direction only). Carry: DB auditor owns mig 0057 apply (dev:54329 + test:5433); DB-gated tests not executed in this audit (no DATABASE_URL).

- **2026-06-16 — Billing slice 5a — `commission_rates` master-data module (mig 0058 + repo/service/controller/routes + SDK + tests, UNCOMMITTED). VERDICT: PASS.**
  ADR-0036's CONFIG foundation for unified per-case Billing & Commission: a per-user `(user, rate_type,
  client[nullable=universal]) → amount` table, deliberately mirroring `rates`. Audited adversarially against
  the `rates` SoT (modules/rates/* + sdk/rates.ts) + ADR-0036:
  - **Effective-dated revise — CORRECT, byte-faithful to rates.** `withTransaction` → `SELECT … FOR UPDATE`
    (row lock) → version-guard (`cur.version !== expected → AppError.stale(cur)`) → `!isActive → 409
    COMMISSION_RATE_NOT_ACTIVE` → end-date the current row FIRST (`effective_to = COALESCE($2,now())`,
    `version+1`) → INSERT new dated row. Ordering is the load-bearing detail and it is right: the old row is
    end-dated *before* the new open-ended row is inserted, so within the tx the active periods never overlap.
  - **No-overlap EXCLUDE — CORRECT + needs btree_gist (present).** `EXCLUDE USING gist (user_id WITH =,
    rate_type WITH =, (COALESCE(client_id,-1)) WITH =, tstzrange(effective_from, COALESCE(effective_to,
    'infinity'),'[)') WITH &&) WHERE (is_active)` — identical idiom to `rates_no_overlap` (0012/0013). The
    equality columns (uuid/varchar/int) require **btree_gist** for GiST equality opclasses; `CREATE EXTENSION
    IF NOT EXISTS btree_gist` is in 0058 (and already in 0012) → available. COALESCE(client_id,-1) folds
    universal(NULL) into a sentinel so a universal row and a client-scoped row for the same user+rate_type do
    NOT collide (different sentinel vs real id) — exactly the "most-specific-wins coexistence" the resolver
    relies on (test confirms universal ₹50 + client ₹80 coexist). `[)` half-open + `infinity` upper bound =
    abutting ranges (old.effective_to == new.effective_from) touch-but-don't-overlap → revise never trips the
    constraint. **Revise can NEITHER violate the EXCLUDE nor deadlock:** the partial predicate is `WHERE
    is_active` and revise leaves both rows active but with disjoint `[)` periods; `FOR UPDATE` serializes
    concurrent revisers of the same id (second waits, re-reads bumped version → STALE 409), and there is no
    second-row lock acquired in reverse order anywhere → no lock-ordering cycle.
  - **resolveAmount — sound.** `WHERE user_id=$1 AND rate_type=$2 AND is_active AND (client_id IS NULL OR
    client_id=$3) AND effective_from<=now() AND (effective_to IS NULL OR effective_to>now()) ORDER BY
    client_id DESC NULLS LAST LIMIT 1`. Most-specific-client-wins via `DESC NULLS LAST` (a real client_id
    sorts before NULL=universal). **DB `now()` is the right temporal anchor** (not a host `Date`): skew-proof,
    single clock, and CONSISTENT with the list view's current-rows predicate (`effective_to IS NULL OR
    effective_to > now()`) — identical `now()` choice as rates.list. Returns `null` when unconfigured =
    "unset, not failure" per ADR §2 (test: unknown rate_type → null). The resolve index
    `(user_id, rate_type, client_id) WHERE is_active` backs the predicate; mirrors `idx_rates_resolve`.
  - **Pattern parity (faithful to the clients/rates list SoT).** `service.list` = `resolvePage(raw,
    CR_PAGE_SPEC)` + domain-filter extract (userId string-guard, clientId via `toPosInt`, tri-state `active`,
    `history` 'true'/undefined) + `resolveFilters` + `repo.list({...})` + `buildPage`. Shared `CR_FROM`
    (commission_rates cr JOIN users u LEFT JOIN clients c) reused by BOTH COUNT and items → search predicate
    on joined cols (u.name/u.email/c.name/c.code/cr.rate_type) is valid in the COUNT WHERE; INNER users +
    LEFT clients are FK→PK ≤1-row joins → no COUNT/items row-count drift. ORDER BY `${o.sortColumn}` is
    whitelisted via `CR_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap` (8 cols, all real) + `cr.id` tiebreak; `history` default
    (current-rows-only) applied identically to COUNT + items. `amount::float8` cast (numeric→JS number),
    asserted by the test (`typeof amount === 'number'`).
  - **Correct OMISSIONS vs rates.** No `rate_history` table / `history()` method / history INSERTs (rates keeps
    a domain history table; commission self-historizes via effective-dating, no `rate_history` analog exists —
    ADR §3) — so `revise`/`setActive`/`create` correctly DON'T wrap extra history writes, and `setActive` is a
    single autocommit `UPDATE` (no `withTransaction` needed since there's no second write — divergence from
    rates.setActive is justified, not a regression). No `import.ts` / export route / `/import-template` /
    `bulk-*` / `PUT /:id` (UpdateRate legacy flat edit) — all rates extras the ADR doesn't ask for. SDK omits
    `RateHistory`/`UpdateRateSchema`. money max correctly tracks the column: rates `numeric(10,2)`→
    `max(99999999.99)`, commission `numeric(12,2)`→`max(9999999999.99)`.
  - **RBAC — no new permission (ADR §3).** Reads `page.masterdata` (MASTERDATA_VIEW), writes `masterdata.manage`
    (MASTERDATA_MANAGE) — both exist in @crm2/access; same authority as rates. Test proves FIELD_AGENT → 403 on
    both read + write. Route order safe (`/:id/{revise,activate,deactivate}` two-segment, no static-path
    collision). `parseId` rejects non-positive-int → 400.
  - **Contract/SDK — clean leaf.** zod-only `commissionRates.ts`; `client.ts` adds a `commissionRates` group
    mirroring `rates` (list via `pageQueryToParams`→`Paginated<CommissionRateView>`, create/revise/activate/
    deactivate carry `version` for OCC); `index.ts` re-export added; `client.test.ts` exercises all 5 calls +
    asserts the `/api/v2/commission-rates` URL. `app.ts` mounts the router beside rates.
  - **Hygiene.** 0 `any`/suppressions/`console.*`/magic-numbers in any new file (`FK_VIOLATION`/
    `EXCLUSION_VIOLATION` are named consts; `-1` sentinel lives only in SQL mirroring rates). SDK + API
    `tsc --noEmit` both EXIT 0. SDK contract test green. The api suite is `describe.skipIf(!RUN)` (DB-gated) —
    NOT executed here (no DATABASE_URL in this env), consistent with the rates suite; `migrate()` globs+sorts
    all `db/v2/migrations/*.sql` so 0058 is auto-picked. The suite encodes the right matrix (201+numeric+
    joined-view, overlap→409 / different rate_type allowed, revise end-dates+new-id / stale→409, deactivate→
    resolver-drop+reactivate, resolveAmount client-wins/fallback/null, RBAC 403×2, bad-uuid→400).
  - **SHOULD-FIX (none blocking).** NOTE: `status` sort on `cr.is_active` orders positionally (bool) — valid,
    expected. NOTE: live HTTP E2E is the owner's stated proof for 5a (ADR §Consequences, backend-only); the
    DB-gated suite was not run in this read-only audit — Carry to whoever applies mig 0058 (DB auditor owns
    triple-write apply dev+test+prod-pending) to run the suite against a live DB before/with commit.
  - **Bottom line:** revise ordering + EXCLUDE + FOR UPDATE + OCC compose correctly (no overlap-violation, no
    deadlock possible); resolver is most-specific-wins + active + DB-`now()`-temporal, skew-proof and
    consistent with the list; COALESCE(-1) sentinel + btree_gist are correct and the extension is present;
    every rates extra (history/import/export/bulk/PUT) is correctly OMITTED with justification; raw SQL stays
    in the repo, layering intact, 0 suppressions, typecheck EXIT 0. **PASS — cleared to commit** (run the
    DB-gated api suite against a live DB as part of the apply). No FLAG, no BLOCK.

- **2026-06-16 — Billing slice 5b — per-case Billing & Commission read-model (ADR-0036, working tree, UNCOMMITTED). VERDICT: PASS.**
  New `modules/billing/{repository,service,controller,routes}.ts` + `__tests__/billing.api.test.ts`, SDK leaf
  `packages/sdk/src/billing.ts` (+ `client.ts` `billing.{cases,caseTasks,export}` + index export), `app.ts` mount,
  `permissions.ts` `BILLING_VIEW` + migration `0059_billing_view_perm.sql`. Read-only money view: per COMPLETED
  task a client bill (rates engine) + agent commission (commission_rates), both DERIVED, no billed-state.
  Audited adversarially against the brief's six axes:
  - **(1) Chained-LATERAL correctness — CONFIRMED LEGAL & EXACT.** `COMMISSION_LATERAL` references `rt.rate_type`
    from `RATE_LATERAL`; SQL lateral scoping makes a later `LEFT JOIN LATERAL` see the output columns of an
    earlier one in the same FROM, so `cmr.rate_type = rt.rate_type` is valid *because* the rate lateral is
    declared first (order is load-bearing — the repo comment says so and it's true). Both laterals are `LIMIT 1`
    → at most one row each → no row multiplication; `LEFT JOIN … ON true` keeps the driving `case_tasks ct` row
    even when a lateral yields nothing (rt/com → NULL, not dropped). So `count(*)` per group = #completed tasks
    and `SUM(rt.bill_amount)`/`SUM(com.commission_amount)` are exact per-task sums. The RATE_LATERAL ladder is
    byte-faithful to `cases/repository.ts` TASK_VIEW_COLS (task area>task pincode>case area>case pincode>
    location-less>any, temporal, active) — same six ORDER BY legs; the only delta is selecting `r.amount` too
    (cases selects rate_type only) and materializing as LATERAL vs scalar subselect — the correct adaptation
    since billing needs the amount. NULLS-LAST on the IS NULL leg is cosmetic (bool DESC already orders
    true-first); ordering identical.
  - **(2) GROUP BY + ORDER-BY-by-aggregate-alias — CORRECT in PG.** `ORDER BY ${o.sortColumn} ${o.sortOrder},
    cs.id ${o.sortOrder}`: PG resolves an ORDER BY identifier to a SELECT output column name, so the aggregate
    aliases `bill_total`/`commission_total`/`completed_task_count`/`last_completed_at` are valid sort targets;
    the non-aggregate sort cols (`cs.case_number`/`cl.name`/`p.name`/`cs.status`) are all in GROUP BY. `cs.id`
    tiebreak is in GROUP BY → valid, and is the unique PK so the order is total/stable for pagination. sortColumn
    is whitelisted via `BILLING_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap` through `resolvePage` (unknown/injection → default
    `lastCompletedAt`), so the interpolation is safe.
  - **(3) count(DISTINCT cs.id) matches grouped-row count — CORRECT.** The page query GROUPs BY cs.id (+functional
    deps), so #grouped rows = #distinct cs.id satisfying the same WHERE; COUNT reuses the IDENTICAL `clause`
    +`params` and the same `CASES_FROM` (so the laterals are present but irrelevant to a DISTINCT-on-cs.id count
    — `count(DISTINCT cs.id)` is immune to the 1:1 lateral fan-in anyway). No drift between count and page.
  - **(3-adversarial) the null-commission drop trap — does NOT occur.** A case whose only completed task has no
    commission rate: `COMMISSION_LATERAL` returns 0 rows → `LEFT JOIN…ON true` keeps the task row with
    `com.commission_amount = NULL` → `COALESCE(SUM(com.commission_amount),0)` → `commissionTotal = 0`, the case
    STAYS in the list (gate is `ct.status='COMPLETED'`, not commission presence). Same protection on `bill_total`.
    The test `eligibility = ANY completed task; commission null…` proves exactly this (commissionTotal 0,
    billTotal 100, row present; line commissionAmount NULL un-coalesced as intended). COALESCE placement correct.
  - **(4) reuse-vs-fork the ladder — module-local copy is the RIGHT boundary call.** Both the rate ladder and
    `caseScopePredicate` are duplicated locally rather than imported from cases/dashboard. This matches the
    established v2 convention (dashboard already duplicates caseScopePredicate + SLA windows; ENGINEERING
    layering forbids cross-feature internal imports, dependency-cruiser-enforced). `caseScopePredicate` here is
    byte-identical to `dashboard/repository.ts:41`. Extracting a shared rates-ladder helper would create a
    cross-module SQL-fragment dependency with no current second consumer beyond cases — premature. Correct to
    keep local; the DON'T-REGRESS is that the two ladders must stay in lockstep (carry below).
  - **(5) raw-SQL/params/no-magic/exactOptionalProps — CLEAN.** Raw SQL only in the repository; controller→service
    →repository layering intact (controller never touches repo). Params fully bound: the `add()` helper pushes
    then rewrites `$?`→`$N`; search/ids/filterClauses/scopePred all push onto the SAME `params` and `params.length`
    is captured AFTER scope-append so `LIMIT $${len+1} OFFSET $${len+2}` with `[...params,limit,offset]` indexes
    correctly. No `any`/`eslint-disable`/`ts-*`/`console.*` (grep clean); no magic numbers (the only literals are
    the `+1/+2` bind offsets — standard pattern). exactOptionalProps-safe conditional spreads for
    clientId/completedFrom/completedTo/search/ids into both repo opts and echoed `filters`. tsc EXIT 0 across
    api + sdk + access.
  - **(6) caseVisible scope-guard — 404 IDOR-safe, CONFIRMED.** `caseTasks` service calls `repo.caseVisible`
    (same `caseScopePredicate` over `cases cs`); false → `AppError.notFound('CASE_NOT_FOUND')`. Absent AND
    out-of-scope both → 404 (no existence leak). Controller `parseCaseId` UUID-regex-guards before the DB →
    non-uuid is 400 not a 500 (`WHERE cs.id=$1` on a uuid col can't blow up). Test asserts BE 404 on absent,
    400 on non-uuid, 200 on real. The `caseTasks` repo read is itself UNGUARDED by design — the service is the
    sole caller and guards first (documented "caller guards visibility"); acceptable since it's not route-mounted.
  - **Permission wiring parity:** `BILLING_VIEW` granted MANAGER+BACKEND_USER in code (`ROLE_PERMISSIONS`) AND
    migration 0059 — exact match; TEAM_LEADER correctly excluded; SUPER_ADMIN via grants_all. routes gate list+
    lines on `BILLING_VIEW`, export on `DATA_EXPORT` (mirrors platform export standard; same web roles hold it).
    Test asserts BE 200 / TL 403 / FIELD_AGENT 403. SDK `billing.export('billing/cases')` follows the reqBlob
    convention; client.test count 138→140 + url assertions added. Migration 0058/0059 sequential, tail of chain.
  - SHOULD-FIX (none blocking). NOTE: export gate (`data.export`) differs from the read gate (`billing.view`) —
    intentional per the export standard, flagged for awareness only. **CARRY:** the billing RATE_LATERAL and
    `cases` TASK_VIEW_COLS rate ladder are duplicated — any change to the rates resolution precedence MUST be
    applied to BOTH (grep `r.location_id = ct.area_id` finds both sites). Same lockstep applies to the local
    `caseScopePredicate` copies (billing + dashboard). **PASS — cleared to commit** (run the DB-gated billing
    api suite against a live DB as part of the apply; DB-apply of 0059 owned by the DB ledger). No FLAG, no BLOCK.

- **2026-06-16 — Billing slice 5c — FE: `BillingPage` + `CommissionRatesPage` (ADR-0036, working tree, UNCOMMITTED). VERDICT: PASS.**
  Two new FE pages over the 5a/5b backends: `features/billing/BillingPage.tsx` (read-only per-case bill+commission
  DataGrid w/ lazy per-case expand) + `features/commissionRates/CommissionRatesPage.tsx` (SA-only commission-rate
  config w/ create/revise dialog + bulk activate/deactivate) + `App.tsx` routes (`/billing`, `/admin/commission-rates`)
  + `Layout.tsx` nav (2 items) + e2e `a11y.spec.ts`/`viewport.spec.ts` (both pages registered). `web-v2 typecheck` EXIT 0.
  Audited adversarially on the brief's six axes:
  - **(1) Hooks rules — NO conditional-hook bug.** Every hook runs unconditionally BEFORE the permission early-return.
    `BillingPage`: useAuth→useState(clientId)→useQuery(client-options)→useMemo(columns), THEN `if(!has('billing.view'))
    return`. `CommissionRatesPage`: useAuth→useState(dialog)→useMemo(columns), THEN `if(!has('masterdata.manage'))
    return`. `CommissionRateDialog` (useState×6 / useQuery×3 [user-options/rate-types/client-options] / useMutation /
    useQueryClient) and `BillingCaseLines` (single useQuery) are SEPARATE components — their hooks all precede their
    returns; they mount/unmount at real component boundaries (dialog conditional render, accordion `renderExpanded`),
    which is correct React, not a conditional hook. CONFIRMED clean.
  - **(2) react-query — cache-coherent, no stale-closure.** Lazy per-case lines key on `['billing-case-tasks', caseId]`
    (per-row isolation, correct). Revise/create mutation `invalidateQueries(['commission-rates'])` matches the DataGrid
    `queryKey="commission-rates"` root → list refetches post-write. OCC `version` threaded ONLY on revise
    (`row!.version` + `row!.id`); create omits version (insert path). Shared `['client-options']` key reused across both
    pages + dialog — coherent, fine. No stale closure: `columns` useMemo deps `[]` close only over stable `setDialog`;
    `clientId` is read fresh each render via the DataGrid `filters` prop, NOT captured in a memo. `isStale` (409 +
    `code==='STALE_UPDATE'`) is byte-identical to the LocationsPage convention and matches `AppError.stale`'s wire
    shape (`{error:'STALE_UPDATE'}` → sdk `ApiError.code`).
  - **(3) DataGrid integration — faithful to RateManagementPage/CpvPage SoT.** Every prop matches the DataGrid contract
    (columns/queryKey/rowId/defaultSort[+Order]/searchPlaceholder/filters/fetchPage/dateFilters/exportFn/renderExpanded/
    toolbar/selectable/bulkActions/`hideable:false` on actions col). `filters={{clientId: clientId||undefined}}` flattens
    via `pageQueryToParams` (pagination.ts:44 iterates `q.filters`) → `clientId=` ON THE WIRE; "All clients" → undefined
    → param dropped. Export reuses the SAME merged filters via `exportQueryToParams`→`pageQueryToParams`. Loop closed.
  - **(4) types — clean, zero `any`/suppressions.** All from `@crm2/sdk` (BillingCaseRow/BillingTaskLine/CommissionRate/
    CommissionRateView/Option/UserOption/RateType/PageQuery/Paginated/ExportRequest). grep for `any`/eslint-disable/
    ts-ignore/ts-expect-error/console.* = 0 hits in both files. typecheck EXIT 0.
  - **(5) create-vs-revise branching — sound.** `isRevise=!!row` DISABLES the identity selects (User/RateType/Client)
    and POSTs only `{amount, effectiveFrom, version}`→`/:id/revise`; create POSTs full body w/ `clientId: clientId?
    Number:null` (universal=null). `valid` gate differs correctly (revise=amount only; create=user+rateType+amount).
  - **(6) money()/formatDateTime reuse, no magic numbers.** `formatDateTime`/`toDateInput`/`toIsoDate` reused from
    `lib/format`; local `money()` helpers (one nullable→'—', one non-null) match the slice's display idiom. Sole named
    const `HTTP_CONFLICT=409`; only other literals are `toFixed(2)` (currency, conventional) — no offending magic numbers.
  - **Nav/perm mirror — CORRECT.** Both Layout nav perms equal their page read-endpoint perms: `billing.view` (BE
    `billingRoutes` list gates `billing.view`) and `masterdata.manage` (BE `commissionRateRoutes` list gates
    `MASTERDATA_MANAGE`, deliberately NOT the broader `page.masterdata` — comp data, SA-only audience). The page-level
    `has()` guard matches the nav perm matches the BE read gate — three-way consistent. e2e viewport flags
    CommissionRates `primary:/New/` (has + New button), Billing without (no primary CTA) — accurate.
  - SHOULD-FIX (none blocking). NOTE: the export gate inconsistency flagged in 5b is BACKEND-side and unchanged here;
    FE export button simply calls the endpoint. **PASS — cleared to commit.** No FLAG, no BLOCK.

### 2026-06-16 — ADR-0036 Slice 5d (Pipeline billable/commissionable VIEW + platform/billing/laterals.ts) — VERDICT: BLOCK
Working tree, uncommitted. Pipeline TaskView gains `billable`/`billAmount`/`commissionAmount` + TaskStats.`commissionable`; FE adds a Commissionable bucket + 2 ₹ columns; rate/commission LATERALs extracted to `apps/api/src/platform/billing/laterals.ts` (shared by billing + tasks repos). Audited adversarially.
- **🛑 BLOCK — `assignedTo` export filter DROPPED (incidental scope regression).** `modules/tasks/service.ts:184-193` (`exportData` → `repo.list`): the diff hunk REMOVED `...(d.assignedTo !== undefined ? { assignedTo: d.assignedTo } : {})` and replaced that line with the new `commissionable`/`billing` spreads. Net: **export of the Pipeline filtered by assignee (`?assignedTo=<uuid>`) now ignores the filter and exports ALL assignees' rows.** `list` and `stats` still pass `assignedTo` correctly — only `exportData` lost it. Violates the B-13 contract comment one line above ("re-runs the SAME scoped list query") and Karpathy rule 3 (surgical — an unrelated filter was collaterally deleted while inserting billing spreads). No test covers assignedTo-as-export-filter (the 18 new tests don't), which is why the gate stayed green. **FIX:** re-add the `assignedTo` spread to the `exportData` `repo.list({...})` call alongside the billing spreads.
- **Lateral extraction — byte-faithful & correct home.** `platform/billing/laterals.ts` RATE_LATERAL is byte-identical to the prior `billing/repository.ts` const (diffed: only an added doc-comment between the two consts); COMMISSION_LATERAL identical (the diff's `-` lines match). `platform/billing/` is the right home (both billing and tasks are leaf modules; a tasks→billing cross-module import would violate the no-cross-feature-internals rule, platform/ is the sanctioned shared layer). The FROM-contract is documented (consumer supplies `cs`/`ct`; `com` must follow `rt`). The scope predicate stays copied per-module by design — correct, it's module-visibility policy, not rate config.
- **SQL alias-without-lateral injection surface — CLOSED.** The load-bearing guard `commissionable = billing && !!o.commissionable` (repository.ts list) means the WHERE `com.commission_amount IS NOT NULL` predicate can NEVER be emitted unless `billing` is also true, which forces `TASK_FROM_BILLING` into BOTH the COUNT (`countFrom`) and SELECT (`selectFrom`) FROM. Traced all 3 actor classes (non-billing / billing-no-filter / billing+commissionable): no path reaches `rt.`/`com.` without the laterals in FROM. sortMap has NO billing entries and filterMap columns are all `ct./cs./cl./vu./au./pa.` → user-supplied `sortBy`/column-filters can never inject a lateral alias into ORDER BY or WHERE. `stats` commissionable block builds its own `cParams`/`cClause` over `TASK_FROM_BILLING`, gated on `o.billing`. No SQL-error / injection surface.
- **COUNT / perf split correct.** `list` COUNT lateral-free unless commissionable active (then both laterals in FROM, both LIMIT 1 → 1:1 so `count(*)` exact). `stats` keeps ONE lateral-free aggregate over TASK_FROM for the existing cheap status/SLA buckets (no regression) + isolates the commissionable count in a second query PRE-FILTERED to COMPLETED so the lateral runs only over completed rows. Amount columns nulled (`NULL::float8`) + laterals skipped for non-billing actors → also cheaper.
- **RBAC / comp-data gating sound.** `canViewBilling` = grantsAll || `BILLING_VIEW` (controller, single SoT); threaded controller→service→repo. Non-holders: amounts null, laterals skipped, commissionable filter inert (ignored in service AND re-normalised in repo — defence in depth), Commissionable bucket → 0. FE only HIDES columns/bucket (server already nulls). 5b money-export rule honoured: `taskExportColumns(canViewBilling)` pushes the ₹ columns only for holders.
- **`billable` correctly ungated** = `(ct.status='COMPLETED')`, status-derived/non-sensitive, always present. SDK contract leaf well-documented (derived-at-read, no persisted billed-state). FE `money()` null→'—'. `useMemo` dep correctly bumped to `[canViewBilling]`.
- **No `any`/suppressions/`console.*`** in additions (grep clean). TS-strict conditional spreads throughout.
- **Gate:** my sandbox lacks the test DATABASE_URL → 11 platform/env tests fail on `[@crm2/config] invalid environment: DATABASE_URL` (password/totp/storage-mail/system/push/export) and 576 DB-integration tests skip — NONE are the tasks suite, NONE relate to this diff. The author's 643/643 claim is credible (env present on their side); build/lint turbo tasks passed here.
- **Carried NOTE (not introduced here):** the 5b export-gate inconsistency persists; this slice does the RIGHT thing (gates ₹ export columns on the resource perm). The cases/repository.ts `TASK_VIEW_COLS` rate-ladder duplication is correctly flagged in BOTH the old and new lateral doc-comments (⚠ PRECEDENCE DUPLICATION) — acceptable as a documented mirror, not a fork.
**VERDICT: BLOCK** on the dropped `assignedTo` export filter (one-line fix). Everything else PASS. Re-run with assignedTo restored + a test asserting export honours `?assignedTo=` → clears to commit.

- **2026-06-16 — ADR-0037 MIS Layout Engine Slice 1 — `report_layouts`/`report_layout_columns` CRUD module (working tree, uncommitted; new module `modules/reportLayouts/*`, `0060_report_layouts.sql`, `packages/sdk/src/reportLayouts.ts`, ADR-0037). VERDICT: PASS, no MUST-FIX.**
  New per-(client,product,kind∈{DATA_ENTRY,MIS,BILLING_MIS}) layout-config pair + CRUD (list/get/by-config/create/update/activate/deactivate), mirroring the `commissionRates` module conventions. Audited adversarially against the points the CTO flagged:
  - **Layering/boundaries — faithful to commissionRates SoT.** controller→service→repository; raw SQL only in repo; controller thin (`parseId` + delegate + std try/catch→`next(e)`); service does zod-validate + `resolvePage`/`resolveFilters`/`buildPage`; routes `authorize(TEMPLATE_MANAGE)` on EVERY route. `LAYOUT_FROM` shared by COUNT+page+findHeader. No cross-feature import; SDK leaf is zod/type only.
  - **OCC (ADR-0019) — correct.** `update`: `SELECT … FOR UPDATE` → `cur.version !== expectedVersion → AppError.stale(cur)` → name UPDATE + (if columns) DELETE+reinsert, ALL inside `withTransaction`. `setActive`: version-guarded `WHERE id=$1 AND version=$4 RETURNING`, 0 rows → `AppError.stale(before)`. `requireVersion(input)` pulled from the body (controller for (de)activate, service for update) → 400 VERSION_REQUIRED on missing/non-int. Matches commissionRates byte-for-byte in shape.
  - **The 23505 / two-unique distinction — CORRECT & not mis-mapped (the CTO's key question).** `mapWriteError` maps ONLY `code===23505 && constraint==='uq_report_layouts_active'` → 409 `REPORT_LAYOUT_EXISTS`. The SECOND unique `uq_report_layout_columns_key (layout_id,column_key)` is intentionally NOT mapped, and is **unreachable from the API**: `layoutColumnsSchema.superRefine` rejects duplicate column keys in-payload (400), and `update` does DELETE-then-reinsert the ENTIRE column set in one tx with the header row `FOR UPDATE` (serializes concurrent same-layout writes → no cross-payload key collision). If it ever fired it falls to `throw e` → 500 (genuinely exceptional, acceptable). No path mis-attributes a column-key clash to REPORT_LAYOUT_EXISTS. ✅
  - **create/update TRANSACTION — sound.** create = header INSERT + `insertColumns` both in-tx (atomic; `RETURNING id` then re-`findDetail`). update DELETE+reinsert-all is the right model for "replace the full column set in place" given per-layout key-uniqueness + `ON DELETE CASCADE` FK; no partial-write window (single tx). insertColumns binds 11 params incl `::jsonb` casts for options/validation, `displayOrder ?? i` index fallback, ref/section `.trim() || null`.
  - **SQL-injection surface — NONE.** `source_type`/`source_ref` are ALWAYS bound ($4/$5 in insertColumns; via `add('rl.kind=$?',…)` bound in WHERE) — never interpolated. `o.sortColumn` IS interpolated into `ORDER BY` but is provably whitelisted by `resolvePage`→`LAYOUT_PAGE_SPEC.sortMap` (7 cols, all real `rl./c./p.`) with default fallback for unknown/stale `sortBy`; `rl.id` tiebreak. `filterClauses` columns come from `filterMap` (whitelisted), values always bound; `likeContains` escapes `\%_`. The `add()` `$?`→`$N` replace is first-occurrence, exactly one per clause — index-safe. LIMIT/OFFSET bound as `$N+1/$N+2`. `resolvePage` caps `limit≤MAX_PAGE_SIZE` (400 LIMIT_TOO_LARGE). No crafted `sortBy`/filter/source reaches FROM/ORDER BY/WHERE unparametrized.
  - **by-config null — correct contract.** `findActiveByConfig` → null → service → 200 `null` (NOT 404); test asserts both the hit (`.id===id`) and the miss (`body===null`). Missing/!int clientId|productId|kind → 400 BAD_REQUEST (guarded in `byConfig` service via `toPosInt`/`toKind`).
  - **validateColumnSource FIXED/REFLESS/FREE contract — correct.** REFLESS (RATE_AMOUNT/COMMISSION_AMOUNT/TAT) rejects a stray ref; FIXED (TASK/CASE/APPLICANT_FIELD) requires `source_ref ∈ fields[].key`; FREE (DATA_ENTRY_FIELD/FORM_DATA_PATH/DOC_TYPE_COUNT/COMPUTED) accepts any non-empty. Enforced in `ReportLayoutColumnInputSchema.superRefine` → 400 (test covers bad-fixed-ref + stray-refless-ref). DB CHECK on `source_type`/`data_type` mirrors the SDK enums.
  - **No N+1 / perf-trap in this slice.** list = scalar `column_count` subquery per row (bounded by page limit) + separate `count(*)::int` sharing the SAME clause/params (no drift; `LAYOUT_FROM` INNER joins clients/products = FK→PK 1:1, no row-multiply). findDetail = 2 queries (header + ordered columns), not N+1.
  - **No `any`/suppressions/`console.*`** (grep clean on module + SDK leaf). TS-strict conditional spreads in service list-opts/filters and update patch. **Independently re-verified `tsc --noEmit`: SDK_EXIT=0, API_EXIT=0.** Author's gate claim (api 650/650, sdk 124/124) credible; the api.test.ts is `describe.skipIf(!RUN)` (DB-gated, env-present on author side) and asserts create-order/by-config-null/unique-active-409/deactivate-frees-slot/reactivate-409/update-replaces-cols+stale-409/source-validation-400/RBAC-403+bad-id-400.
  - **Migration 0060 — forward-only + idempotent** (`CREATE TABLE/INDEX IF NOT EXISTS`, partial-unique `uq_report_layouts_active … WHERE is_active`, lookup idx, cascade FK, column-key unique). DB auditor owns triple-write apply.
  - **ADR-0037 present & coherent** — dedicated pair (not `report_templates` overload) justified as implementation-evolution of Accepted-but-unbuilt ADR-0015 §3 (not a frozen-decision reopen); RBAC reuses `report_template.manage` (no new perm). SDK client methods return `Paginated<View>`/`Detail|null` correctly; index re-export ordered before consumers.
  - **SHOULD-FIX (non-blocking, parity-note):** `setActive` reads `before`/`after` via `findHeader` OUTSIDE the tx around the guarded UPDATE (3 round-trips, non-atomic) — but this is BYTE-FAITHFUL to the commissionRates reference (approved pattern, not a regression) and the version-guard is the real correctness gate. No action. OPEN (deferred to later slices per ADR): Layout Designer FE (slice 2), data-entry write + `case_data_entries` (slice 3), MIS/Billing-MIS generation + `v_mis_rows` (4–5). **Nothing blocks the commit.**

- **2026-06-16 — ADR-0037 MIS Engine Slice 2 (FE Layout Designer) — `features/reportLayouts/ReportLayoutsPage.tsx` + `/admin/report-layouts` route/nav + e2e registration (working tree, uncommitted, FE-only). VERDICT: PASS (2 FLAG-level UX papercuts, non-blocking; no MUST-FIX).**
  New `/admin/report-layouts` page (DataGrid list + Edit/Activate-Deactivate) + Layout Designer dialog (build per-(client,product) layout for one KIND from blank; columns bind to SOURCE_CATALOG; up/down reorder; OCC). Mirrors CommissionRatesPage. Audited adversarially on the CTO's five axes. `pnpm --filter @crm2/web typecheck` re-run here EXIT 0.
  - **(1) set-state-during-render hydration — SOUND, no infinite loop.** `if (isEdit && detail.data && !hydrated) { …5 setters…; setHydrated(true) }` is React's sanctioned "adjusting state during render" idiom: the `!hydrated` guard is idempotent → React re-renders once without committing the intermediate DOM, then the guard suppresses re-fire. Terminates. **Refetch risk = none/by-design:** a background `detail` refetch (refocus) yields a new `detail.data` but `hydrated` is already true → re-hydration suppressed → the user's in-progress edits are NOT clobbered; a server-side change since open is caught by OCC `version` → 409 on save (handled). **Stale-editId risk = none:** the dialog has no `key` but `editId` is provably stable for each mount — the only opens are `setDialog({editId:r.id})` / `setDialog({editId:null})` from the grid, the dialog is a full-screen overlay so Edit/New are unreachable while open, and Cancel sets `dialog=null` (unmount) before any re-open → fresh mount + fresh `hydrated=false`. No A→B in-place transition. useEffect would be marginally more conventional but this is correct React and matches the codebase's render-time-derivation idiom.
  - **(2) column→payload mapping — matches the slice-1 zod contract, with two FE-vs-server gaps (see FLAG).** REFLESS→`sourceRef:undefined` (zod `.nullish()` ✓); FIXED/FREE empty-ref blocked by `canSave` (rowError gate) ✓; `displayOrder:i` ✓ (`.int().min(0)`); `isRequired` only when `kind==='DATA_ENTRY'` ✓ (`.optional()`); `section` omitted when empty ✓ (`.nullish()`); `columnKey: r.columnKey || slug(headerLabel)`.
  - **(3) misc — clean.** `useMemo([toggle])` on columns: `toggle` (react-query mutation obj) changes identity on status transitions → columns rebuild a few extra times; harmless, matches CommissionRatesPage convention. `move` swap non-null asserts bounds-guarded ✓. `ROW_SEQ` module counter: Vite SPA, no SSR, single bundle instance/tab, dialogs never coexist → monotonic React-key uniqueness is all that's needed ✓ (acceptable for CSR admin per brief). `canSave` = name+rows+per-row-valid+(create→client&product). Error mapping VALIDATION/REPORT_LAYOUT_EXISTS/STALE_UPDATE/(toggle)REPORT_LAYOUT_EXISTS all verified against REAL wire codes: ZodError→`{error:'VALIDATION'}` (http/app.ts:115), AppError.stale→`STALE_UPDATE`, partial-unique→`REPORT_LAYOUT_EXISTS` (repository.ts:23); web `ApiError.code = json.error` (sdk.ts:76) → mappings correct.
  - **(4) TS-strict / styling / reuse — CLEAN.** grep: 0 `any`/eslint-disable/ts-ignore/ts-expect-error/console.*. typecheck EXIT 0. 0 raw hex/rgb — token-only (`bg-st-approved-bg`/`text-st-approved` reuse existing tokens used in Pipeline/CaseDetail/RateManagement; `bg-card`/`border-border`/`text-muted-foreground`/`input`/`btn`/`btn-ghost`). Reuses DataGrid/HexagonLoader/toast/`formatDateTime`. `slug` helper local, correct.
  - **(5) SDK contract — consumed correctly, validation mirror is byte-identical.** All types from `@crm2/sdk` (LayoutKind/SourceType/ColumnDataType/ReportLayout/View/Detail/Option/PageQuery/Paginated). `validateColumnSource` is the **same SDK function** the server's `superRefine` calls (FE imports it for the live per-row hint) → ZERO divergence on source-binding validation (REFLESS-rejects-ref / FIXED-requires-catalog-key / FREE-non-empty). Toggle route+body (`POST …/activate|deactivate {version}`) matches controller `requireVersion(req.body)`. PUT update sends `{name,columns,version}` — `version` survives because service calls `requireVersion(input)` on the RAW input, not the schema-stripped `validated` (service.ts:103-104). Three-way perm consistency: nav `report_template.manage` == page `has()` guard == BE route `TEMPLATE_MANAGE`.
  - **🟡 FLAG (non-blocking, UX papercut — NO data-integrity risk; server is the real gate, slice-1 audited PASS):** the FE binding mirror does NOT mirror two server-only column rules, so a *valid-looking* designer state can be rejected with only a generic VALIDATION toast and no per-row highlight: **(a) empty columnKey** — a pure-punctuation/diacritic-only header (e.g. `"!!!"`, `"___"`) → `slug()` returns `''` → `columnKey=''` → server zod `min(1)`/regex 400; `canSave`/`rowError` pass it (header non-empty). **(b) duplicate columnKey** — two columns labelled identically (e.g. both "Case Number" → `case_number`) → server `layoutColumnsSchema` duplicate-key 400; `canSave` has no cross-row uniqueness check. Both reliably 400 server-side (no bad data ever persists), but the FE can't point the operator at the offending row. SHOULD-FIX in a follow-up: extend `canSave`/`rowError` with an empty-derived-key check + cross-row key-collision check (cheap, reuses `slug` + the same map already computed). Cosmetic only.
  - **Gate:** typecheck EXIT 0 (re-verified here); author's `pnpm verify` EXIT 0 + browser-verify (create/edit/REFLESS/0-console) credible. e2e a11y+viewport register the page (`primary:/New Layout/`, card:true) — accurate to the rendered CTA. **PASS — cleared to commit.** No BLOCK. The two FLAGs are UX-quality follow-ups, not correctness or contract violations.

### 2026-06-16 — ADR-0037 MIS Engine Slice 3a (office data-entry backend) — VERDICT: PASS (1 FLAG, non-blocking; no MUST-FIX)
Working tree, uncommitted. New `modules/caseDataEntries/*` (GET/PUT `/api/v2/data-entry/tasks/:taskId`), `0061_case_data_entries.sql`, `packages/sdk/src/caseDataEntries.ts`, `DATA_ENTRY_MANAGE` perm, app.ts wire, + immutable-once-used guard in `reportLayouts/repository.ts` update. Audited adversarially on every CTO axis. API tsc EXIT 0, SDK tsc EXIT 0, 0 `any`/suppressions/`console.*` (grep). DB-gated api.test.ts skipIf in my sandbox (no DATABASE_URL); author's api 652 + live :4000 E2E green credible.
- **Layering / cross-module `reportLayoutRepository` import — ACCEPTABLE, consistent with precedent.** `caseDataEntries/service.ts:3` imports `../reportLayouts/repository.js` to resolve the active DATA_ENTRY layout. This mirrors the SANCTIONED pattern: the cases module imports `taskRepository` cross-module the same way; reportLayouts is a *config/catalog* read (findActiveByConfig — a pure lookup, no write coupling), not a feature-internal. Not worth a platform helper for a single read-consumer (Karpathy rule 2 — no speculative abstraction). If a 2nd consumer (slice 4/5 MIS-gen) lands, promote then. Consistent with the existing module graph; no new circular risk (reportLayouts does not import caseDataEntries).
- **Upsert race (insert path) — TOCTOU is CLOSED by the DB, check-then-insert is belt-and-suspenders.** `save` does `findByTask` → branch insert/update. Two concurrent first-saves both read null → both insert; the 2nd hits `uq_case_data_entries_task` (UNIQUE task_id) → `23505` caught → 409 `DATA_ENTRY_EXISTS` ("reload"). The check-then-insert is NOT the integrity gate (the unique constraint is); the pre-read just routes the common case. Correct + race-safe. Only the FK/unique enforce truth. ✅
- **OCC "first save no version / subsequent requires version" — SOUND, no silent lost update.** `requireVersion(input)` is called ONLY on the update branch (existing entry present). First save needs no version (nothing to clobber). The classic lost-update concern (A & B both read v1, both save) does NOT apply to first-save (the unique constraint forces the 2nd into the insert-409 path, not a silent overwrite). On update, `requireVersion` pulls `version` from the RAW body (occ.ts VersionEnvelope) → 400 VERSION_REQUIRED if missing/non-int/negative; the guarded `UPDATE … WHERE version=$4` → 0 rows → `AppError.stale(before)` → 409 with the fresh row. A stale read CANNOT cause a lost update: the version mismatch fails the WHERE. The non-tx `before` SELECT in `update` is only for the 404-vs-409 distinction + stale payload (READ COMMITTED; a row deleted between SELECT and UPDATE → 0 rows → stale-409 instead of 404 — harmless, both are non-2xx and the operator reloads). ✅
- **🟡 FLAG (non-blocking, theoretical lost-WORK window — NOT lost-update; no data corruption):** the version the client echoes on update comes from the GET (`entry.version`), but `save` re-reads `existing`/`before` server-side and the guard is purely the echoed `version`. If operator A reads v1, B reads v1, A saves→v2, B saves with version=1 → B gets 409 (correct, B reloads). The only true "blind overwrite" path: a client that omits `version` on a *second* save → 400 (not an overwrite). So no silent lost update exists. The FLAG is merely that there is no field-level merge — a full-map PUT replaces `data` wholesale (last-writer-wins AMONG callers who pass the right version). That is the intended single-operator-per-task model (one row per task, office-keyed); acceptable per ADR-0037. No action.
- **Validation: required-present + unknown-key-DROP — RIGHT call, not reject.** Dropping unknown keys (vs 400) is correct for a layout-driven form: a layout re-column (add/remove a column on a NEW active layout — old layout is immutable-once-used) means a client briefly holding a stale layout would send keys the server no longer knows; silently keeping only `layout.columns[].columnKey` keeps the stored `data` canonical to the CURRENT layout and never persists orphan keys. Required-empty (`undefined|null|''`) → 400 DATA_ENTRY_REQUIRED{field}. Test asserts the drop (`bogus` stripped) + required-400. **Type coercion intentionally absent — ACCEPTABLE this slice:** `data` is `z.record(z.unknown())`, stored as jsonb verbatim; per-column `data_type`/`validation` are NOT yet enforced (the column catalog carries them but the data-entry write treats all values as opaque). This is a known carry (the test's `deCol` comment flags COMPUTED/no-MANUAL-source-type as least-wrong). Values are typed/validated at MIS-generation (slice 4/5) or a later hardening. Not a correctness defect for 3a — no bad data is *rejected-as-valid*; it's stored as-supplied jsonb. Worth a follow-up to enforce `data_type` (numeric/date) at write.
- **Immutable guard placement + race vs concurrent first data-entry save — CORRECT.** Guard sits INSIDE `reportLayouts.update`'s `withTransaction`, AFTER the layout-header `SELECT … FOR UPDATE` (repository.ts:193) and BEFORE the DELETE/reinsert of columns (line 218). The FOR UPDATE on the layout row is the serialization point: a concurrent `case_data_entries` INSERT must acquire `FOR KEY SHARE` on the parent layout row for FK validation, which CONFLICTS with FOR UPDATE → the insert blocks until the update tx commits. So: (a) update-then-insert → insert proceeds against the recolumned layout (data keyed to NEW cols, no orphan); (b) insert-then-update → update's `SELECT 1 FROM case_data_entries` sees the committed row → 409 REPORT_LAYOUT_IN_USE. No interleaving lets columns change out from under keyed data (READ COMMITTED is sufficient *because* of the FOR-UPDATE/FK-KEY-SHARE conflict — no SERIALIZABLE needed). `idx_case_data_entries_layout` backs the guard SELECT. ✅
- **taskScope SQL / scope contract — FAITHFUL.** `taskScope` FROM = `case_tasks ct JOIN cases cs ON cs.id=ct.case_id`, exactly `taskScopePredicate`'s documented contract (scope/index.ts:75-87). `taskScopePredicate(params, scope)` appended as `AND <pred>` (or nothing for SUPER_ADMIN/ALL); null row → service 404 (IDOR-safe, out-of-scope == absent). `resolveScope` reuses the platform seam unchanged (BACKEND_USER/MANAGER hierarchy + dimension caps) — the office-role *reachability* of a task (assigned_to/created_by leg) is PRE-EXISTING platform policy, not a slice regression; the slice correctly delegates rather than inventing a parallel visibility rule. ✅
- **Injection — NONE.** taskId guarded by UUID_RE (service) before any query; `data` JSON.stringify'd + bound `$3::jsonb` (insert) / `$2::jsonb` (update) — never interpolated; layout columns iterated by server-owned `columnKey` (not user input) to build `clean`. `findActiveByConfig` binds client/product/kind. The guard SELECT binds `layout_id=$1`. No string interpolation of any user value anywhere in the module.
- **Perm/migration alignment — CONSISTENT.** Code `ROLE_PERMISSIONS` grants DATA_ENTRY_MANAGE to MANAGER + BACKEND_USER (+ SA via grants_all); migration 0061 `INSERT … role_permissions` for MANAGER + BACKEND_USER (ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING). Match. TEAM_LEADER deliberately EXCLUDED (test asserts TL → 403). PERMISSION_META label present. Route gates DATA_ENTRY_MANAGE on BOTH verbs. DB auditor owns triple-write apply of 0061 (forward-only, idempotent: IF NOT EXISTS table+index, UNIQUE(task_id), FK→case_tasks/report_layouts, ON CONFLICT perm insert).
- **TS-strict / reuse — CLEAN.** No `any`/eslint-disable/ts-ignore/ts-expect-error/console.* (grep, exit 1). Reuses `requireVersion`/`resolveScope`/`taskScopePredicate`/`AppError`/`query`/`withTransaction`. SDK leaf = zod+type only; client `dataEntry.{get,save}` + index re-export ordered before consumers. Controller thin (actor()+taskId()+delegate+next(e)). Error codes verified vs wire: stale→409 STALE_UPDATE, versionRequired→400 VERSION_REQUIRED, conflict→409, notFound→404, badRequest→400 (errors.ts).
- **Gate:** api tsc EXIT 0 + sdk tsc EXIT 0 (re-run here); DB-gated api.test.ts skipIf(!RUN) — env-absent in my sandbox, present author-side (author claims api 652, sdk 126, live :4000 E2E green — credible; the 3 tests cover save/required-400/unknown-drop/OCC-400-409-v2, immutable-409+rename-OK, not-configured-400/TL-403/absent-404/non-uuid-400). **PASS — cleared to commit.** No BLOCK, no MUST-FIX. Two carries for later slices: (1) enforce per-column `data_type` coercion/validation at the data-entry write (currently opaque jsonb), (2) promote reportLayoutRepository read to a platform helper if a 2nd cross-module consumer lands. Neither blocks 3a.

### 2026-06-16 — ADR-0037 MIS Engine Slice 3 RE-GRAIN (per-task → per-CASE) — VERDICT: PASS (1 carried FLAG; no MUST-FIX)
Staged diff (`git diff --cached`). Re-grains the slice-3a office data-entry from per-task to per-CASE per the ADR-0037 correction (Zion `NewDataQC` keys MIS fields once per case): mig `db/v2/migrations/0062` (DROP+recreate `case_data_entries` `uq(case_id)` FK `cases`, test-data-only), BE `caseDataEntries/{repository,service,controller,routes}.ts`+test, SDK `caseDataEntries.ts`(`CaseDataEntry`)+`client.ts`+`client.test.ts`, web `cases/CaseDetailPage.tsx` (new per-CASE `DataEntrySection`), `openapi.json` regen, ADR-0037 correction note. Audited adversarially on every CTO axis. **API tsc EXIT 0, SDK tsc EXIT 0 (re-run here); 0 `any`/eslint-disable/ts-ignore/ts-expect-error/`console.*` across module+SDK+FE (grep).**
- **(1) module-local `caseScopePredicate` (repository.ts:18-26) — BYTE-IDENTICAL mirror of `cases/repository.ts:180-188`, boundary-clean, IDOR-safe.** Same `composeScopePredicate(params, scope, (ph)=>'cs.created_by = ANY(${ph}) OR EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM case_tasks ct WHERE ct.case_id = cs.id AND ct.assigned_to = ANY(${ph}))')` — verb-for-verb identical to the cases reference (diffed). Module-local copy is the established pattern (slice-5d audit affirmed scope predicates stay copied per-module = visibility policy, not config). **Parenthesization — CORRECT, in fact MORE defensive than the reference.** `composeScopePredicate` (scope/index.ts:66-69) ALREADY self-wraps: OR-leg → `(${orParts})`, whole → `(${parts})`, so the returned `pred` is fully parenthesized. The reference applies it bare (`AND ${scopePred}`, cases/repo:497); the new code applies `AND (${pred})` (repository.ts:30) — a redundant-but-harmless extra layer. The `cs.id = $1 AND (…OR…)` head query binds correctly either way; no precedence/IDOR bug. FROM contract matches (`FROM cases cs`, `cs` alias) — slice-3a's `case_tasks ct JOIN cases cs` was right for taskScope; the new single-table `FROM cases cs` is right for caseScope. `caseScope` SELECTs `cs.id AS case_id, cs.client_id, cs.product_id` (dropped the now-irrelevant `ct.status`) — clean.
- **(2) cross-module `reportLayoutRepository` import (service.ts:3) — UNCHANGED from 3a, still ACCEPTABLE (1 consumer).** Same sanctioned config/catalog read (`findActiveByConfig`, pure lookup, no write coupling, no circular risk). Carried follow-up: promote to platform helper if slice 4/5 adds a 2nd consumer. No action this slice.
- **(3) FE useState-initializer-from-props + remount `key=`${caseId}:${data.entry?.version ?? 0}`` — SOUND.** Both `useState` calls use lazy initializers (`() => {…}`) seeded from `entry.entry?.data` — runs once per mount, no set-during-render, no effect needed. Re-hydration after save is driven by the remount `key`: `save.onSuccess` → `invalidateQueries(['data-entry',caseId])` → refetch → new `version` → key changes → `DataEntryFields` REMOUNTS with fresh initializers seeded from the just-saved values. Tracks the slice-2 render-time-hydration idiom but via the cleaner key-remount route. **No edit-clobber risk** (key only bumps on `version`, which only changes after a *successful save* that already invalidated; an in-flight refetch returning the same version leaves the key stable → no remount → in-progress edits preserved). Parent gates the empty/error/null-layout states so `DataEntryFields` only mounts with a non-null layout.
- **(4) `Number(v)` NaN risk (CaseDetailPage.tsx buildData) — REAL but minor data-quality edge, NOT a correctness/security defect.** A NUMBER column fed non-numeric text (the `type="number"` input mostly prevents this, but paste/locale edge cases exist) → `Number("abc")` = NaN → `JSON.stringify(NaN)` = `null` → stored as jsonb `null`. No crash, no bad-typed value persisted-as-valid; it lands as null. This is the SAME class as 3a's carried FLAG (per-column `data_type` not enforced at write — `data` is `z.record(z.unknown())`, opaque jsonb). The blank-omit guard (`if (v==='') continue`) is correct (only keyed values stored). Worth folding into the existing slice-4/5 data_type-hardening carry; does not block.
- **(5) `entry.layout!` non-null assertion (DataEntryFields:`entry.layout!.columns`) — JUSTIFIED & DOCUMENTED.** Parent `DataEntrySection` renders the null-layout empty state (`!data.layout ? <empty> : <DataEntryFields …>`) so the child only mounts with a non-null layout; the `!` is commented (`// layout is non-null here (the parent renders the empty state otherwise)`). The lone `!` is the cleanest expression of that parent-guaranteed invariant (an extra runtime guard would be dead code). `column.options` is a non-optional `{label,value}[]` on `ReportLayoutColumn` (reportLayouts.ts:128) → `column.options.map` is safe with no guard. No other suppressions.
- **(6) RE-GRAIN CONSISTENCY end-to-end — COMPLETE, zero half-migrated artifact.** grep `task_id`/`taskScope`/`TaskCpv`/`findByTask`/`TaskDataEntry`/`data-entry/tasks` across `caseDataEntries/**`, SDK `caseDataEntries.ts`+`client.ts`, and web = **0 hits** (the only `taskId` survivors are unrelated `cases.tasks` SDK methods — assign/complete/revoke etc.). All renamed coherently: repo `caseScope`/`findByCase`/`CaseCpv`, service `CaseDataEntry`/`CASE_NOT_FOUND`, controller `caseId(req)`, routes `/cases/:caseId`, SDK `CaseDataEntry`/`/data-entry/cases/${caseId}`, `client.test.ts` URL, `openapi.json` (`/api/v2/data-entry/cases/{caseId}`, both operationIds), test seeds a CASE (drops the task/applicant/post-tasks dance — correct: a case alone suffices). Mig 0062 `uq(case_id)` FK `cases(id)`, layout idx retained (immutable guard keys off `layout_id`, grain-agnostic — preserved). ADR-0037 correction note coherent + supersedes the 3a "one record per task" line. The 23505 insert-race comment updated (`uq_case_data_entries_case`).
- **(7) "persistent card removed onClose cleanly" — N/A (no such artifact in this diff).** The FE diff is purely ADDITIVE (no `-` source lines beyond the diff header); slice-3a shipped no per-task FE wiring, so there was nothing to remove. The new `DataEntrySection` is a plain `{canDataEntry && <…>}` conditional render — no modal, no `onClose`, no persistent card, no cleanup obligation. The OCC/insert-race/immutable-guard/scope-404 invariants from the 3a audit are all preserved unchanged at the new grain (verified: `requireVersion` still update-branch-only; `findByCase` pre-read routes the common case while `uq(case_id)` is the integrity gate → concurrent first-save 2nd → 23505 → 409 DATA_ENTRY_EXISTS; UUID_RE guards `caseId` before any query; all values bound, never interpolated).
- **Gate:** api+sdk tsc EXIT 0 (re-run here); DB-gated api.test.ts skipIf(!RUN) — env-absent in my sandbox, present author-side (author: typecheck 8/8, build, sdk 124/124, changed modules pass isolated, 1 full-run fail = documented rotating flake, openapi 208 paths, browser-verified at case grain — all credible). **PASS — cleared to commit.** No BLOCK, no MUST-FIX. Carries (both pre-existing, neither introduced nor worsened materially here): (1) per-column `data_type` coercion at the data-entry write — now also covers FE `Number()`→NaN→null (fold into slice-4/5 hardening); (2) promote `reportLayoutRepository` read to platform helper on 2nd consumer. file:lines — repository.ts:18-30, service.ts:18-52, CaseDetailPage.tsx DataEntrySection/DataEntryFields/buildData, 0062_case_data_entries_case_grain.sql:11-26.

### 2026-06-16 — CASE-DETAIL PAGE: pickup + field-photos + lifecycle reorder + report-engine ADR-0038 — VERDICT: PASS (1 low-sev style FLAG; no MUST-FIX)
Staged `git diff --cached`. Audited adversarially on correctness/layering/reuse/TS-strict/React. **API+SDK+WEB tsc EXIT 0 (re-run here); sdk 128/128 (re-run); eslint CaseDetailPage EXIT 0; openapi 210 paths incl both new routes; 0 suppressions in diff.**

- **(a) Add-Tasks fold — behavior PRESERVED.** `addingTasks` state moved out of CaseDetailPage into `TasksSection` (CaseDetailPage:281 `const [addingTasks,setAddingTasks]=useState(false)`); the toggle now lives in the card header (`canCreate && !addingTasks` button :194; the form renders below the header `canCreate && addingTasks` :200). `onAdded` → `setAddingTasks(false)` + `qc.invalidateQueries({queryKey:['case',caseId]})` (:209-211) — byte-identical to the prior `['case',id]` invalidate (caseId IS id, passed as prop). `canAssign` is a PRE-EXISTING TasksSection prop (:277,288) so AddTasksForm still gets it. New props `canCreate/clientId/productId/applicants` threaded + typed (`applicants: CaseDetail['applicants']`). No regression. ✓
- **(b) listFieldPhotos scope-guard — IDOR-safe, fails-closed.** repository.ts:1346: `taskScopePredicate(params,scope)` → `AND EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM case_tasks ct2 JOIN cases cs ON cs.id=ct2.case_id WHERE ct2.id=ca.task_id AND ${pred})`; service.ts:431 gates on `repo.caseVisible` first (404 if case not visible). Filter is `kind='FIELD_PHOTO' AND deleted_at IS NULL`. **Correctly OMITS the `task_id IS NULL` leg** that listAttachments has — field photos are always device/task-scoped (insertFieldAttachment always binds task_id; a NULL-task field photo would fail-closed = hidden), so unlike office reference attachments there is no case-level leg to admit. Out-of-scope/absent → empty/404, IDOR-safe. ✓
- **🟡 FLAG (low-sev, STYLE only — not a bug).** listFieldPhotos's EXISTS subquery aliases `case_tasks ct2` but the injected `taskScopePredicate` text references `ct.assigned_to` (its FROM-contract is `case_tasks ct`). It resolves CORRECTLY only by correlation to the OUTER `LEFT JOIN case_tasks ct ON ct.id=ca.task_id` — `ct` and `ct2` are provably the same row (both `=ca.task_id`), and `cs.created_by` binds to the subquery's own `cs`, so the predicate is semantically right and fails-closed if outer `ct` is NULL. But it DIVERGES from the canonical listAttachments pattern (repository.ts:1328) whose subquery aliases `ct`/`cs` self-contained matching the predicate contract exactly. The `ct2` is redundant; the predicate already covers the task via the outer correlation. SHOULD-FIX (cheap, non-blocking): drop `ct2`, alias the subquery `case_tasks ct` like listAttachments, so the predicate's documented FROM-contract (`ct`) is satisfied locally rather than by accidental outer correlation — protects against a future edit to the outer join. No data-integrity/IDOR risk today.
- **(c) FieldPhotoThumb per-photo presigned URL (N queries) — ACCEPTABLE.** Each thumb fires its own `['field-photo-url',caseId,photo.id]` query → one presigned-URL call per photo (CaseDetailPage:1511). For case galleries (handful–dozens of photos) this is fine and react-query dedups/caches; the URLs are short-lived presigned so a batch endpoint would need its own expiry handling. NOTE for scale: a batch `/field-photos?withUrls=1` would cut the round-trips if galleries grow large — not needed now.
- **(d) Pickup TAT compute + datetime round-trip — CORRECT.** Server `buildPickup` (service.ts): `timeOfVerificationDays = Math.max(0, Math.floor((Date.parse(reported)-Date.parse(pickup))/86_400_000))`, null until both set, `Number.isNaN` guarded → no NaN leak; `Math.max(0,…)` clamps reported<pickup to 0. api.test asserts =2 for 22nd→24th. FE round-trip: `isoToLocalInput` (ISO→`datetime-local` local-minute, NaN-guarded→'') / `localInputToIso` (`new Date(v).toISOString()` or null). Round-trips through the user's local TZ (correct for a `datetime-local` widget). PUT is full-replace (omitted field → null) — the documented data-entry contract; FE always submits the full set. ✓
- **(e) `_caseId` unused placeholder param — eslint SATISFIED.** `MobileReportSection({caseId:_caseId}:{caseId:string})` (:372): destructure-rename to `_caseId`, matches root `eslint.config.js:46` `argsIgnorePattern:'^_'`. Lint EXIT 0 confirmed. Intentional honest placeholder (the engine slice will consume caseId). ✓
- **(f) #9 disabled controls — not half-wired.** PDF/Word/Excel buttons `disabled title="Coming soon"` (:481); no onClick, no dangling handler. #6 is pure copy. Clean placeholders. ✓
- **(g) reorder — no section dropped, Case Result conditional intact** (verified by render-grep CaseDetailPage:175-234; conditional `COMPLETED||AWAITING_COMPLETION` verbatim at :204). ✓
- **Layering / reuse / TS-strict.** Pickup BE mirrors the audited caseDataEntries idioms (controller thin→service zod+scope+OCC→repo raw-SQL/bound-params; `requireVersion(input)` update-branch-only, insert version-less; 23505→409 PICKUP_EXISTS; UUID_RE guard; `caseScope` reused). `PICKUP_COLS` shared by all 3 verbs (no SELECT drift). SDK leaf = zod+type only, `isoDateNullish` helper, client methods barrel-correct. FE reuses `Meta`/`Field`/`HexagonLoader`/`api`/`ApiError`/toast; OCC STALE_UPDATE→reload copy. Migration 0063 forward-only/idempotent, correctly sequenced after 0062, OCC version col, FK cases. No `any`/eslint-disable/ts-ignore/ts-expect-error/console.* in the diff (grep clean). ✓
- **Gate:** tsc 3/3 EXIT 0 + sdk 128/128 + eslint 0 + openapi 210 (all re-run here); backend integration suites `skipIf(!RUN)` (DB-absent sandbox) — author's cases 60/60 + caseDataEntries pass + 1 documented rotating flake credible (pickup api.test reads correct: derived/TAT=2/OCC 400-409-v2/TL-403/absent-404 both verbs).

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit.** No BLOCK, no MUST-FIX. The lone FLAG is a SQL alias style-divergence in listFieldPhotos (`ct2` vs the predicate's `ct` contract) that works by outer correlation + fails closed — cosmetic robustness, not a correctness/IDOR hole. Carries: (1) align listFieldPhotos subquery alias to `ct` like listAttachments; (2) optional batch presigned-URL endpoint if galleries grow; (3) pre-existing data-entry carries unchanged. file:lines — cases/repository.ts:1346-1369, caseDataEntries/{repository.ts:122-196, service.ts:55-110}, CaseDetailPage.tsx:194-216/372/463/1349-1556, 0063_case_pickups.sql.

### 2026-06-16 — FIELD_REPORT ENGINE slice 1 (ADR-0039): Handlebars render + report_layouts extend — VERDICT: PASS (1 carried duplication-ratchet FLAG; no MUST-FIX)
Untracked module `apps/api/src/modules/fieldReports/**` + mig `db/v2/migrations/0064` + reportLayouts repo/service/SDK extend + cases route. No `Cannot read prop of null`. `formData` null (pre-submit, repository.ts:13) → `walkPath(null,…)` returns undefined at the first non-object guard (render.ts:27) → '' . ## 2026-06-16 — FIELD-REPORT S2a: combined #6 card (buildSections + FieldReportView ripple + lazy N-fetch) — VERDICT: PASS

Reviewed `git diff HEAD` (4 files) + new `apps/api/src/modules/fieldReports/sections.ts`. Pure-helper layering: `buildSections(ctx.formData)` is DB-free, called from `service.ts` on both render branches; SDK contract grows `sections`; FE accordion lazy-fetches per task.

### buildSections correctness — sound
- **SKIP_KEYS** lowercased-compared against `k.toLowerCase()` (sections.ts:47) so any device casing of `geoLocation`/`formData`/etc is dropped. Includes `formdata` so the nested-fallback path can't re-surface the raw `formData` sub-object as a field when the blob is flattened directly. ✓
- **Nested fallback** (sections.ts:61-63): `blob.formData` used when it's a non-array object, else the blob itself — covers both ingest shape (`{formData:{...}, verificationOutcome, ...}`) and a flat slug (`{noc:{remark,area}}`, test :49-56). ✓
- **toLabel** regexes: `_`→space, camel boundary `([a-z0-9])([A-Z])`, acronym boundary `([A-Z]+)([A-Z][a-z])`. `tpc1Name`→"Tpc1 Name" (digit-then-Upper splits), `met_person_relation`→"Met Person Relation" (test :5-9). The `w[0]!` non-null is guarded by the `(w ? ... : w)` ternary — safe under TS-strict. ✓
- **toValue** array/object/null: `null|undefined|''`→null (dropped); array→primitives-only filtered + `, `-joined (empty→null); `typeof==='object'`→null so nested objects are dropped (no `[object Object]`). String/number/bool→`String(v)` (`4`→"4"). ✓
- **verificationOutcome** appended AFTER keyed fields (sections.ts:66-67) — matches test ordering (api.test :183, sections.test :27). Section dropped entirely when `fields.length===0` (sections.ts:68) so a system-only slug yields no empty heading (test :61). ✓

### Edge cases — covered
- `formData` null/non-object → `[]` (sections.ts:55; test :59-60, api.test :196). ✓
- slug with only system keys → dropped (test :61). ✓
- deeply nested values → leaf object returns null, dropped (test :38 `nested:{deep:1}` absent from output). Note: nesting is flattened only ONE level (the `.formData` unwrap); deeper nested objects are intentionally dropped, not recursed — correct for v1 parity (v1 viewer is also flat). ✓

### Layering / TS-strict / ripple
- Pure helper, no DB import — correct module boundary. `FieldReportView.sections` added as required (non-optional) field; both service return sites populate it (service.ts:39,49) so no partial-shape; SDK consumers = only the FE `FieldReportBody`, which reads `report.sections`/`report.narrative`/`report.layoutName`/`report.verificationType` — all present. `ctx.formData` typed `Record<string,unknown>|null` (repository.ts:14) matches the helper's param. ✓

### FLAG (non-blocking) — the N-fetch pattern
- `TaskFieldReport` issues one `useQuery` per expanded task (`enabled: open`, key `['field-report', caseId, task.id]`). For a typical case (1–5 tasks) this is fine: lazy, cached, parallelizable, and the prior #6 was a single static placeholder so there's no regression. **ACCEPTABLE as shipped.** If a case ever carries many tasks AND a reviewer expand-alls, this is N round-trips — a future batch endpoint (`GET /cases/:id/field-reports`) would collapse it, but that's a premature abstraction now. Defer; revisit only if task-per-case counts grow.

OPEN/carries (unchanged by this slice): (1) promote `findActiveByConfig` layouts-read to a platform helper — ratchet still due; (2) `{{#eq}}` strict-=== template footgun; (3) CASE_REPORT/PDF + KYC deferred per ADR.

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit.** buildSections is correct and well-tested (sections.test 5: label/group/skip/fallback/empty), the contract ripple is total (no partial shape), untrusted-blob handling is defensive, TS-strict clean. file:lines — fieldReports/{sections.ts:16-71, service.ts:26-49}, sdk/reportLayouts.ts:287-310, cases/CaseDetailPage.tsx:1452-1543, __tests__/{sections.test.ts, fieldReports.api.test.ts:181-196}.

## 2026-06-16 — FIELD-REPORT S2b: designer for FIELD_REPORT + /by-config verificationType resolve (ADR-0039) — VERDICT: PASS

Reviewed `git diff HEAD` (4 files): `reportLayouts/service.ts` (byConfig +optional vt), `sdk/client.ts` (byConfig +optional 4th arg → query param), `web/ReportLayoutsPage.tsx` (designer opens to FIELD_REPORT), `reportLayouts.api.test.ts` (+1 FIELD_REPORT by-config test). Audited adversarially on byConfig back-compat, designer save logic, hydration, and the RATCHET. Gate authoritative: `pnpm verify` EXIT=0 (sdk 133, api 670 = +1, web build, openapi UNCHANGED, no flake).

- **(1) byConfig change — BACKWARD-COMPATIBLE, undefined→type-less path preserved (verified end-to-end).** `service.byConfig` (service.ts:94-97) reads `rawQuery['verificationType']`, guards `typeof vt === 'string' && vt.trim()` → either a trimmed value or `undefined`; forwards as the optional 4th arg. The repo (repository.ts:152-170, unchanged this slice) maps `undefined → AND verification_type IS NULL`, a value → bound `= $N`. The two prior callers (caseDataEntries:24,35 'DATA_ENTRY', no 4th arg) are UNCHANGED and hit the IS NULL leg — and the mig-0064 coherence CHECK forces non-FIELD_REPORT rows to `verification_type IS NULL`, so the IS NULL leg matches EXACTLY the pre-S2a result set. No previously-matching row stops matching. The empty/whitespace param degrades to `undefined` (not `''`) so it never tries to match a row the `verification_type <> ''` CHECK forbids. ✓ openapi UNCHANGED is correct: by-config parses loose `rawQuery`, has no zod query-schema, so an optional param is invisible to the spec.
- **(2) SDK arg — clean, encoded, optional.** `byConfig(clientId, productId, kind, verificationType?)` (client.ts:344-349) appends `&verificationType=${encodeURIComponent(verificationType)}` ONLY when truthy. Encoding is correct (codes are UPPER_SNAKE so encoding is a no-op today, but defensive + right). Existing 3-arg callers compile unchanged (optional param). ✓
- **(3) Designer save logic — CORRECT field routing per mode + reused column mapping.** The mutation (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:178-194) builds `columns` once (same mapping for all kinds — FIELD_REPORT "Variables" ARE columns, the relabel is cosmetic), then: EDIT → PUT `{ name, columns, version, ...(isFieldReport ? { templateBody } : {}) }` — sends templateBody only (verificationType OMITTED, immutable); CREATE → POST `{ clientId, productId, kind, name, columns, ...(isFieldReport ? { verificationType, templateBody } : {}) }` — sends BOTH. This is byte-aligned with the schemas: `UpdateReportLayoutSchema` (sdk/reportLayouts.ts:274-282) accepts only name/templateBody/columns — it does NOT accept verificationType, so the immutability is SERVER-ENFORCED, not just FE-cosmetic; `CreateReportLayoutSchema.superRefine(refineFieldReport)` requires both for FIELD_REPORT. The non-FIELD_REPORT POST/PUT carry neither → refine's "only for FIELD_REPORT" branch passes. Three-layer immutability (FE disable + FE omit-on-PUT + zod reject-on-PUT). ✓
- **(4) Hydration of verificationType/templateBody — ONCE, alongside existing fields.** The `if (isEdit && detail.data && !hydrated)` block (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:130-148) adds `setVerificationType(d.verificationType ?? '')` + `setTemplateBody(d.templateBody ?? '')` and the existing `setHydrated(true)` (unchanged) fires the whole block exactly once. `?? ''` coerces the nullable SDK contract (`verificationType: string | null`) to a controlled-input string. No second-render re-hydration, no flthat-state churn. ✓
- **(5) canSave — total over both modes.** `(!isFieldReport || (templateBody.trim() !== '' && (isEdit || verificationType !== '')))` (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:240-242). Non-FIELD_REPORT: clause is vacuously true (unchanged behaviour). FIELD_REPORT create: requires templateBody non-blank AND verificationType chosen. FIELD_REPORT edit: requires templateBody only (type locked). Mirrors Create-needs-both / Update-needs-only-body exactly. The `fieldUnits` source = `units.filter(u => u.kind === 'FIELD_VISIT')` (typed enum compare, not a string literal). ✓
- **(6) DESIGNER_KINDS widen — safe.** `DESIGNER_KINDS = LAYOUT_KINDS` (was `.filter(k !== 'FIELD_REPORT')`). The S1 reason for the filter ("create can't be attempted without a template body") is now MOOT because the FIELD_REPORT branch supplies both body+type and canSave gates them. Kind select stays `disabled={isEdit}` so the widened list can't re-key an existing row. ✓
- **(7) New api test — asserts the right invariants.** `mk('RESIDENCE')`+`mk('OFFICE')` both 201; 2nd active RESIDENCE → 409 (the `uq_report_layouts_active` COALESCE(vt,'') partial index, mig 0064:34-35); by-config WITHOUT type → null (type-less leg); by-config WITH `verificationType=OFFICE` → resolves the OFFICE row (name+verificationType+templateBody). Covers the exact new code path + the one-active-per-(cpv,type) DB guarantee. ✓ (DB-gated `describe.skipIf(!RUN)`; +1 reflected in api 670, author-side credible.)

### RATCHET RULING — CTO decision ADOPTED → ratchet CLOSED (keep import, do NOT promote)
At S2a I FLAGGED `findActiveByConfig` as having tripped the "promote to platform on 2nd consumer" ratchet (caseDataEntries=1st, fieldReports=2nd) and said "land it next slice." This IS next slice, and the CTO has ruled: **KEEP the cross-module `reportLayoutRepository.findActiveByConfig` import and document it; do NOT promote to `platform/`.** I CONCUR and RETIRE the carry. Engineering rationale (mine, aligned with the CTO's):
  - v2 `platform/` is INFRA (db pool, errors, scope primitives, auth) — it holds NO domain SQL. `findActiveByConfig` is a SELECT against `report_layouts` (a reportLayouts-owned table). Hoisting it to platform would put domain SQL in the infra layer → layering INVERSION, the exact thing the architecture forbids.
  - The correct home for a table's read method is its OWNING domain repo. Cross-domain READ reuse via direct import (fieldReports → reportLayouts, one-way, acyclic, no write coupling) is a SANCTIONED dependency direction, not a violation. The alternative (a platform facade) would add an indirection layer that owns nothing and resolves no real coupling.
  - The duplication ratchet exists to prevent COPY-PASTE divergence (cf. caseScopePredicate, which is correctly copied because it's per-module POLICY). `findActiveByConfig` is the inverse: a single canonical read that MUST stay shared. Sharing it via import is already the ratchet's desired end-state — there is nothing to de-duplicate. The tripwire forced a deliberate decision; the decision is "the current shape is correct."
  - Verified the import is still pure-read + one-directional this slice (no new write, no cycle): `fieldReports/service.ts:5` imports `reportLayoutRepository`, calls only `findActiveByConfig`. ✓
  **DISPOSITION: ratchet CLOSED. Standing carry "(1) promote findActiveByConfig" RETIRED.** Going forward, additional consumers of `findActiveByConfig` may import it directly without re-tripping (the shared-read-via-domain-import pattern is now the ADOPTED rule, documented here).

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit.** byConfig is backward-compatible (undefined→IS NULL preserved, verified against all 3 call sites + the mig-0064 CHECK), the designer routes verificationType create-only / templateBody both, immutability is triply-enforced (FE disable + FE omit + zod reject), hydration is once. Gate green (pnpm verify EXIT=0, +1 api test, openapi unchanged) + browser-verified :5273. RATCHET CLOSED. file:lines — reportLayouts/service.ts:94-97, sdk/client.ts:344-349, web/ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:{41-44,130-148,178-194,240-242,318-355,633-639}, __tests__/reportLayouts.api.test.ts:114-160, sdk/reportLayouts.ts:{262-282}, db/v2/migrations/0064_field_report_layouts.sql:34-35.

OPEN/carries (unchanged): (2) `{{#eq}}` strict-`===` numeric-vs-string footgun — designer help shows the string form; add a numeric-literal note; (3) FORM_DATA_PATH slug-must-match-ingest authoring caveat; (4) CASE_REPORT/PDF + KYC field-reports deferred per ADR.
