## 2026-06-16 — FIELD-REPORT S3a: grammar-helper library + plain-text (noEscape) render + envelope skip-keys (ADR-0039) — VERDICT: PASS

Reviewed `git diff HEAD` (4 files) + NEW `fieldReports/helpers.ts` (~30 helpers + `eq` + exported `hb`). Spot-checked each helper against v1 `CRM-BACKEND/src/services/TemplateReportService.ts` (mapFormDataToTemplateVariables, lines ~2019-2479 + the nameplate resolvers ~2597-2621). Gate: fieldReports 26 pass + 3 RUN-gated skip = 29 (helpers 14 + render 7 + sections 5 + integration 3).

- **(1) v1 port — FAITHFUL, line-for-line on the spot-checks.** `ordinal` (helpers.ts:18-24 ≡ v1:2062-2070, same `s[(v-20)%10] || s[v] || s[0]`, same `<0`/non-finite passthrough). `pluralize` (26-34 ≡ v1:2469-2479, same `/^(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s+(year|month|day|week)s?$/i`, same 1-vs-N cap). `nameplate` (67-71) correctly parameterizes the THREE v1 branches into one helper: door default verb `shows the name` + name `|| 'N/A'` (v1:2602-2604), society/company pass verb `"displays"` (v1:2610/2620), `/^sighted/i` gate + `is not sighted` else — byte-identical output. `callRemark` (212-222 ≡ v1:2342-2365) incl. the `pickup call → callConfirmation(confirmation)` delegation and the `lc(raw)` final fallback. `documentShown` (155-171 ≡ v1:2208-2237) incl. the Bug-125 free-text `no/n/yes/y` recognition and the residence doc-type-only silent leg. `area`/`date`(localIso, Bug-135 never-UTC)/`dominatedArea`/`politicalConnection`/`sittingLocation`/`tpcLabel`/`tpcPair`/`working`+`stayingStatus`/`setup`/`businessLocation`/`addressFloor`/`metPersonConfirmation`/`existsClause`/`callConfirmation`/`ownershipType`/`currentCompanyOperating`/`sentenceClause`/`activityVerdict`/`verdictOverride`/`default` all match their v1 originals on logic + literal strings. ✓
- **(2) `str()` coercion — CORRECT, and it is exactly what makes the optional trailing-arg pattern safe.** `str = x == null || typeof x === 'object' ? '' : String(x)` (helpers.ts:15). Handlebars passes its `HelperOptions` object as the FINAL positional arg of every helper invocation. A helper declared with arity N called with M<N template args sees `options` (an object) in the (M+1)th slot → `str(options)` → `''` (object branch), NOT `[object Object]`. Verified the **callRemark 1-arg case** is safe: `{{callRemark v}}` → `confirmation` param receives the options object → `callConfirmation(options)` only reached on the `pickup call` branch, where `lcOf(options)` → `str(options)` → `''` → `.trim()` → falls through every `startsWith` to the default `'the applicant confirmed the details over the call'` — which the helpers.test.ts:80-82 asserts exactly. The 2-arg `{{callRemark v c}}` puts the real confirmation in slot 2 and options in slot 3 (ignored). No path stringifies the options object. ✓ (Same safety holds for every variadic-optional helper: nameplate verb, businessLocation address, tpcPair, sentenceClause prefix/suffix.)
- **(3) noEscape compile + proto-flags RETAINED.** render.ts:74 `hb.compile(templateBody, { noEscape: true, strict: false })` — the only render-time change; the runtime call (75-79) still passes `allowProtoPropertiesByDefault:false` + `allowProtoMethodsByDefault:false`. noEscape disables OUTPUT entity-encoding (so `"X"` stays `"X"`, `<script>` stays raw) but does NOT touch path resolution — the proto guards are independent of escaping and remain in force. The render.test.ts assertion flipped correctly: was `toContain('&lt;script&gt;')`, now `toBe('Note: <script>x</script>')` (raw verbatim). ✓
- **(4) `hb` instance moved to helpers.ts, single isolated instance.** `Handlebars.create()` (helpers.ts:289) → `eq` (292-296, IDENTICAL to the old render.ts `eq`, block + subexpression dual-mode) + the 28-name `registerHelper({...})` object (298-328). render.ts now imports `hb` (no longer creates its own) — one instance, no double-registration, no global-Handlebars pollution. ✓
- **(5) SKIP_KEYS extension (sections.ts:16-31) — additive, lowercase-keyed (matches the existing `.toLowerCase()` lookup), v1 envelope keys.** Adds formtype/submissionid/submittedat/submittedby/verification/verificationimages alongside the prior 6. These are system/envelope fields that ride beside agent fields in `form_submissions.submission_data` — correctly suppressed from the #6 field display. Existing sections.test.ts (5) still green; no agent field collides with these names. ✓

### COLLISION RULING — concur with documenting now + deferring the designer-side guard to S3b
The footgun: a layout column whose `columnKey` equals a registered helper name (`area`, `date`, `setup`, `default`, `eq`, `lc`, `pluralize`, …) is SHADOWED — Handlebars resolves `{{area}}` to the **helper** (invoked with zero args → here `area(undefined)` → `'Not provided'`), never to the variable. This is intrinsic Handlebars name-resolution (helpers outrank context properties for bare mustaches), not a bug in this slice. The api-test hit it with `area` and fixed it by renaming the column to `loc` (test:151,155 + the NB comment:150). **RULING: documenting the rule + deferring a hard guard to S3b is ACCEPTABLE; it does NOT need to be guarded now.** Engineering rationale:
  - The blast radius is bounded and non-silent at AUTHORING time: a shadowed key renders a wrong/empty clause, which a template author sees immediately in the #6 preview (the same loop S2b's browser-verify exercised). It is not a data-corruption or security path.
  - The right place for the guard is the DESIGNER (reject/warn on save when a columnKey ∈ helper-name set), which is FE work that belongs with the S3b authoring-UX slice that already owns the `{{#eq}}` numeric-footgun note and the FORM_DATA_PATH slug-match caveat (carries 2+3). Bolting a backend 400 onto the layout schema now would be scope-creep into S3b's lane and would need the helper-name set exported as a contract anyway.
  - The reserved-name set is now KNOWABLE (the `registerHelper` object keys + `eq`); S3b can import it directly from helpers.ts for the validator. Documented here so it is not lost.
  **DISPOSITION: collision = KNOWN, documented, designer-side validation DEFERRED to S3b (new carry 5). Not a blocker.**

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit.** Faithful v1 port (spot-checks line-for-line), `str()` makes the trailing-options-arg pattern safe (callRemark 1-arg verified through the default leg), noEscape is the CORRECT decision (plain-text narrative, proto-guards retained, consumer output-encodes), SKIP_KEYS additive. Collision ruled KNOWN+deferred-to-S3b. fieldReports 26/26 + 3 skip. file:lines — helpers.ts:{15,18-24,26-34,67-71,155-171,172-175,212-222,289-328}, render.ts:{3,71-79}, sections.ts:16-31, __tests__/helpers.test.ts (14), render.test.ts:96-108, fieldReports.api.test.ts:150-155.

Independently confirmed: registerHelper block (29 named + `default:defaultHelper`) + the separately-registered `eq` = 31 === the 31-entry SDK `FIELD_REPORT_HELPERS` (diff IDENTICAL). This closes the loop: the collision guard's reserved set provably equals what the engine actually registers, so the guard can neither under- nor over-block. Real guard, not a tautology — it fails if anyone adds/removes a helper without updating the SDK list (the exact drift it's meant to catch). ✓

- **(a) Scope/correctness — CONFIRMED mirrors `attachmentForAccess`.** `fieldPhotoForGeocode` (repository.ts:1407-1438) byte-for-byte reuses the `attachmentForAccess` (1374-1396) scope idiom — same `params=[attachmentId, caseId]`, same `taskScopePredicate(params, scope)`, same `task_id IS NULL OR EXISTS(case_tasks⋈cases WHERE ${pred})` task-leg, `rows[0] ?? null` → svc throws `notFound('FIELD_PHOTO_NOT_FOUND')` (IDOR-safe: out-of-scope id is indistinguishable from absent → 404, test 2250 asserts). ADDS `ca.kind = 'FIELD_PHOTO'` + `deleted_at IS NULL` to the WHERE (1431) — enforces the ADR-0040 FIELD_PHOTO-only rule at the data layer, OFFICE_REF rows return null=404. `resolveFieldPhotoAddress` (service.ts:444-460): frozen-address early return `{address, cached:true}` (never re-resolves, freeze-safe); no-coords → `{address:null, cached:false}` with NO geocode call (test 2236 asserts geocoder uncalled); else reuses cache-first `geocodeService.reverse(lat,lng)`; Google miss (`res.address===null`) → null, nothing persisted (test 2229). ✓
- **(b) Write-through NULL-guarded — CONFIRMED freeze-safe.** `setFieldPhotoReverseGeocodedAddress` (repository.ts:1440-1443): `UPDATE … SET reverse_geocoded_address=$2 WHERE id=$1 AND kind='FIELD_PHOTO' AND reverse_geocoded_address IS NULL`, then re-SELECTs and returns the frozen value (1445-1448) — on a concurrent race the guard no-ops and the SELECT returns the winner's value, never the trigger-blocked one. **Verified this is the ONLY app writer to the column** (grep: 1 hit) → the BEFORE-UPDATE freeze trigger can never be tripped by the app. Trigger logic re-read: blocks only when `OLD.reverse_geocoded_address IS NOT NULL AND NEW IS DISTINCT FROM OLD` → legit soft-delete UPDATE (`SET deleted_at`, address unchanged) passes cleanly. ✓
- **(c) Layering — clean.** Raw SQL confined to repository.ts; cases→geocode cross-module import (`geocodeService` from `../geocode/service.js`, service.ts:28) is one-way pure read/cache (matches the fieldReports→reportLayouts ratchet precedent). No new platform leak; reuses `platform/geocode` seam transitively. ✓
- **(d) Pattern reuse / no dup — CONFIRMED.** Route (routes.ts:49-53) ordered before bare `/:id` (69) AND before the static `/:id/attachments` sibling (66) — `/:id/field-photos/:attachmentId/address` is strictly more specific, no Express shadowing. `parseUuidParam` used for both ids (controller.ts:259-260). Reuses `ReverseGeocodeResult` (sdk/geocode.ts) as the wire shape; SDK `cases.fieldPhotoAddress` (client.ts:644-645) parallels existing `geocode.reverse` (730). ✓
- **(e) Migration — forward-only/idempotent, verified live on test:5433.** `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS`; CHECK dropped-then-added (idempotent); `CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION` + `DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS`/`CREATE`; `CREATE TABLE/INDEX IF NOT EXISTS`. geo CHECK allows NULL (OFFICE_REF inert) else requires numeric lat+lng via `jsonb_typeof` — **confirmed geo_location is jsonb** (the `?` key-test operator is valid). DLQ FK `uuid REFERENCES case_attachments(id) ON DELETE CASCADE` + partial-unique `WHERE replayed_at IS NULL` (one open row/attachment). **psql test:5433: reverse_geocoded_address column ✓, trg_case_attachments_freeze_address ✓, reverse_geocode_dlq regclass ✓, chk_case_attachments_geo_location_shape ✓.** ✓
- **(f) TS-strict — clean.** No `any`/`@ts-`/`eslint-disable` in the diff; repo return types explicit; FE narrows `typeof lat==='number'` before `.toFixed`. ✓

**Gate:** CTO-reported pnpm verify EXIT 0 (modulo documented reportTemplates.api socket-hang rotating flake → cases field-photo 4/4 green isolated); SDK 160/160; openapi regen committed; LIVE :4000 real-Google E2E (first→address+cached:false+persisted+frozen, second→cached:true, #7 list carries reverseGeocodedAddress); browser caption address+GPS(±8m)+capture-time, 0 console errors. Re-verified the 4 tests assert exactly the claimed branches (2207 resolve+freeze+list+cached, 2229 null-result, 2236 no-coords-no-call, 2250 404-IDOR).

**Verdict: PASS — cleared.** Faithful v1-parity port; scope guard re-derived identical to attachmentForAccess + FIELD_PHOTO/deleted_at filter, write-through is the sole column writer and NULL-guarded so the DB freeze is app-untouchable, migration idempotent and verified on test:5433, route ordering sound, no dup. **NOTE (not a blocker):** triple-write to dev:54329 unverifiable this session — dev DB (`crm2_dev`@:54329) not running; the column/trigger/DLQ shipped with foundation commit 3f61598 so dev should already carry mig 0065, but Slice A is uncommitted → confirm dev psql -f + commit Slice A before the slice closes. **Minor (intentional, documented):** `resolveFieldPhotoAddress` hardcodes `cached:false` on the resolve branch, discarding `geocodeService.reverse`'s inner cache flag — here `cached` means "address already frozen on THIS attachment", not "geocode_cache hit"; semantic divergence from the bare `/geocode/reverse` flag, faithful to ADR + E2E. OPEN carry: Slice B (async-on-upload queue/worker/DLQ-insert/replay) + Slice C (#9 CASE_REPORT photo context) not in this diff per ADR build-slice plan; device-must-not-geocode invariant to re-assert on mobile. file:lines — repository.ts:{1407-1438 fieldPhotoForGeocode, 1440-1448 setFieldPhotoReverseGeocodedAddress, 1361-1366 listFieldPhotos +col}, service.ts:{28 import, 444-460 resolveFieldPhotoAddress}, controller.ts:258-266, routes.ts:49-53, sdk/cases.ts:497-499, client.ts:644-645, CaseDetailPage.tsx:1601-1657 (FieldPhotoThumb), mig 0065, ADR-0040, cases.api.test.ts:2207/2229/2236/2250.

## 2026-06-17 — CASE_REPORT S5 Slice 1: assembly engine + /report/preview (ADR-0041) — VERDICT: PASS (2 SHOULD-FIX)

Audited the uncommitted slice against ADR-0041 + the FIELD_REPORT/FIELD_PHOTO precedents. Re-derived every claim against live code.

- **(a) Correctness — clean.** `caseReportService.assemblePreview` (service.ts:25-162): UUID guard → resolveScope → scope-guarded `caseRepository.findById` (404 IDOR-safe) → `Promise.all(detail.tasks.map(fieldReportService.render))` (parallel per-task narrative; preserves order via index) → scope-guarded `listPhotosForReport` → presign each → group by taskId → compose. Single-layer result invariant **HONOURED**: outcome/totals read `t.verificationOutcome` (task) and `detail.verificationOutcome` (case), never an FE-only column (no `task_backend_reviews` reference anywhere in the diff — grep clean). TAT math is correct (`completedAt - createdAt`, clamped ≥0, whole days). The `tasks` array index-maps to `fieldReports[i]!` — safe because `Promise.all` preserves order. ✓
- **(b) Layering / boundaries — clean.** Repo (repository.ts) is the ONLY place doing SQL in the new module (3 raw SQL strings: listPhotosForReport / userName / caseTrigger; grep confirms). Service imports repo + sibling-module services (caseRepository, fieldReportService, reportLayoutRepository) — no controller→repo, no SQL in service. Controller is thin (controller.ts:14-21): actor extract + delegate + next(e). Routes wire `case.view` (routes.ts:63) — ordering OK: `/:id/report/preview` is more specific than the bare `/:id` (line 73) and registered before it; no Express shadowing. `taskScopePredicate` imported from `platform/scope/index.js` (repository.ts:2) — canonical (not from cases/repository). ✓
- **(c) Pattern reuse — exemplary, no reinvention.** Per-task narrative = `fieldReportService.render` (ADR-0039 engine), NOT a re-implementation. Photo scope predicate (repository.ts:25-44) mirrors `cases.repository.listFieldPhotos` (cases/repository.ts:1349-1370) byte-identical: same `kind='FIELD_PHOTO'`, same `deleted_at IS NULL`, same `EXISTS(... WHERE ct.id = ca.task_id AND ${pred})` task-leg. Layout pointer = `reportLayoutRepository.findActiveByConfig(clientId, productId, 'CASE_REPORT')` — same primitive FIELD_REPORT uses (fieldReports/service.ts:29-34). The undefined-verificationType branch (reportLayouts/repository.ts:159 `AND verification_type IS NULL`) matches the new CASE_REPORT shape (mig 0066 enforces `verification_type IS NULL` via chk_report_layouts_shape). ✓
- **(d) Migration — forward-only, idempotent, ADR-faithful.** `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS` × 2; `DROP CONSTRAINT IF EXISTS` then `ADD CONSTRAINT`; the shape CHECK is correctly CASE-disjoint over kind ∈ {FIELD_REPORT, CASE_REPORT, ELSE} — FIELD_REPORT keeps (verification_type+template_body); CASE_REPORT requires (template_body+page_size ∈ {A4,LETTER,LEGAL}+page_orientation ∈ {portrait,landscape}+verification_type IS NULL); ELSE rejects template_body/verification_type/page geometry. The existing `uq_report_layouts_active (client_id, product_id, kind, COALESCE(verification_type,''))` collapses CASE_REPORT's NULL verification_type to '' → one active CASE_REPORT per (client,product), per ADR §1. (DB Auditor will verify live-apply.)
- **(e) TS-strict / no suppressions — CLEAN.** Grep over the new module (caseReports/*.ts + sdk/caseReports.ts + the diff hunks): **zero** `: any`, `@ts-ignore`, `@ts-expect-error`, `eslint-disable`. The two casts `as PageSize` / `as PageOrientation` (service.ts:104-105) are **acceptable**: they live behind a null-guard `layoutRow.pageSize && layoutRow.pageOrientation` AND the DB CHECK constraint guarantees the runtime value is in the type's literal union. The repo SELECTs `page_size, page_orientation` (HEADER_COLS:31) — pg's global snake→camel transform (platform/db.ts:18-19 `camelize`) materializes them as `pageSize`/`pageOrientation` on the typed `ReportLayoutDetail`. Refactor option (not required): widen the SDK type to `string | null` and let the service validate-on-read with the constants — neither cleaner nor stricter than the current cast under the CHECK. ✓
- **(f) API shape — matches ADR.** `GET /api/v2/cases/:id/report/preview` (ADR-0041 §9 slice 1) → `CaseReportContext` envelope. SDK `cases.reportPreview(caseId)` (client.ts:654-655) returns `Promise<CaseReportContext>`. Naming aligned (`preview`, not `report`, because slice 1 is JSON only; the binary endpoint is slice 2's `POST /report?format=…`). No OCC — read-only, correctly absent (confirmed: no `If-Match` header, no `version` in response). ✓
- **(g) Tests — happy-path + layout pointer + 400/404 — present, but coverage gaps.** The 3 tests in caseReports.api.test.ts exercise: (1) full assembly with rendered narrative + 2 photos (one frozen address, one null) + totals + null layout; (2) layout pointer surfaced when configured; (3) bad-uuid→400 + absent→404. The single-task happy path is well-anchored (asserts `task.id`, `verificationType`, exact `narrative` string, sections, photo url shape, captureTime, photoCount=2, totals=zeros, layout=null). The 400/404 test is good — note (3) is a TRUE IDOR-safety test only because it exercises an ID that doesn't exist for any user; a real cross-tenant IDOR test (CLIENT_A's case ID queried by CLIENT_B's executive → 404, NOT 403) would tighten it, but that's not a slice-1 regression risk (the scope guard is `caseRepository.findById`'s, well-tested elsewhere).

- **(h) FINDING #1 — `photosById` is dead code (service.ts:40,54).** The Map is constructed and populated but never read. The grouping by task uses `photosByTask`; presigned photos are never looked up by ID. **Disposition: SHOULD-FIX — remove the dead Map** (3 lines). Not a correctness bug.
- **(i) FINDING #2 — case-level FIELD_PHOTOs (task_id IS NULL) are silently dropped from per-task arrays but counted in `totals.photoCount` (service.ts:55-59, 90).** The grouping loop only buckets photos with a non-null `taskId`; orphans are skipped. But `photoCount: photoRows.length` includes them, so `Σ(task.photos.length) ≤ totals.photoCount` is possible. Per ADR §3 the photo block IS per-task — orphans should not exist for FIELD_PHOTOs (they're always device-uploaded against a task), but the DB CHECK does not enforce `task_id IS NOT NULL` for `kind='FIELD_PHOTO'`. **Disposition: SHOULD-FIX — either (a) drop orphans from the photoCount too (so the totals match the renderable surface), or (b) add a case-level `photos` bucket if the renderer ever wants them.** Pick (a) for slice 1 since renderers only render per-task per ADR. Not a BLOCK because the data invariant holds in prod (device uploads task-bound), but the math drift is a footgun the moment a manual insert lands.
- **(j) NOTE — N+1 scope resolution.** Each `fieldReportService.render(caseId, t.id, actor)` call internally calls `resolveScope(actor)` (fieldReports/service.ts:22) — so a case with N tasks does N+1 scope resolutions (one in assembly, one per task). Not a blocker: scope resolution is typically cached/cheap and the slice 1 happy-path is single-task. Revisit if hot. **Disposition: NOTE, not actionable now.**
- **(k) NOTE — DRY (caseReportRepository.userName + caseTrigger).** Two tiny helpers (4 + 5 lines). The `userName` lookup is the only generation-block source-of-name; the `caseTrigger` (earliest task's trigger) is genuinely case-shaped data not on the CaseDetail. Inlining would put SQL in service.ts (boundary violation). Separate file would be over-modularization for 9 lines. **Current placement is correct — keep as repo helpers.**
- **(l) NOTE — photo ordering divergence.** `caseReportRepository.listPhotosForReport` uses `ORDER BY ca.created_at ASC` (chronological in report) vs `cases.repository.listFieldPhotos`'s `DESC` (latest-first in card). Deliberate per-consumer ordering — keep.

### Coverage RECOMMENDATIONS (additive, not blockers):
1. **Multi-task assembly** — 2 tasks under one case, distinct narratives, distinct photo groupings; assert tasks[].length===2 and photos correctly bucketed.
2. **Photos without a taskId** (orphan FIELD_PHOTO) — currently untested; would surface FINDING #2 either way.
3. **FIELD_REPORT not configured for a verificationType** → assert task.narrative===null (no template, but sections still render) — already a documented degraded path; one assert in the existing test would pin it.
4. **Outcome totals after task completion** — set `case_tasks.verification_outcome` to POSITIVE/NEGATIVE/REFER and assert the four counters increment.

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit AFTER FINDINGS #1 + #2 fix.** Faithful to ADR-0041 §3-§4-§9; pattern reuse exemplary (fieldReportService.render, listFieldPhotos scope predicate, findActiveByConfig); single-layer result invariant honoured (zero FE-column reads); SQL boundary clean; migration shape-correct + ELSE-disjoint; TS-strict + zero suppressions. file:lines — service.ts:{29-30 scope+findById, 33-35 per-task render, 38-60 photos+grouping, 83-91 totals, 94-108 layout, 110-119 TAT}, repository.ts:{25-44 listPhotosForReport, 48-51 userName, 55-61 caseTrigger}, controller.ts:14-21, routes.ts:61-63, sdk/caseReports.ts (full), sdk/reportLayouts.ts:{18,20-27,159-161}, sdk/client.ts:654-655, mig 0066 (shape CHECK lines 24-40), reportLayouts/repository.ts:{31,116,132} (HEADER_COLS+SELECTs add page_size/page_orientation; OK under snake→camel transform). FINDINGS: #1 SHOULD-FIX (dead Map), #2 SHOULD-FIX (orphan-photo total-count drift). No BLOCK. OPEN: slice 2 (Designer) + slice 3 (PDF renderer w/ Puppeteer pool + lint gate on triple-stash) pending.

## 2026-06-17 — CASE_REPORT S5 Slice 2a: HTML render engine + report.html endpoint + FE preview button (ADR-0041 §5/§7/§9) — VERDICT: PASS (no MUST-FIX; 2 NOTEs)

Audited the uncommitted slice (`render.ts` + `render.test.ts` NEW; `service.ts`/`controller.ts`/`cases/routes.ts`/`CaseDetailPage.tsx` MODIFIED). Re-derived every claim against live code; ran both tsc projects (API + web, EXIT 0) and the 5 render unit tests (5 passed).

- **(a) The assemble() refactor — CORRECT, no behavioural drift.** `assemblePreview` → `(await assemble(caseId, actor)).context`; `renderHtml` → `renderCaseReportHtml(context, layoutBody)` (service.ts:27-36). The extraction moved the entire Slice-1 inline body into a free `assemble()` returning `{ context, layoutBody }`. Verified line-by-line against the Slice-1 entry's documented body (UUID-guard → resolveScope → scope-guarded findById/404 → Promise.all per-task render → scope-guarded photos+presign+group → tasks compose → totals → layout pointer → TAT → generation): **byte-equivalent**; the only delta is the added `layoutBody` return computed from the SAME `layout`/`layoutRow` already resolved (no second fetch). FINDINGS #1/#2 from Slice 1 were carried into the fix: the dead `photosById` Map is GONE (service.ts:64 only `photosByTask`), and orphan FIELD_PHOTOs are now `.filter(r => r.taskId !== null)` BEFORE both grouping and `photoCount` (service.ts:60-62, 111) — so Σ(task.photos.length) === totals.photoCount holds. Both prior SHOULD-FIXes resolved. ✓
- **(b) The `{ ... }` inner block — HARMLESS, cosmetic only.** `function assemble(...) { { …body… } }` (service.ts:45-184) is a bare JS block statement (leftover from method-body extraction). Legal JS, no scoping/return effect (the `return` exits the function), tsc EXIT 0 confirms. NOTE not finding — recommend dropping the inner braces for readability but it changes nothing. Not a defect.
- **(c) `layoutBody` resolution — CORRECT.** `layout ? (layoutRow?.templateBody ?? null) : null` (service.ts:183). `layout` is truthy only when `layoutRow && layoutRow.pageSize && layoutRow.pageOrientation` (service.ts:120-129); in that branch `layoutRow` IS the `ReportLayoutDetail` from `findActiveByConfig`, whose `templateBody` (sdk/reportLayouts.ts:158, repo HEADER_COLS:30 selects `template_body`) is the active CASE_REPORT body. So a configured CASE_REPORT layout renders through ITS body; no layout → null → built-in default. The mig-0066 CHECK guarantees a CASE_REPORT row has non-null template_body, so the `?? null` is belt-and-suspenders. ✓
- **(d) render.ts quality — clean, pure, no IO.** Helpers `eq`/`nl2br`/`orDash`/`fmtDate`/`badge` are pure functions, no IO, no SQL, no scope, no proto-walk. `Handlebars.create()` isolates the helper registry (render.ts:19) — no global pollution. The big built-in template is a TS string const (render.ts:55-158) — **consistent with precedent** (fieldReportDefaults are TS consts in the SDK); acceptable for a default, no need for a file. ✓
- **(e) Output-encoding (Security BLOCK-level) — HONOURED.** `hb.compile(body, {strict:false})` with NO `noEscape` → auto-escape ON (engine default). Proto access blocked at call time via the runtime options `allowProtoPropertiesByDefault:false`/`allowProtoMethodsByDefault:false` (render.ts:172-175) — correct Handlebars runtime-option placement (defence-in-depth). The two `SafeString` producers (`nl2br`, `badge`) BOTH `escapeExpression` FIRST then add only structural `<br>`/`<span>` markup (render.ts:30-31, 162-163) — no user input reaches the DOM unescaped. The built-in default has ZERO triple-stash (test pins it). The XSS test proves `<script>`/`<img onerror>`/url-attr-breakout all inert (escaped to entities incl `=`→`&#x3D;`, `"`→`&quot;`). ✓
- **(f) Layering / boundaries — clean.** render.ts = pure render (no SQL, no scope, imports only Handlebars + the SDK type). service orchestrates (assemble + delegate to render). controller is thin (controller.ts:25-33: actor → renderHtml → `res.type('html').send`). Good DRY — the renderer reuses the SAME context the JSON preview returns; no second assembly path. ✓
- **(g) FE button — correct, reuses the canonical helper.** `apiBlob` (the established export-download helper — also used by UsersPage scope-export + ImportModal import-template, sdk.ts:85) carries the Bearer token (a plain `<a href>` couldn't) → `URL.createObjectURL` → `window.open(url,'_blank','noopener')` → `setTimeout(revoke, 60s)` (CaseDetailPage.tsx:1670-1683). The 60s revoke is reasonable: the new tab needs the blob URL live long enough to load the document; 60s is generous-but-bounded (matches the "let the tab load then free memory" pattern). Error path is a `try/catch` → `toast.error(...)` with a `finally{ setBusy(false) }` — busy state can't get stuck. The 3 PDF/Word/Excel buttons are `disabled title="Coming soon"` per ADR slice ordering. ✓
- **(h) Route naming — no Express gotcha.** `GET /:id/report.html` (routes.ts:65) registered BEFORE bare `/:id` (routes.ts:75) and `/:id/report/preview` (routes.ts:63). Express treats `report.html` as a LITERAL path segment (the `.` is regex-special only inside RegExp path patterns, not string paths) → no shadowing of `/:id` or the param routes. The 400/404 API test resolving to the controller confirms the route binds. ✓
- **(i) Test coverage — adequate for 2a; one E2E gap (NOTE).** render.test (5): default render / XSS escape (name+narrative+section) / url-attr escape / **admin layout body renders + still auto-escaped** / no-triple-stash. API (2 new): `report.html` 200 text/html + `<!doctype html>` + 'Verifications' + escaped `<script>` payload; `report.html` 400-bad-uuid / 404-unknown. The admin-body case IS covered in render.test (isolated), but the **API-level `report.html` 200 only exercises the built-in default** (no seeded CASE_REPORT layout) — so the configured-layout-body path end-to-end through the HTTP endpoint (assemble→layoutBody→render→stream) is NOT pinned at the integration level. **Disposition: NOTE — recommend one additive API test seeding an active CASE_REPORT `report_layouts` row and asserting `report.html` renders ITS body (e.g. a sentinel marker), proving the layoutBody wiring in (c) end-to-end.** Not a BLOCK: the wiring is type-checked, the render-side admin-body case is unit-tested, and the layout-pointer surfacing is already API-tested in Slice 1's `surfaces the active CASE_REPORT layout pointer` test (which proves `findActiveByConfig` returns the configured row).
- **(j) TS-strict / no suppressions — CLEAN.** Grep over render.ts/service.ts/controller.ts/render.test.ts: zero `: any`, `@ts-ignore`, `@ts-expect-error`, `eslint-disable`. Both tsc projects EXIT 0.
- **NOTE — SDK header still says "Zod-validated" (caseReports.ts:13-17 / ADR §3) but the context is a plain TS interface, not a runtime Zod schema.** Pre-existing from Slice 1 (the assembly produces the typed object; no runtime validation guards a missing required key → it would render blank rather than 500 as ADR §3 promised). Out of scope for 2a (no new drift); flag for the Slice-1 carry list — if runtime context validation is wanted, it belongs in `assemble()` before render. Not a 2a regression.

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit, no MUST-FIX.** The assemble() refactor preserved Slice-1 behaviour byte-for-byte AND folded in both prior SHOULD-FIXes (dead Map removed; orphan-photo count drift fixed via pre-filter). The inner `{ }` block is harmless cosmetic. layoutBody resolves the active CASE_REPORT body correctly. Output-encoding invariant honoured (auto-escape ON, proto blocked, dual SafeString escape-first, no triple-stash, XSS + url-attr-breakout proven inert). Layering clean (pure renderer / orchestrating service / thin controller). FE reuses the canonical `apiBlob` helper; revoke timing + error path correct. `report.html` route literal-segment, no Express shadowing. TS-strict, zero suppressions, tsc×2 EXIT 0, 5 render tests green. file:lines — render.ts:{19 isolated registry, 22-47 helpers, 55-158 default template, 161-164 badge, 170-176 renderCaseReportHtml}, service.ts:{27-36 facade, 41-184 assemble, 60-62 orphan pre-filter, 120-129 layout, 183 layoutBody}, controller.ts:{25-33 html}, cases/routes.ts:65, CaseDetailPage.tsx:{1664-1713 CaseReportSection, 1670-1683 preview()}. NOTE: (1) inner-brace cleanup (cosmetic); (2) add an API test for the configured-layout-body path end-to-end (additive). OPEN: slice 2 (Designer) + slice 2b/3 (PDF renderer w/ Puppeteer pool + triple-stash lint gate at save).

## 2026-06-17 — CASE_REPORT S5 Slice 2b: Puppeteer PDF via CASE_REPORT background job (ADR-0041 §5/§9 reuse-mapped) — VERDICT: PASS (no MUST-FIX; 1 SHOULD-FIX, 3 NOTEs)

Audited the uncommitted slice against ADR-0041 + the Explore-mapped jobs-engine reuse plan + my Slice-1/2a entries. Re-derived every claim against live code. Ran tsc×2 (API + web, EXIT 0), the real-Puppeteer pdf.test (2 passed: portrait A4 valid `%PDF-` buffer + landscape LETTER with browser-reuse proven — 27s first launch vs 3.6s second). The DB-backed job E2E (`caseReports.api.test`, `describe.skipIf(!RUN)`) needs a live test DB (not provisioned here) — its shape is correct (enqueue→202→awaitAllJobs→SUCCEEDED→result-url) and the suite ran green in the Slice-1/2a E2E env.

- **(a) Reuse-vs-reinvent — CORRECT, the right call. No parallel infra.** CASE_REPORT rides the EXISTING jobs engine end-to-end: `enqueue('CASE_REPORT', payload, userId)` (service.ts:61) → `runJob` (jobs/index.ts:78) → injected processor → `jobRepository.setSucceeded(result)` → presigned download via the UNCHANGED, type-agnostic `jobs/service.resultUrl` (jobs/service.ts:42-51, reads `result.storageKey` for ANY type, own-job-only `getOwned(id,userId)` → 404 IDOR-safe). Mig 0067 ONLY widens `chk_jobs_type` to add `'CASE_REPORT'` — no new table/column. JobsTray widened ONE condition `j.type==='EXPORT'||j.type==='CASE_REPORT'` (JobsTray.tsx:145) reusing the same `download`→`fetchJobResultUrl`→`window.open` path. **The reuse is architecturally justified, not lazy:** I diffed the lifecycle shapes — CASE_REPORT is byte-for-byte EXPORT's (user-initiated · awaited · PENDING→RUNNING→SUCCEEDED|FAILED · progress events · `result={storageKey,filename}` · presigned download · bell `JOB_COMPLETED`+DOWNLOAD action). The geocode queue (geocode/queue.ts) is the OTHER shape — fire-and-forget resolve+persist, NO resultUrl/download/presign/notify (grep-confirmed). So a dedicated geocode-style queue would be the WRONG analog; matching EXPORT is correct. ✓
- **(b) Boundaries — clean, mirrors EXPORT exactly.** `platform/jobs` imports NO feature module (grep: only sdk types + platform deps). The CASE_REPORT processor is injected at the boot layer `http/registerJobs.ts:30` (`registerJobProcessor('CASE_REPORT', caseReportJobProcessor)`) — same seam as EXPORT/IMPORT and the geocode processor injection (lines 27-28,45). `platform/pdf/index.ts` is a PURE wrapper: imports only `puppeteer` (dynamic) + `@crm2/logger` + sdk types `PageSize/PageOrientation` — ZERO feature import (the "trusted HTML in → PDF buffer out" contract is documented at the file head). The processor `modules/caseReports/job.ts` imports platform/pdf + the service + render — correct direction (feature→platform, never reverse). ✓
- **(c) The service↔job import cycle — type-only, ZERO runtime edge.** service.ts:18 `import type { CaseReportJobPayload } from './job.js'` (erased at compile); job.ts:5 `import { caseReportService } from './service.js'` (runtime). So exactly ONE runtime edge (job→service); no runtime cycle. tsc EXIT 0 confirms the type-only import resolves. The payload interface living in job.ts (next to the processor that consumes it) is the natural home; importing it as a type into the enqueuer is clean. ✓
- **(d) Actor-in-payload — SOUND, with a noted minor staleness.** `enqueueReport` puts `{caseId, actor:{role,userId}}` in the payload (service.ts:60); the worker re-resolves scope via `assemble`→`caseRepository.findById(caseId, scope)` where `scope=resolveScope(actor)`. This is a STRONGER posture than EXPORT (which stores only `actorId` and re-derives) but still server-created (actor comes from `req.auth`, controller.ts:7-10 — never client-supplied), so no privilege-injection vector. **Staleness:** if the user's role changes between enqueue and run, the worker uses the SNAPSHOT role in the payload, not the live role. Direction matters: a DOWNGRADE between enqueue+run means the report could contain rows the user can no longer see (the report is generated against stale-elevated scope). For a report this is acceptable (the window is seconds-to-minutes, the artifact is owner-only-downloadable, and EXPORT has the identical class of issue since it captured the query at enqueue). **Disposition: NOTE — acceptable; if ever tightened, re-resolve from `userId` (re-fetch role) at run instead of trusting payload.role, matching EXPORT's actorId-only pattern.** Recommend EXPORT-parity (store userId, re-fetch role) for the next hardening pass — not a blocker.
- **(e) The platform/jobs title maps — clean, type-forced.** `DONE_TITLE`/`FAIL_TITLE` are `Record<JobType,string>` (jobs/index.ts:63-72) so adding `'CASE_REPORT'` to `JOB_TYPES` (sdk/jobs.ts:9) made the maps a compile error until filled — exactly the exhaustiveness guarantee you want; both got correct strings. `DOWNLOAD_TYPES: ReadonlySet<JobType> = {'EXPORT','CASE_REPORT'}` (line 75) replaces the prior `type==='EXPORT'` ternary at the notify `actionType` (line 106). Set-membership is the right generalization for a 2nd downloadable type. ✓
- **(f) assemble() exposure — acceptable, NOT a smell.** The free function `assemble()` (service.ts:67) stayed private; the object gained a public method `assemble` (service.ts:49) that DELEGATES (`return assemble(caseId, actor)`). Two names, ONE implementation — the method is a thin published surface so the processor gets `{context, layoutBody}` without re-deriving layoutBody. `assemblePreview` (returns only `.context`) and `renderHtml` (assembles+renders) are the other two facades over the same core. This is a deliberate facade trio over one engine, not duplication. The shadowing (method name === function name) is legal and reads fine given the one-line delegate. Keep. ✓
- **(g) The concurrency gate (pdf/index.ts:51-65) — hand-rolled, CORRECT.** No `p-limit` in the tree (grep-confirmed) → hand-rolling is fine if correct. I traced the invariant: `acquire()` increments `active` ONLY on the fast path OR after a waiter wakes (NOT before sleeping); `release()` decrements THEN wakes the next waiter (`waiters.shift()?.()`). At saturation (active=6): a 7th caller pushes a waiter, active stays 6; on `release()` active→5 then the waiter wakes and does active++→6. Net: `active` never exceeds `PDF_MAX_CONCURRENCY=6`, FIFO order preserved, no double-count, no lost wakeup (the resolve is captured in the closure). The `finally{release()}` (line 101-103) runs even on render throw, so a failed render frees its slot — no leak. Browser is promise-cached + relaunched on `disconnected` (crash/OOM resilience), failed launch un-caches (line 44-47). Page always `.close()` in `finally` (line 98-100). Hard timeouts on setContent(30s)+pdf(60s) so a hung render fails the JOB not the worker. Reliability/SRE owns the OOM posture; correctness is sound. ✓
- **(h) TS-strict / suppressions — CLEAN.** Grep over pdf/index.ts + job.ts + service.ts + repository.ts: ZERO `: any`, `as any`, `@ts-ignore`, `@ts-expect-error`, `eslint-disable`. The `row.taskId!` non-null assertions (service.ts:100, and the earlier filter at :85) are JUSTIFIED: TS does not narrow through `.filter(r => r.taskId !== null)` (no user-defined type predicate), so the `!` is the canonical idiom AFTER a value-guard that provably excludes null — the runtime value is non-null by construction. The two `as PageSize/as PageOrientation` casts in `assemble` are the pre-existing Slice-1 ones (under the mig-0066 CHECK + null-guard), unchanged. tsc×2 EXIT 0. ✓
- **(i) Test coverage — adequate.** pdf.test (2): REAL render portrait-A4 (asserts `%PDF-` magic + >500 bytes) + landscape-LETTER (proves browser reuse via the launch-time delta). caseReports.api (2 new): full job E2E (enqueue→`type==='CASE_REPORT'`+202→`awaitAllJobs`→SUCCEEDED→`result.storageKey` matches `^case-reports/.+\.pdf$`→`result.filename` matches `^report-CASE-.+\.pdf$`→result-url 200) running REAL in-process Puppeteer, AND the 400-bad-uuid/404-out-of-scope fail-fast at enqueue. The E2E covering enqueue→worker→store→presign in one test is strong. **Missing: a FAILED-job-path assertion** (processor throws → job FAILED → JOB_FAILED notify → result-url 400 `JOB_NO_ARTIFACT`). Hard to force without injecting a crash (the real render rarely fails on trusted HTML); the generic FAILED path is already covered by the EXPORT "unregistered resource fails + result-url 400s" test (jobs.api.test:114) which exercises the SAME `runJob` catch + `setFailed` + notify branch — so the engine-level failure handling is pinned, just not CASE_REPORT-specific. **Disposition: acceptable to skip the CASE_REPORT-specific FAILED test for 2b; NOTE it for hardening.** ✓
- **(j) FLAG-1 reconciliation (repository.ts:31-41) — CORRECT + SAFE; genuinely fixes the asymmetry.** `listPhotosForReport` DROPPED the per-task `EXISTS(... AND ${taskScopePredicate})` leg; the query is now `WHERE ca.case_id=$1 AND ca.kind='FIELD_PHOTO' AND ca.deleted_at IS NULL` (case-scoped, `caseId` the only param). **Correctness verdict: this is right.** The access gate IS case visibility, enforced upstream identically on BOTH paths — `assemble`→`caseRepository.findById(caseId, scope)` (404) and `enqueueReport`→`caseRepository.caseVisible(caseId, scope)` (404), and I verified `caseVisible` (cases/repository.ts:1212-1220) uses the SAME `caseScopePredicate` as `findById`. Since `findById` returns ALL tasks of a visible case (tasks aren't individually re-scoped), the OLD per-task photo predicate was STRICTER than the surrounding task surface: a colleague's task on a case I can legitimately see rendered 0 photos while STILL counting in `totals.photoCount` (Σ(task.photos) < photoCount). Case-scoping the photo read realigns the photo surface with the task surface — and combined with the Slice-2a orphan pre-filter (`.filter(r => r.taskId !== null)`, service.ts:85,134), the invariant Σ(task.photos.length) === totals.photoCount now provably holds for any visible case. The comment (repository.ts:24-30) documents the rationale faithfully and correctly distinguishes this from the #7 card's deliberately per-task `listFieldPhotos`. Security owns the IDOR re-derivation; on CORRECTNESS this fix is sound and the math no longer drifts. ✓
- **NOTE — HTTP shape deviates from ADR §6/§9 Slice-3 (DOCUMENTED + better).** ADR §6 specs `POST /:caseId/report?format=pdf` STREAMING the binary synchronously (Puppeteer pool inline on the request). The implementation instead does `POST /:id/report` → 202 + JobView → async job → presigned download (controller.ts:41-49, routes.ts:67). This is the Explore-mapped reuse plan, NOT a regression: a synchronous Puppeteer render on the request thread would block an HTTP worker for seconds and couple report latency to request timeouts — the async job is the correct posture for a 1-5s render and reuses the proven EXPORT lifecycle + tray UX. Mig-0067's own comment records this decision. **Disposition: NOTE — ADR §6/§9-Slice-3 text is now stale vs the shipped async-job design; recommend a one-line ADR amendment so the doc matches (the binary-stream `?format=` shape was superseded by the jobs-engine reuse).**
- **NOTE — `report.html` (slice 2a, public-ish render) and the PDF job render the SAME HTML via `renderCaseReportHtml`** (job.ts:32, service.renderHtml:44) — good DRY, the auto-escape invariant is enforced once. The PDF page-geometry falls back to `DEFAULT_PDF_PAGE_SIZE='A4'`/`'portrait'` (render.ts:5-6) when `context.layout` is null — matches the built-in-default-layout path. ✓

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit, no MUST-FIX.** CASE_REPORT correctly REUSES the jobs engine (enqueue/runJob/worker), the jobs table (mig 0067 widens the type CHECK only), the type-agnostic owner-scoped `resultUrl` download, and the JobsTray DOWNLOAD path — zero parallel infra, and reuse is the architecturally RIGHT call (CASE_REPORT === EXPORT's lifecycle, ≠ geocode's fire-and-forget). Boundaries clean (platform/jobs feature-free; processor injected at boot; platform/pdf a pure wrapper; service↔job cycle is type-only/zero-runtime-edge). Actor-in-payload is server-created + re-resolved at run (sound; minor downgrade-staleness NOTEd, EXPORT-parity recommended). Title maps type-forced; DOWNLOAD_TYPES set clean; assemble() facade trio is one engine not dup; hand-rolled concurrency gate traced CORRECT (FIFO, no over-admit, slot freed on throw, page+browser leak-safe, hard timeouts). TS-strict, zero suppressions, `taskId!` justified post-filter, tsc×2 EXIT 0, real-Puppeteer pdf.test 2/2 green. FLAG-1 case-scoping is correct + safe + actually heals the Σ(photos)===photoCount asymmetry (gate = case visibility, enforced identically via findById/caseVisible on the same predicate). file:lines — pdf/index.ts:{28-49 browser cache+relaunch, 51-65 concurrency gate, 83-104 htmlToPdf, 98-100 page close, 107-112 closePdfBrowser}, caseReports/job.ts:{25-49 processor, 41 storageKey}, service.ts:{49-51 assemble facade, 56-62 enqueueReport gate}, repository.ts:{20-41 listPhotosForReport FLAG-1}, jobs/index.ts:{63-75 title maps+DOWNLOAD_TYPES, 78-121 runJob}, jobs/service.ts:42-51 resultUrl, registerJobs.ts:30, sdk/jobs.ts:9, sdk/client.ts:659, JobsTray.tsx:{83-90,145-153}, CaseDetailPage.tsx:1688-1726, mig 0067. SHOULD-FIX: none code-blocking — (1) amend ADR §6/§9-Slice-3 to the async-job shape (doc drift). NOTEs: (a) actor downgrade-staleness → EXPORT-parity (store userId, re-fetch role at run); (b) add a CASE_REPORT-specific FAILED-job test (engine-level failure already covered by EXPORT's). No BLOCK. OPEN: slice 2 (Designer + triple-stash lint gate at save) + slices 4/5 (docx/xlsx renderers).

## 2026-06-17 — CASE_REPORT S5 Slice 3: Designer (CASE_REPORT branch) + schema refine refactor + `{{{` gate + single-source template move (ADR-0041 §9 slice 3) — VERDICT: PASS (no MUST-FIX; 2 SHOULD-FIX, 2 NOTEs)

Audited the uncommitted slice against ADR-0041 §9-slice-3 + mig-0066's `chk_report_layouts_shape` + my S1/2a/2b entries. Re-derived every claim against live code. Ran tsc×3 (SDK + API + web, ALL EXIT 0), SDK reportLayouts.test (26/26 green), render.test (5/5 green — proves the single-source template move didn't break the re-export importer).

- **(a) `refineLayoutShape` — CORRECT, matches the DB CHECK byte-for-byte over all 5 kinds; ZERO Zod-accepts-DB-rejects gap.** Walked the disjunction (reportLayouts.ts:248-289 vs mig-0066:26-42): **CASE_REPORT** → Zod {no type, body required, pageSize required, pageOrientation required, colCount===0} ; DB {vt NULL, body NOT NULL, page_size∈{A4,LETTER,LEGAL}, page_orientation∈{portrait,landscape}} — page enums enforced by `z.enum(REPORT_PAGE_SIZES/ORIENTATIONS)` at the field, columns aren't a DB-CHECK concern (separate `report_layout_columns` table) so the Zod col-0 rule is a strict superset, no DB conflict. **FIELD_REPORT** → Zod {type req, body req, no page, ≥1 col} ; DB {vt NOT NULL/≠'', body NOT NULL, page NULL} — aligned (`hasPage` rejects any page geometry). **MIS/DATA_ENTRY/BILLING_MIS** (ELSE) → Zod {no type, no body, no page, ≥1 col} ; DB {vt NULL, body NULL, page NULL} — aligned. **No kind-combination the Zod refine admits that the DB CHECK then rejects (→ would be a 500).** The trim-vs-raw edge is closed UPSTREAM of refine: `templateBodySchema` is `.trim().min(1)`, so a whitespace-only body fails the FIELD-level parse (400) before it can reach an ELSE-kind's `hasBody` check or the repo INSERT — no `template_body='   '` ever hits the `template_body IS NULL` DB CHECK. ✓
- **(b) The `.min(1)` move — CORRECT, no column-min regression.** `layoutColumnsSchema` dropped its array `.min(1)` (reportLayouts.ts:213-227, now only `.max(200)` + dup-key superRefine); the per-kind minimum moved into `refineLayoutShape` (`if (colCount < 1) issue(...)` for every non-CASE_REPORT kind, line 288). Empty columns are STILL rejected for MIS/DATA_ENTRY/BILLING_MIS/FIELD_REPORT, and now ALLOWED (required ===0) for CASE_REPORT — exactly the intent. **SDK test pins it**: `{...base(MIS), columns:[]}` → `success===false` (reportLayouts.test.ts:83) AND `{...cr, columns:[col()]}` → false (line 143). The dup-key check survives in the array schema (correct — it's column-set-internal, kind-independent). ✓
- **(c) Single-source template move — CLEAN re-export, no duplicate-binding, no drift.** `DEFAULT_CASE_REPORT_TEMPLATE` + `DEFAULT_PDF_PAGE_SIZE/ORIENTATION` + `CASE_REPORT_VARIABLE_CATALOG` now live in `@crm2/sdk` (caseReports.ts:6-7,128-298). render.ts:2 `import { DEFAULT_CASE_REPORT_TEMPLATE }` (local binding, used at render.ts:64) THEN render.ts:6 `export { … DEFAULT_CASE_REPORT_TEMPLATE } from '@crm2/sdk'` (a separate re-export, NOT a local re-declaration) → no TS duplicate-binding error (tsc EXIT 0 confirms). render.test.ts:3 still imports it from `../render.js` and the re-export keeps it resolving (5/5 green; line 136 asserts no `{{{`). job.ts:6 imports `DEFAULT_PDF_*` from `./render.js` — also via the re-export. **The renderer (render.ts:64), the FE Designer (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:12,450), and the PDF job (job.ts:36-37) all read the ONE SDK copy** — drift-proof. ✓
- **(d) Repo persistence — param indices CORRECT, OCC-guarded, immutable-once-used untripped.** create() INSERT `(…template_body, page_size, page_orientation, created_by, updated_by) VALUES ($1..$8,$9,$9)` with params [clientId,$1 … templateBody,$6 pageSize,$7 pageOrientation,$8 userId,$9] — page_size=$7/page_orientation=$8, $9 reused for both audit cols. ✓ update() `SET … template_body=COALESCE($4,…), page_size=COALESCE($5,…), page_orientation=COALESCE($6,…)` with params [id,$1 name,$2 userId,$3 templateBody,$4 pageSize,$5 pageOrientation,$6] — indices correct (repository.ts:240-254). HEADER_COLS + the list/findHeader SELECTs carry page_size/page_orientation (S1 add). Update is OCC-guarded via `cur.version !== expectedVersion → AppError.stale` (line 226). The immutable-once-used guard (`SELECT 1 FROM case_data_entries`) gates ONLY column changes (`if (patch.columns)`, line 229) — CASE_REPORT layouts have no data-entry rows, so even when the FE sends `columns:[]` the guard query returns empty and never trips. ✓
- **(e) FE Designer CASE_REPORT branch — correct.** `isCaseReport` → `hasColumns=false` (line 144), so the column editor block (line 501 `{hasColumns && …}`) is hidden; the CASE_REPORT block (411-499) renders page-size + orientation pickers, the HTML body textarea, the live `hasTripleStash` warning (463-468), and the variable catalog (478-496). `canSave` for CASE_REPORT = `name≠'' && (!hasColumns short-circuits the column gate) && (isEdit||client&product) && (!isCaseReport || (body≠'' && !hasTripleStash))` (263-271) — body+no-`{{{`, NOT columns. ✓ Save sends `columns:[]` + `templateBody` + `pageSize` + `pageOrientation` on BOTH create (219) and update (210). Edit-hydration sets pageSize/pageOrientation from `detail.data` (156-157, guarded `if (d.pageSize)`). **Kind is immutable on edit** (the Kind `<select disabled={isEdit}>`, line 326) AND client/product/verificationType are too — so an existing FIELD_REPORT can NOT be switched to CASE_REPORT through the API (kind not in UpdateReportLayoutSchema). On CREATE, switching kind mid-form leaves stale `rows`/`templateBody` in state, but the submit payload is kind-gated (CASE_REPORT sends `columns:[]` regardless of stale rows; ELSE kinds omit templateBody) so **no stale value corrupts the request** — verified the create branch (212-220). ✓
- **(f) TS-strict / suppressions / `any` — CLEAN.** Grep over all 8 slice-3 files: zero `: any` / `as any` / `@ts-ignore` / `@ts-expect-error` / `eslint-disable` (the one "any" hit is the word in a test-description string). The FE `as PageSize`/`as PageOrientation` casts (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:419,433) are on `<select>` onChange over the `REPORT_PAGE_SIZES/ORIENTATIONS` literal option lists — the value provably belongs to the union. tsc×3 EXIT 0. ✓
- **(g) Test coverage — adequate.** SDK 26 (CASE_REPORT: valid shape / missing body|pageSize|pageOrientation / columns-or-vt rejected / bad page enums / **`{{{` rejected on create AND update** / page geometry on non-CASE rejected / page-geometry update accepted). API test (1 new, +49 lines): create CASE_REPORT 201 → assert kind/pageSize/pageOrientation/verificationType=null/columns=[] → read-back via `by-config` (type-less resolve) → `{{{` 400 on create AND on update → page-orientation update 200 via OCC. The "existing FIELD_REPORT → CASE_REPORT" case is **correctly untested because it's impossible** (kind immutable on update — confirmed (e)). ✓
- **FINDING #1 — SHOULD-FIX (benign no-op write on CASE_REPORT update).** The FE sends `columns:[]` on a CASE_REPORT *edit* (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:204-211). `UpdateReportLayoutSchema.columns` is `.optional()` → `validated.columns===[]` (not undefined) → service includes `columns:[]` in the patch (service.ts:115) → repo `if (patch.columns)` is **truthy for `[]`** (repository.ts:229) → runs the `case_data_entries` in-use SELECT + `DELETE FROM report_layout_columns` + empty insertColumns. All no-ops for CASE_REPORT (no columns, no data-entries) so **harmless and correct**, but it's a wasted SELECT+DELETE per CASE_REPORT body/page edit. **Disposition: SHOULD-FIX — either have the FE omit `columns` on a CASE_REPORT update (only send it for column kinds), or guard `if (patch.columns?.length)` / `if (patch.columns && patch.columns.length)` in the repo.** Not a BLOCK (idempotent no-op, no data loss).
- **FINDING #2 — SHOULD-FIX (UpdateReportLayoutSchema has NO per-kind coherence refine).** Unlike Create, `UpdateReportLayoutSchema` (reportLayouts.ts:313-329) does NOT call `refineLayoutShape` — it only checks "≥1 mutable field present". This is **safe today** because kind/verificationType are immutable (not in the schema) so an update can't violate the kind↔shape contract that the DB CHECK still enforces, AND the per-field schemas (`templateBodySchema` `{{{`-gate, page enums) still apply. But it means e.g. an update could send `pageSize` to a FIELD_REPORT layout and Zod would accept it → the repo COALESCEs it onto a FIELD_REPORT row → **the DB CHECK `page_size IS NULL` for FIELD_REPORT would reject it as a 500-class write error** (it surfaces via `mapWriteError`'s `throw e` fallthrough, NOT a clean 400). The FE never does this (it only sends page geometry for CASE_REPORT), so it's not reachable through the UI, but a direct API caller with `report_template.manage` could trip it. **Disposition: SHOULD-FIX — gate page-geometry/templateBody on update by the row's kind (fetch kind in the service or add a refine that rejects page geometry unless the target is CASE_REPORT), OR map the CHECK-violation pg error (23514) to a 400 in `mapWriteError` so a hostile patch returns a clean 400 not a 500.** Not a BLOCK: unreachable via the shipped FE, gated behind an admin-only perm.
- **NOTE — `hasTripleStash` FE warning is CASE_REPORT-only in `canSave` but the server bans `{{{` on ALL bodies.** `canSave` blocks `{{{` only for CASE_REPORT (line 271); a FIELD_REPORT body with `{{{` passes FE canSave then gets a clean 400 from `templateBodySchema` (server authoritative). Acceptable — pre-existing FIELD_REPORT behaviour, server is the gate; the FE could mirror the warning for FIELD_REPORT too (cosmetic).
- **NOTE — page geometry pickers default to A4/portrait (`DEFAULT_PDF_*`) on a fresh CASE_REPORT** (ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:135-136) — sensible, matches the renderer's no-layout fallback (render/job.ts), so a Designer-created CASE_REPORT and the built-in default render at the same geometry unless changed. ✓

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit, no MUST-FIX, no BLOCK.** `refineLayoutShape` faithfully mirrors the mig-0066 CHECK over all 5 kinds with ZERO Zod-accepts/DB-rejects gap on the create path (trim-vs-raw edge closed upstream by `templateBodySchema.trim().min(1)`). The `.min(1)→per-kind-refine` move preserves the column-min for all 4 column/FIELD kinds and correctly admits col-0 for CASE_REPORT (SDK test pins both directions). Single-source template move is a clean re-export — no duplicate-binding, renderer+Designer+PDF-job all read the ONE SDK copy, render.test's `../render.js` import still resolves (drift-proof). Repo param indices correct ($7/$8 create, $4/$5/$6 update COALESCE), OCC-guarded, immutable-once-used untripped for CASE_REPORT. FE Designer hides columns, shows page+body+catalog+Load-default, `canSave` is body+no-`{{{` (not columns), edit-hydrates page geometry, kind immutable on edit (FIELD→CASE impossible — correctly untested), no stale-state payload corruption on mid-form kind switch. TS-strict, zero suppressions, tsc×3 EXIT 0, SDK 26/26 + render 5/5 green. file:lines — sdk/reportLayouts.ts:{213-227 layoutColumnsSchema (.min(1) dropped), 234-242 templateBodySchema+`{{{` gate, 248-289 refineLayoutShape, 291-307 Create+superRefine, 313-329 Update (no refine)}, sdk/caseReports.ts:{6-7 DEFAULT_PDF_*, 128-185 VARIABLE_CATALOG, 195-298 DEFAULT_CASE_REPORT_TEMPLATE}, caseReports/render.ts:{2 import, 6 re-export, 64 use}, reportLayouts/repository.ts:{178-192 create INSERT $7/$8, 229-239 cols-only in-use guard, 240-254 update COALESCE $4/$5/$6}, reportLayouts/service.ts:{105-119 update patch}, ReportLayoutsPage.tsx:{135-157 state+hydrate, 144 hasColumns, 185-221 save, 263-271 canSave, 411-499 CASE_REPORT branch}, mig-0066:26-42 CHECK. SHOULD-FIX: #1 benign `columns:[]` no-op write on CASE_REPORT update (FE omit or repo `?.length` guard); #2 UpdateReportLayoutSchema lacks a kind-coherence refine → a direct admin API caller patching page-geometry onto a FIELD_REPORT would hit a 500-class CHECK violation (unreachable via FE) — gate by kind or map pg 23514→400. NOTEs: (a) FE `{{{` warning CASE_REPORT-only (server bans all bodies — cosmetic); (b) page pickers default A4/portrait = renderer fallback. No BLOCK. OPEN: slices 4/5 (docx/xlsx renderers).

## 2026-06-17 — CASE_REPORT S5 Slice 4: docx renderer + CASE_REPORT `format` parameterization (ADR-0041 §9 slice 4, re-shaped) — VERDICT: PASS (no MUST-FIX; 2 NOTEs)

Audited the staged slice against ADR-0041 §9-slice-4 + my S1/2a/2b/3 entries. ADR speced slice 4 as a SEPARATE "DOCX JobType (same shape as CASE_REPORT/PDF)"; the CTO instead parameterized the EXISTING `CASE_REPORT` JobType with a `format` payload field. Re-derived every claim against live code. Ran tsc×2 (API + web, EXIT 0); docx.test 2/2 green (valid 9.3KB zip + XSS-inert). docx@9.7.1 d.ts inspected directly. New `docx.ts`; changed `job.ts`/`service.ts`/`controller.ts`/`sdk/caseReports.ts`/`sdk/client.ts`/`CaseDetailPage.tsx`/tests/package.json.

- **(a) The format-parameterization decision — RIGHT CALL, strictly better than the ADR's 3-JobType design.** ONE `CASE_REPORT` JobType + a `format` payload field vs three JobTypes (CASE_REPORT/DOCX/XLSX). The 3-JobType design would have BLOATED: `JOB_TYPES` (sdk/jobs.ts) → 3 entries → 3 rows each in the type-forced `DONE_TITLE`/`FAIL_TITLE` `Record<JobType,string>` maps + the `DOWNLOAD_TYPES` set + the `chk_jobs_type` CHECK; the JobsTray condition would grow to a 3-way OR; and you'd register 3 near-identical processors. The parameterized design keeps ONE processor (job.ts), ONE tray label, ONE download path, and distinguishes the artifact purely by extension/MIME — the format is a property of the SAME report job, not a different kind of job. This is the correct DRY axis (the lifecycle is identical across formats; only the final sink differs — exactly the "one assembly engine, N sinks" the ADR §Positive itself states). The branch lives at the one place it must (the render step, job.ts:26-32). **Architecturally cleaner than what the ADR text proposed; recommend a one-line ADR §9 amendment recording that slices 4/5 are `format=` params on CASE_REPORT, not new JobTypes (companion to the slice-2b §6 async-shape drift NOTE).** ✓
- **(b) Back-compat — PRESERVED, verified two ways.** (1) controller `reportFormat(req)` returns `'pdf'` when `req.query.format === undefined` (controller.ts:14-21) → the slice-2b bare `POST /:id/report` (no query) still enqueues a pdf job unchanged. (2) SDK `generateReport(caseId, format = 'pdf')` defaults the param (client.ts:659-660) → any existing caller passing one arg is byte-identical to before. (3) An IN-FLIGHT slice-2b job enqueued BEFORE this deploy has a payload WITHOUT `format` → the processor reads `format` as `undefined` → `format === 'docx'` is false → falls to the pdf branch (job.ts:28-32); BUT `storageKey`/`filename` would then interpolate `.${undefined}` → `.undefined` and `MIME[undefined]` → `undefined` content-type. **This is a real edge but NOT reachable in practice:** jobs are processed within seconds of enqueue (in-process in dev, worker tier in prod) so the enqueue→deploy→run straddle window is effectively nil, and the dev env (per project context) drains its queue continuously. The validation gate at the controller guarantees every NEW job carries a valid format. **Disposition: NOTE — if a durable queue (Redis/BullMQ) could hold a pre-deploy payload across the upgrade, add `const format = (payload.format ?? 'pdf')` defensive-default at the processor; for the current in-process/fast-drain posture it's not a defect.** ✓ (the bad-format path itself is correctly a 400 — `?format=exe` → `AppError.badRequest`, API-tested.)
- **(c) docx.ts quality — clean pure builder, correct structure.** Pure function `CaseReportContext → Buffer`: NO SQL, NO scope, NO repo import (imports only `docx`, `@crm2/logger`, sdk types). Helpers are small + single-purpose: `dash`/`fmtDate` (null→'—' formatters), `kvRow`/`gridTable`/`cell`/`headerCell` (table primitives), `narrativeParagraphs` (line-split), `taskBlock` (per-task heading+meta+narrative+section-tables+photos). Document assembled top-down (header → Case kv-table → Applicants grid → per-task Verifications → totals footer). Mirrors the HTML renderer's section order (drift-resistant by reading the SAME context). Reasonable + idiomatic. ✓
- **(d) docx 9.x API usage — CORRECT, verified against the installed d.ts.** `Document({creator,title,sections:[{children}]})`, `Packer.toBuffer(doc)`, `Paragraph({heading:HeadingLevel.*, children:[TextRun]})`, `Table({width:{size,type:WidthType.PERCENTAGE}, rows, borders:{...BorderStyle.SINGLE}})`, `TableCell`/`TableRow`, `ImageRun({data, type, transformation})` — all match docx@9.7.1 (`dist/index.d.ts`). **`Packer.toBuffer` is typed `Promise<Buffer>` (d.ts:2435)** — so the `Buffer.from(buf)` wrap (docx.ts:249) is REDUNDANT (a Buffer wrapping a Buffer is a copy, harmless, ~no cost at report scale). Not a defect; could drop it. The `ImageRun.type` field is REQUIRED in 9.x and typed `"jpg"|"png"|"gif"|"bmp"` (d.ts:2622) — the code's `'jpg'|'png'` is a valid SUBSET, so passing the content-type-sniffed value type-checks and is correct for 9.x (older docx inferred type from bytes; 9.x mandates it). ✓
- **(e) Image fetch — sequential N-fetch in a background job, ACCEPTABLE; degrade correct.** `fetchImage` is `await`ed per-photo inside the `for (const photo of task.photos)` loop in `taskBlock` (docx.ts:122-123) → N SEQUENTIAL network GETs for a task with N photos (and tasks themselves run sequentially in `renderCaseReportDocx`, docx.ts:221). For a LATENCY-CRITICAL request path this would be a smell; but this runs on the WORKER tier inside a background job whose whole point is to absorb multi-second work off the request thread (same rationale as the slice-2b Puppeteer async-job decision). Each fetch is bounded by a 15s AbortController timeout (docx.ts:82-85) so a hung object-store can't wedge the worker indefinitely. **Could parallelize** (`Promise.all(task.photos.map(fetchImage))` then assemble in order) to cut wall-time for photo-heavy cases — a reasonable future optimization — **but per instruction this is NOT a block.** Graceful degrade is CORRECT: `fetchImage` returns `null` on `!res.ok` OR any throw (timeout/abort/network) → the `if (img)` guard (docx.ts:124) skips the `ImageRun` and the caption-only `Paragraph` still emits (docx.ts:137-145) → one bad photo never fails the report. **Disposition: NOTE — sequential fetch acceptable for a background job; parallelize if photo-heavy cases get slow.** ✓
- **(f) Boundaries — CONFIRMED clean.** `renderCaseReportDocx` is imported ONLY by `job.ts` (the processor) — grep over `apps/api/src` returns exactly job.ts + docx.ts(self) + its test (no other consumer). The processor is injected at boot (`http/registerJobs.ts`, unchanged seam from slice 2b). `platform/jobs/*` imports NEITHER docx.ts NOR caseReports (grep clean) → the platform engine stays feature-agnostic. Import direction is feature→platform (docx.ts→`docx` pkg + logger; job.ts→platform/pdf + platform/storage + the renderers) — never reversed. ✓
- **(g) MIME map + extension — clean, type-forced.** `MIME: Record<CaseReportFormat,string>` (job.ts:21-24) is exhaustiveness-forced — adding `'xlsx'` to `CASE_REPORT_FORMATS` makes this a compile error until an entry is added (same guarantee as the slice-2b title maps). `storageKey`/`filename` use `.${format}` (job.ts:42,47) so the extension always tracks the format; `put(storageKey, bytes, MIME[format])` sets the right content-type for the presigned download. ✓
- **(h) TS-strict / suppressions / `any` — CLEAN.** Grep over docx.ts + job.ts + service.ts + controller.ts + sdk/caseReports.ts + sdk/client.ts: ZERO `: any`, `as any`, `@ts-ignore`, `@ts-expect-error`, `eslint-disable`. The controller's `(CASE_REPORT_FORMATS as readonly string[]).includes(raw)` cast (controller.ts:17) is the canonical idiom for membership-testing a `readonly [...] as const` tuple against an arbitrary string (TS's `.includes` on a literal tuple rejects a `string` arg) — narrows correctly to `CaseReportFormat` via the subsequent `as CaseReportFormat` only after the runtime membership check proves it. tsc×2 EXIT 0. ✓
- **(i) Test coverage — adequate; image path is E2E-only (noted + acceptable).** docx.test (2): valid `.docx` → `Buffer.isBuffer` + `>1000 bytes` + PK\x03\x04 zip-magic; XSS-inert → malicious `<script>` customerName + `<b>` narrative → still valid zip AND `buf.includes('<script>alert(1)</script>') === false` (proves the OOXML serializer entity-encodes the text run — structural output-encoding, ADR §5/§7 honoured for the docx sink with NO HTML at all). api.test (+2 reshaped): `?format=docx` → enqueue 202 + `type==='CASE_REPORT'` → `awaitAllJobs` → SUCCEEDED + `storageKey` `/^case-reports\/.+\.docx$/` + `filename` `/^report-CASE-.+\.docx$/` + `result.format==='docx'`; and bad-format `?format=exe` → 400 (alongside bad-uuid 400 + out-of-scope 404). **The docx UNIT test uses `photos:[]` to avoid a network fetch (commented at docx.test.ts:49), so the `fetchImage`→`ImageRun` embed path is exercised ONLY by the live E2E** (which seeds a real case and runs the in-process worker against real presigned bytes). Acceptable + explicitly noted: the embed branch is small, type-checked, and the degrade-to-null path is structurally simple; a unit test could mock `fetch` but the live E2E is the higher-fidelity proof. The XSS-inert unit test is the load-bearing security pin and it runs without network. ✓
- **(j) Reusability for xlsx (slice 5) — the shape SCALES cleanly.** Adding the 3rd format is exactly: (1) append `'xlsx'` to `CASE_REPORT_FORMATS` (sdk) → this ALONE forces compile errors at `MIME` (must add the spreadsheetml content-type) — the type system drives the checklist; (2) add a `format === 'xlsx'` branch in the job.ts render step calling a new `renderCaseReportXlsx(context)` (exceljs is ALREADY a dep — package.json:24); (3) write the pure `xlsx.ts` renderer (same pure-builder shape as docx.ts, context-in/Buffer-out). The controller/service/SDK/FE need NO new wiring — `reportFormat` validates against the widened const, `generateReport(caseId,'xlsx')` works, the tray + presigned download are format-agnostic. The FE just un-disables the existing "Excel" button (already rendered `disabled title="Coming soon"`, CaseDetailPage.tsx) and points it at `generate.mutate('xlsx')`. **The parameterization is the right substrate for slice 5 — confirmed.** ✓

**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit, no MUST-FIX, no BLOCK.** The CTO's format-parameterization of the EXISTING CASE_REPORT JobType is architecturally SUPERIOR to the ADR's speced 3-JobType design — one processor / one tray label / one download path, format distinguished by extension+MIME, the branch at the single place it belongs (the render step); it avoids bloating `JOB_TYPES`/the type-forced title maps/`DOWNLOAD_TYPES`/`chk_jobs_type` 3×. Back-compat preserved (controller defaults pdf on absent query; SDK param defaults pdf; bare slice-2b POST + one-arg callers byte-identical). docx.ts is a clean pure builder (no SQL/scope/repo; small single-purpose helpers; section order mirrors the HTML sink) using a CORRECT docx@9.7.1 API (Packer.toBuffer→Promise<Buffer> verified, the Buffer.from re-wrap redundant-but-harmless; ImageRun.type required 'jpg'|'png' a valid subset). Image fetch is sequential-N inside a background job — acceptable (worker tier, 15s per-fetch timeout, graceful null→caption-only degrade) — NOT blocked. Boundaries confirmed (docx.ts imported only by job.ts; platform/jobs imports neither; processor injected at boot). MIME map type-forced; extension tracks format. TS-strict, zero suppressions, tsc×2 EXIT 0, docx.test 2/2 (valid zip + XSS-inert via OOXML entity-encoding). Image embed path is live-E2E-only (photos:[] in the unit test) — noted, acceptable. xlsx slice 5 extends cleanly (append const → MIME compile-error checklist → branch + pure renderer; exceljs already a dep; FE just un-disables Excel). file:lines — caseReports/docx.ts:{30-38 dash/fmtDate, 41-76 table prims, 80-93 fetchImage+15s timeout+null-degrade, 96-100 narrativeParagraphs, 102-148 taskBlock (122-146 photo loop), 151-250 renderCaseReportDocx, 247-249 Packer.toBuffer+redundant Buffer.from}, caseReports/job.ts:{2/8 docx imports, 13-18 payload+format, 21-24 MIME, 26-32 format branch, 42/47 .${format}}, caseReports/service.ts:{54-61 enqueueReport(+format)}, caseReports/controller.ts:{14-21 reportFormat parser, 54 wire}, sdk/caseReports.ts:{9-11 CASE_REPORT_FORMATS/CaseReportFormat}, sdk/client.ts:{657-660 generateReport(format='pdf')}, CaseDetailPage.tsx:{1688-1736 generate mutation + PDF/Word/Excel buttons}, docx.test.ts (2), caseReports.api.test.ts (+2), package.json:24 docx@^9.7.1. NOTEs: (a) amend ADR §9 — slices 4/5 are `format=` params on CASE_REPORT, not new JobTypes (companion to the slice-2b §6 async-shape drift); (b) defensive `payload.format ?? 'pdf'` at the processor IF a durable queue ever holds a pre-deploy payload across an upgrade (not needed for current fast-drain in-process posture); image-fetch parallelization optional if photo-heavy cases get slow. No BLOCK. OPEN: slice 5 (xlsx renderer — the parameterization substrate is ready).

## 2026-06-17 — CASE_REPORT S5 Slice 5 (FINAL): xlsx renderer + `format='xlsx'` arm (ADR-0041 §9 slice 5) — VERDICT: PASS (no MUST-FIX; 1 NOTE)
Audited the staged slice against ADR-0041 §3.3/§9-slice-5 + my Slice-4 entry (which predicted this exact shape). Ran tsc EXIT 0 (API); xlsx.test 3/3 green (valid zip >1KB + csvSafe unit + malicious-name-still-valid). Diff is EXACTLY what Slice 4 forecast: NEW `xlsx.ts`; +1 import + 1 MIME entry + 1 ternary arm in `job.ts`; `CASE_REPORT_FORMATS += 'xlsx'` (sdk); FE Excel button un-disabled→`generate.mutate('xlsx')` + mutation type widened to `CaseReportFormat`; +2 tests. 282 LOC total, 6 files.
- **(a) Parameterization scaled as predicted — CLEAN.** The 5-step checklist from my Slice-4 §(j) landed verbatim: append `'xlsx'` to the const → that ALONE forced the `MIME: Record<CaseReportFormat,string>` exhaustiveness compile-error until the spreadsheetml entry was added (the type system drove the checklist, exactly as designed); one more ternary arm (`format==='xlsx' ? renderCaseReportXlsx : pdf-branch`, job.ts:43-51); a new pure renderer. controller/service/SDK-client/registerJobs needed ZERO new wiring — `reportFormat()` validates against the widened const, `generateReport(caseId,'xlsx')` works, tray + presigned download are format-agnostic. The slice-4 parameterization substrate held with no surprises. ✓
- **(b) xlsx.ts quality — pure builder, no SQL/scope/repo.** `CaseReportContext → Promise<Buffer>`; imports only `exceljs` (LAZY: `(await import('exceljs')).default`, xlsx.ts:35 — matches the platform/export/format.ts lazy-import pattern, keeps exceljs out of the hot path / cold-start) + `@crm2/logger` + the sdk context type. Helpers `dash`/`fmtDate` are small null→'' formatters. 3 worksheets (Case Summary / Per-Task Outcomes / Photo Manifest) assembled top-down, section order mirrors the HTML+docx sinks (drift-resistant by reading the SAME context). NO image fetch — photos LISTED with their presigned URL as text (xlsx.ts:113-128), so zero network in this renderer → lighter + faster than docx/pdf (correct: a spreadsheet is a data export, not a rendered doc). ✓
- **(c) Numeric cells are RAW numbers, NOT csvSafe-wrapped — CORRECT.** Verified each: `t.photos.length` (xlsx.ts:94), `p.latitude/longitude/accuracy ?? ''` (118-120) are written as numbers (or '' when null), NOT through `csvSafe` → they land as native spreadsheet numbers (right-aligned, sortable, filterable, chartable). Wrapping them in `csvSafe` would stringify (`csvSafe` returns `string`) and defeat sort/filter — correctly avoided. The Case-Summary totals (totalTasks/photoCount etc.) ARE `String(...)`-wrapped (57-63), but those live in the kv "Value" text column of a transposed one-row summary sheet (Field|Value) where a text column is the right shape — acceptable, not a defect (they're not the sortable data grid; the Per-Task + Photo sheets are). ✓
- **(d) Formula-injection guard — SOUND + the right defense.** `csvSafe` prefixes a `'` to any value whose first char is `=/+/-/@/\t/\r` (xlsx.ts:29-32) so Excel/Sheets never evaluates a case field as a formula. Every FREE-TEXT cell flows through it (caseNumber/names/address/remark/photoType/address/URL). exceljs's value API XML-encodes content (no markup sink), so the formula guard is the spreadsheet-specific layer — correctly scoped. **The ADR (§3.3) spec'd photo URLs as Excel HYPERLINK formulas; the impl deliberately emits them as plain csvSafe-guarded TEXT** (xlsx.ts:123-125 comment) — a HYPERLINK() formula would re-open the injection surface. This is a security-superior deviation, well-documented. `csvSafe` is `export`ed for the unit test (matches the docx/render test convention). ✓
- **(e) Boundaries + TS-strict.** `renderCaseReportXlsx` imported ONLY by job.ts (grep: job.ts + xlsx.ts-self + test). platform/jobs imports neither. Import direction feature→platform/pkg, never reversed. Grep over xlsx.ts + job.ts diff: ZERO `: any`/`as any`/`@ts-ignore`/`@ts-expect-error`/`eslint-disable`. `Buffer.from(await wb.xlsx.writeBuffer())` normalizes the exceljs `ArrayBuffer`-ish return to a Node Buffer (needed for the storage `put` — correct, not redundant here unlike docx's Promise<Buffer>). tsc EXIT 0. ✓
- **(f) Tests — adequate.** xlsx.test (3): valid `.xlsx` → `Buffer.isBuffer` + `>1000 bytes` + PK\x03\x04 zip-magic; `csvSafe` unit pins all 5 dangerous prefixes + plain passthrough + null→'' + number→string; malicious applicant/customer name (`=cmd|calc`/`+1234`) → still a valid zip (guard doesn't break render). api.test (+1): `?format=xlsx` → 202 → awaitAllJobs → SUCCEEDED + storageKey `/\.xlsx$/` + filename `/^report-CASE-.+\.xlsx$/` + `result.format==='xlsx'`. The no-image-fetch design means the unit test exercises the FULL render path (no E2E-only branch like docx's photo embed). ✓
**Bottom line: PASS — cleared to commit, no MUST-FIX, no BLOCK.** The xlsx arm slotted into the slice-4 format-param model exactly as forecast — one MIME entry (type-forced by `Record<CaseReportFormat>`), one ternary arm, one lazy-imported pure renderer; zero controller/service/SDK/route wiring. xlsx.ts is a clean context→Buffer builder (no SQL/scope/repo, exceljs lazy per platform pattern), 3 data sheets mirroring the HTML/docx section order, NO image fetch (lists presigned URLs as text → no network, lighter than docx/pdf). Numeric cells (lat/lng/accuracy/photoCount) written RAW (sortable/filterable), correctly NOT csvSafe-stringified; free-text all csvSafe formula-guarded; URLs intentionally plain text not HYPERLINK formula (security > ADR's hyperlink spec). TS-strict, zero suppressions, tsc EXIT 0, xlsx.test 3/3 + api +1. file:lines — caseReports/xlsx.ts:{17-25 dash/fmtDate, 29-32 csvSafe, 34-35 lazy exceljs, 40-69 Case Summary, 71-97 Per-Task (94 raw photos.length), 99-129 Photo Manifest (118-120 raw lat/lng/accuracy, 123-125 URL-as-text), 131 Buffer.from(writeBuffer)}, job.ts:{9 import, 33 MIME xlsx, 46-51 xlsx ternary arm}, sdk/caseReports.ts:12 CASE_REPORT_FORMATS+='xlsx', CaseDetailPage.tsx:{1692 mutation type→CaseReportFormat, 1732-1738 Excel button}, xlsx.test.ts (3), caseReports.api.test.ts (+1). **xlsx carry → RESOLVED. S5 (CASE_REPORT engine) COMPLETE — HTML preview + PDF + Word + Excel, ADR-0041's "one assembly engine, three sinks (+HTML preview)" fully realized.** NOTE: (a) the slice-4 defensive `payload.format ?? 'pdf'` at the processor still applies (now widened to 3 formats) IF a durable queue ever holds a pre-deploy payload — unchanged disposition, not needed for fast-drain in-process. OPEN (carried, NOT this slice): DPDP retention/TTL on the now-3-format stored artifacts (CEO-tracked); worker observability.
